    <text xml:lang="sa-Latn-t-sa-Deva">

        <body>

            <div n="4" type="sthāna">

                <head>cikitsāsthānaṃ</head>


                <div n="21" type="level2" subtype="adhyāya">
                    <head>ekaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ|</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.1"> athātaḥ śūkadoṣacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.3"> saṃlikhya sarṣapīṃ samyak kaṣāyair avacūrṇayet | kaṣāyeṣv
                        eva tailaṃ ca kurvīta vraṇaropaṇam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.4"> aṣṭhīlikāṃ jalaukobhir grāhayec ca punaḥ punaḥ | tathā
                        cānupaśāmyantīṃ kaphagranthivad uddharet|| </l>




                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.5"> svedayed grathitaṃ śaśvan nāḍīsvedena buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhoṣṇair upanāhaiś ca susnigdhair upanāhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.6"> kumbhīkāṃ pākamāpannāṃ bhindyāc chuddhāṃ tu ropayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailena triphalālodhratindukāmrātakena tu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.7"> grāhayitvā jalaukobhir alajīṃ secayet tataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyais teṣu siddhaṃ ca tailaṃ ropaṇam iṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.8"> balātailena koṣṇena mṛditaṃ pariṣecayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhadhuraiḥ sarpiṣā snigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇair upanāhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.9"> saṃmūḍhapiḍakāṃ kṣipraṃ jalaukobhir upācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhittvā paryāgatāṃ cāpi lepayet kṣaudrasarpiṣā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.10"> avamanthe gate pākaṃ bhinne tailaṃ vidhīyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhavāśvakarṇapattaṅgasallakītindukīkṛtam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.11"> kriyāṃ puṣkarikāyāṃ tu śītāṃ sarvāṃ prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         jalaukobhir hareccāsṛk sarpiṣā cāvasecayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.12"> sparśahānyāṃ hared raktaṃ pradihyānmadhurair api |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrekṣurasasarpirbhiḥ secayec ca suśītalaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.13"> piḍakām uttamākhyāṃ ca baḍiśenoddhared bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         uddhṛtya madhusaṃyuktaiḥ kaṣāyair avacūrṇayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.14"> rasakriyā vidhātavyā likhite śataponake |
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthak parṇyādisiddhaṃ ca deyaṃ tailam anantaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.15"> kriyāṃ kuryād bhiṣak prājñas tvakpākasya visarpavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktavidradhivac cāpi kriyā śoṇitaje 'rbude || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.16"> kaṣāyakalkasarpīṃṣi tailaṃ cūrṇaṃ rasakriyām |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanaṃ ropaṇaṃ caiva vīkṣya vīkṣyāvacārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.17"> hitaṃ ca sarpiṣaḥ pānaṃ pathyaṃ cāpi cirecanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitaḥ śoṇitamokṣaś ca yac cāpi laghu bhojanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.18"> arbudaṃ māṃsapākaṃ ca vidradhiṃ tilakālakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyākhyāya prakurvīta bhiṣak samyak pratikriyām ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne śūkarogacikitsitaṃ
                        nāmaikaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||21 ||</l>
                </div>


                <div n="22" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.1"> athāto mukharogacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.2"> yathovaca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.3"> caturvidhena snehena madhūcchiṣṭayutena ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātaje 'bhyañjanaṃ dantavaidarbhe dantamūlāni śodhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ ksāraṃ prayuñjīta kriyāḥ sarvāś ca śītalāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.4"> vidadhyādoṣṭhakope tu sālvaṇaṃ copanāhane| mastiṣke caiva
                        nasye ca tailaṃ vātaharaṃ hitam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.5"> śrīveṣṭakaṃ sarjarasaṃ suradāru saguggulu|
                        yaṣṭīmadhukacūrṇaṃ tu vidadhyāt pratisāraṇam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.6"> pittaraktābhighātotthaṃ jalaukobhir upācaret|
                        pittavidradhivac cāpi kriyāṃ kuryād aśeṣataḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.7"> śirovirecanaṃ dhūmaḥ svedaḥ kavala eva ca| hṛte rakte
                        prayoktavyamoṣṭhakope kaphātmake|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.8"> tryūṣaṇaṃ svarjikākṣāro yavakṣāro viḍaṃ tathā|
                        kṣaudrayuktaṃ vidhātavyametac ca pratisāraṇam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.9"> medoje svedite bhinne śodhite jvalano hitaḥ|
                        priyaṅgutriphalālodhraṃ sakṣaudraṃ pratisāraṇam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.10"> etadoṣṭhaprakopānāṃ sādhyānāṃ karma kīrtitam|
                        dantamūlagatānāṃ tu rogāṇāṃ karma vakṣyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.11"> śītāde hṛtarakte tu toye nāgarasarṣapān| niṣkvāthya
                        triphalāṃ mustaṃ gaṇḍūṣaḥ sarasāñjanaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.12"> priyaṅgavaś ca mustaṃ ca triphalā ca pralepanam| nasyaṃ
                        ca triphalāsiddhaṃ madhukotpalapadmakaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.13"> dantapuppuṭake kāryaṃ taruṇe raktamokṣaṇam|
                        sapañcalavaṇaḥ kṣāraḥ sakṣaudraḥ pratisāraṇam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.14"> hitaḥ śirovirekaś ca nasyaṃ snigdhaṃ ca bhojanam|
                        visrāvite dantaveṣṭe vraṇāṃs tu pratisārayet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.15"> rodhrapattaṅgayaṣṭyāhvalākṣācūrṇairmadhūttaraiḥ| gaṇḍūṣe
                        kṣīriṇo yojyāḥ sakṣaudraghṛtaśarkarāḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.16"> kākolyādau daśakṣīrasiddhaṃ sarpiś ca nasyataḥ| śauṣire
                        hṛtarakte tu rodhramustarasāñjanaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.17"> sakṣaudraiḥ śasyate lepo gaṇḍūṣe kṣīriṇo hitāḥ|
                        sārivotpalayaṣṭyāhvasāvarāgurucandanaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.18"> kṣīre daśaguṇe siddhaṃ sarpirnasye ca pūjitam| kriyāṃ
                        paridare kuyācchītākoktāṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.19"> saṃśodhyobhayataḥ kāryaṃ śiraścopakuśe tathā|
                        kākodumbarikāgojīpatrairvisrāvayed asṛk|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.20"> kṣaudrayuktaiś ca lavaṇaiḥ savyoṣaiḥ pratisārayet|
                        pippalīḥ sarṣapāñ śvetānnāgaraṃ naiculaṃ phalam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.21"> sukhodakena saṃsṛjya kavalaṃ cāpi dhārayet| ghṛtaṃ
                        madhurakaiḥ siddhaṃ hitaṃ kavalanasyayoḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.22"> śastreṇa dantavaidarbhe dantamūlāni śodhayet| tataḥ
                        ksāraṃ prayuñjīta kriyāḥ sarvāś ca śītalāḥ|| </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.23"> uddhṛtyādhikadantaṃ tu tato 'gnimavacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛmidantakavac cāpi vidhiḥ kāryo vijānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.24"> chittvā 'dhimāṃsaṃ sakṣaudrair ebhiś cūrṇair upācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         vacātejovatīpāṭhāsvarjikāyāvaśūkajaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.25"> kṣaudradvitīyāḥ pippalyaḥ kavalaś cātra kīrtitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paṭolatriphalānimbakaṣāyaś cātra dhāvane |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitaḥ śirovirekaś ca dhūmo vair ecanaś ca yaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26ab"> sāmānyaṃ karma nāḍīnāṃ viśeṣaṃ cātra me śṛṇu |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26cd"> nāḍīvraṇaharaṃ karma dantanāḍīṣu kārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.27"> yaṃ dantam abhijāyeta nāḍī taṃ dantamuddharet |
                        <caesura/>
                         chittvā māṃsāni śastreṇa yadi noparijo bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.28"> śodhayitvā dahec cāpi kṣāreṇa jvalanena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhinattyupekṣite dante hanukāsthi gatirdhruvam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.29"> samūlaṃ daśanaṃ tasmād uddharedbhagnamasthiram |
                        <caesura/>
                         uddhṛte tūttare dante ca sthānaṃ vidahet suṣirasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato vidārīyaṣṭyāhvaśṛṅgāṭakakaserukaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.30ab"> raktātiyogāt pūrvektā rogā ghorā bhavanti hi| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.30cd">kāṇaḥ saṃjāyate janturarditaṃ cāsya jāyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.31ab"> calam apy uttaraṃ dantam ato nāpahared bhiṣak|</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.31cd"> dhāvane jātimadanasvādukaṇṭakakhādiram|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.32"> kaṣāyaṃ jātimadanakaṭukasvādukaṇṭakaiḥ|
                        yaṣṭyāhvarodhramañjiṣṭhākhadiraiś cāpi yat kṛtam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.33"> tailaṃ saṃśodhanaṃ taddhi hanyād dantagatāṃ gatim|
                        kīrtitā dantamūle tu kriyā danteṣu vakṣyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.34"> snehānāṃ kavalāḥ koṣṇāḥ sarpiṣastraivṛtasya vā| niryūhāś
                        cānilaghnānāṃ dantaharṣapramardanāḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.35"> snaihikaś ca hito dhūmo nasyaṃ snigdhaṃ ca bhojanam|
                        raso rasayavāgvaś ca kṣīraṃ santānikā ghṛtam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.36ab"> śirobastir hitaś cāpi kramo yaś cānilāpahaḥ|</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.36cd"> ahiṃsan dantamūlāni śarkarām uddhared bhiṣak|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.37"> lākṣācūrṇairmadhuyutais tatastāḥ pratisārayet|
                        dantaharṣakriyāṃ cāpi kuryān niravaśeṣataḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.38"> kapālikā kṛcchratamā tatrāpy eṣā kriyā hitā| jayed
                        visrāvaṇaiḥ svinnam acalaṃ kṛmidantakam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.39"> tathā+avapīḍair vātaghnaiḥ snehagaṇḍūṣadhāraṇaiḥ|
                        bhadradārvādivarṣābhūlepaiḥ snigdhaiś ca bhojanaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.40"> calamuddhṛtya ca sthānaṃ vidahet suṣirasya ca| tato
                        vidārīyaṣṭyāhvaśṛṅgāṭakakaserukaiḥ|| </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.41"> tailaṃ daśaguṇe kṣīre siddhaṃ nasye hitaṃ bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanomokṣe samuddiṣṭāṃ kuryāc cārditavat kriyām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.42"> phalānyamlāni śītāmbu rūkṣānnaṃ dantadhāvanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā 'tikaṭhinān bhakṣyān dantarogī vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.43"> sādhyānāṃ dantarogāṇāṃ cikitsitamudīritam |
                        <caesura/>
                         jihvāgatānāṃ sādhyānāṃ karma vakṣyāmi siddhaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.44"> auṣṭhaprakope 'nilaje yaduktaṃ prāk cikitsitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṇṭakeṣv anilottheṣu tat kāryaṃ bhiṣajā bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.45"> pittajeṣu vighṛṣṭeṣu niḥsṛte duṣṭaśoṇite |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratisāraṇagaṇḍūṣaṃ nasyaṃ ca madhuraṃ hitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.46"> kaṇṭakeṣu kaphottheṣu likhiteṣv asṛjaḥ kṣaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalyādirmadhuyutaḥ kāryas tu pratisāraṇe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.47"> gṛhṇīyāt kavalāṃś cāpi gaurasarṣapasaindhavaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paṭolanimbavārtākukṣārayūṣaiś ca bhojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.48"> upajihvāṃ tu saṃlikhya kṣāreṇa pratisārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirekagaṇḍūṣadhūmaiś cainamupācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.49"> jihvāgatānāṃ karmoktaṃ tālavyānāṃ pravakṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         aṅguṣṭhāṅgulisaṃdaṃśenākṛṣya galaśuṇḍikām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.50ab"> chedayen maṇḍalāgreṇa jihvopari tu saṃsthitām |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.50cd"> notkṛṣṭaṃ caiva hīnaṃ ca tribhāgaṃ chedayed bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.51"> atyādānāt sravedraktaṃ tannimittaṃ mriyeta ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnacchedādbhavec chopho lālā nidrā bhramastamaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.52"> tasmād vaidyaḥ prayatnena dṛṣṭakarmā viśāradaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         galaśuṇḍīṃ tu sañchidya kuryāt prāptamimaṃ kramam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.53"> maricātiviṣāpāṭhāvacākuṣṭhakuṭannaṭaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudrayuktaiḥ salavaṇais tatastāṃ pratisārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.54"> vacāmativiṣāṃ pāṭhāṃ rāsnāṃ kaṭukarohiṇīm |
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣkvāthya picumandaṃ ca kavalaṃ tatra yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.55"> iṅgudīkiṇihīdantīsaralāsuradārubhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcāṅgīṃ kārayet piṣṭair vartiṃ gandhottarāṃ śubhām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.56"> tato dhūmaṃ pibejjanturdvirahnaḥ kaphanāśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣārasiddheṣu mudgeṣu yūṣaś cāpy aśane hitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.57"> tuṇḍikeryadhruṣe kūrme saṅghāte tālupuppuṭe |
                        <caesura/>
                         eṣa eva vidhiḥ kāryo viśeṣaḥ śastrakarmaṇi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.58"> tālupāke tu kartavyaṃ vidhānaṃ pittanāśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehasvedau tāluśoṣe vidhiś cānilanāśanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.59"> kīrtitaṃ tālujānāṃ tu kaṇṭhyānāṃ karma vakṣyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyānāṃ rohiṇīnāṃ tu hitaṃ śoṇitamokṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.60"> chardanaṃ dhūmapānaṃ ca gaṇḍūṣo nasyakarma ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātikīṃ tu hṛte rakte lavaṇaiḥ pratisārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.61"> sukhoṣṇān snehagaṇḍūṣān dhārayec cāpy abhīkṣṇaśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pataṅgaśarkarākṣaudraiḥ paittikīṃ pratisārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.62"> drākṣāparūṣakakvātho hitaś ca kavalagrahe |
                        <caesura/>
                         agāradhūmakaṭukaiḥ ślaiṣmikīṃ pratisārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.63"> śvetāviḍaṅgadantīṣu tailaṃ siddhaṃ sasaindhavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         nasyakarmaṇi yoktavyaṃ tathā kavaladhāraṇe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.64"> pittavat sādhayed vaidyo rohiṇīṃ raktasaṃbhavām |
                        <caesura/>
                         visrāvya kaṇṭhaśālūkaṃ sādhayet tuṇḍikerivat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.65"> ekakālaṃ yavānnaṃ ca bhuñjīta snigdhamalpaśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         upajihvikavac cāpi sādhayed adhijihvikām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.66"> ekavṛndaṃ tu visrāvya vidhiṃ śodhanamācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         gilāyuś cāpi yo vyādhistaṃ ca śastreṇa sādhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.67"> amarmasthaṃ supakvaṃ ca bhedayed galavidradhim |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātāt sarvasaraṃ cūrṇair lavaṇaiḥ pratisārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.68"> tailaṃ vātaharaiḥ siddhaṃ hitaṃ kavalanasyayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato 'smai snaihikaṃ dhūmamimaṃ dadyādvicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.69"> śālarājādanair aṇḍasāraiṅgudamadhūkajāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         majjāno gugguludhyāmamāṃsīkālānusārivāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śrīsarjarasaśaileyamadhūcchiṣṭāni cāharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.70"> tat sarvaṃ sukṛtaṃ cūrṇaṃ snehenāloḍya yuktitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṭiṇḍūkavṛntaṃ sakṣaudraṃ matimāṃstena lepayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.71"> eṣa sarvasare dhūmaḥ praśastaḥ snaihiko mataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphaghno mārutaghnaś ca mukharogavināśanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.72"> pittātmake sarvasare śuddhakāyasya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvaḥ pittaharaḥ kāryo vidhirmadhuraśītalaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.73"> pratisāraṇagaṇḍūṣau dhūmaḥ saṃśodhanāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphātmake sarvasare vidhiṃ kuryāt kaphāpaham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.74"> pibedativiṣāṃ pāṭhāṃ mustaṃ ca suradāru ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         rohiṇīṃ kaṭukākhyāṃ ca kuṭajasya phalāni ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.75"> gavāṃ mūtreṇa manujo bhāgair dharaṇasaṃmitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         eṣa sarvān kaphakṛtān rogān yogo 'pakarṣati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.76"> kṣīrekṣurasagomūtradadhimastvamlakāñjikaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidadhyāt kavalān vīkṣya doṣaṃ tailaghṛtair api || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.77"> rogāṇāṃ mukhajātānāṃ sādhyānāṃ karma kīrtitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         asādhyā api vakṣyante rogā ye tatra kīrtitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.78"> auṣṭhaprakope varjyāḥ syur māṃsaraktatridoṣajāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dantamūleṣu varjyau tu triliṅgagatisauṣirau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.79"> danteṣu ca na sidhyanti śyāvadālanabhañjanāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jihvāgateṣv alāsas tu tālavyeṣv arbudaṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.80"> svaraghno valayo vṛndo vidāryalasa eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         galauṣṭho māṃsatānaś ca śataghnī rohiṇī ca yā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.81"> asādhyāḥ kīrtitā hyete rogā nava daśaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣāṃ cāpi kriyāṃ vaidyaḥ pratyākhyāya samācaret ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne mukharogacikitsitaṃ nāma
                        dvāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||22 ||</l>
                </div>


                <div n="23" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>trayoviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.1"> athātaḥ śophānāṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.3"> ṣaḍvidho 'vayavasamutthaḥ śopho 'bhihito lakṣaṇataḥ
                        pratīkārataś ca; sarvasaras tu pañcavidhaḥ, tad yathā
                        vātapittaśleṣmasannipātaviṣanimittaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.4"> tatrāpatarpitasyādhvagamanādatimātramabhyavaharato vā
                        piṣṭānnaharitakaśākalavaṇāni kṣīṇasya vā 'timātramamlam upasevamānasya
                        mṛtpakvaloṣṭakaṭaśarkarānūpaudakamāṃsasevanādajīrṇino vā
                        grāmyadharmasevanādviruddhāhārasevanāt vā
                        hastyaśvoṣṭrarathapadātisaṅkṣobhaṇādayo sitasya doṣā dhātūn pradūṣya
                        śvayathum āpādayanty akhile śarīre || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.5"> tatra vātaśvayathuraruṇaḥ kṛṣṇo vā
                        mṛduranavasthitāstodādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ; pittaśvayathuḥ pītaḥ sarakto
                        vā mṛduḥ śīghrānusāryūṣādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ; śleṣmaśvayathuḥ pāṇḍuḥ
                        śuklo vā snigdhaḥ kaṭhinaḥ śīto mandānusārī, kaṇḍvādayaś cātra
                        vedanāviśeṣāḥ; sannipātaśvayathuḥ sarvavarṇavedanaḥ; viṣanimittastu
                        garopayogādduṣṭatoyasevanāt prakuthitodakāvagāhanāt
                        saviṣasattvadigdhacūrṇāvacūrṇanādvā saviṣamūtrapurīṣaśukraspṛṣṭānāṃ vā
                        tṛṇakāṣṭhādīnāṃ saṃsparśanāt, sa tu mṛduḥ ksiprotthāno 'valambī calo 'calo
                        vā dāhapākarāgaprāyaś ca bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.6"> bhavanti cātra doṣāḥ śvayathumūrdhvaṃ hi
                        kurvantyāmāśayasthitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                        <caesura/>
                         pakvāśayasthā madhye ca varcaḥsthānagatāstvadhaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.7"> kṛtsnaṃ dehamanuprāptāḥ kuryuḥ sarvasaraṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                        <caesura/>
                         śvayathur madhyadeśe yaḥ sa kaṣṭaḥ sarvagaś ca yaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.8"> ardhāṅge 'riṣṭabhūtaś ca yaś cordhvaṃ parisarpati |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsaḥ pipāsā daurbalyaṃ jvaraś cchardirarocakaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.9"> hikkātīsārakāsāś ca śūnaṃ saṅkṣapayanti hi |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāmānyato viśeṣāc ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi bheṣajam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.10"> śophinaḥ sarva eva
                        parihareyuramlalavaṇadadhiguḍavasāpayastailaghṛtapiṣṭamayagurūṇi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.11"> tatra vātaśvayathau traivṛtameraṇḍatailaṃ vā
                        māsamardhamāsaṃ vā pāyayet, nyagrodhādikakaṣāyasiddhaṃ sarpiḥ
                        pittaśvayathau, āragvadhādisiddhaṃ sarpiḥ śleṣmaśvayathau,
                        sannipātaśvayathau snuhīkṣīrapātraṃ dvādaśabhir amlapātraiḥ pratisaṃsṛjya
                        dantīdravantīpratīvāpaṃ sarpiḥ pācayitvā pāyayet, viṣanimitteṣu kalpeṣu
                        pratīkāraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.12"> ata ūrdhvaṃ sāmānyacikitsitam upadekṣyāmaḥ
                        tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni yānyuktānyudareṣu tato 'nyataman upayujyamānaṃ
                        śvayathumapahanti, mūtravartikriyāṃ vā seveta, navāyasaṃ vā 'haraharmadhunā,
                        viḍaṅgātiviṣākuṭajaphalabhadradārunāgaramaricacūrṇaṃ vā dharaṇamuṣṇāmbunā,
                        trikaṭukṣārāyaś cūrṇāni vā triphalākaṣāyeṇa, mūtraṃ vā tulyakṣīraṃ,
                        harītakīṃ vā tulyaguḍām upayuñjīta, devadāruśuṇṭhīṃ vā, gugguluṃ vā mūtreṇa
                        varṣabhūkaṣāyānupānaṃ vā, tulyaguḍaṃ vā mūtreṇa varṣabhūkaṣāyānupānaṃ vā,
                        tulyaguḍaṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ vā, varṣābhūkaṣāyaṃ mūlakalkaṃ vā saśṛṅgaveraṃ payo
                        'nupānam aharahar māsaṃ, vyoṣavarṣābhūkaṣāyasiddhena vā sarpiṣā mudgolumbān
                        bhakṣayet, pippalīpippalīmūlacavyacitrakamayūrakavarṣābhūsiddhaṃ vā kṣīraṃ
                        pibet, sahauṣadhamuraṅgīmūlasiddhaṃ vā, trikaṭukair aṇḍaśyāmāmūlasiddhaṃ vā,
                        varṣābhūśṛṅgaverasahādevadārusiddhaṃ vā, tathā 'lābubibhītakaphalakalkaṃ vā
                        taṇḍulāmbunā; kṣīrapippalīmaricaśṛṅgaverānusiddhena ca
                        mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇenālpasnehena bhojayed yavānnaṃ godhūmānnaṃ vā;
                        vṛkṣakārkanaktamālanimbavarṣābhūkvāthaiś ca pariṣekaḥ;
                        sarṣapasuvarcalāsaindhavaśārṅgeṣṭābhiś ca pradehaḥ kāryaḥ; yathādoṣaṃ ca
                        vamanavirecanāsthāpanāni tīkṣṇānyajasram upaseveta, snehasvedopanāhāṃś ca;
                        sirābhiś cābhīkṣṇaṃ śoṇitam avasecayed anyatropadravaśophād iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.13"> bhavati cātra piṣṭānnam amlaṃ lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ
                        divāsvapnam ajāṅgalaṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         striyo ghṛtaṃ tailapayogurūṇi śophaṃ jighāṃsuḥ parivarjayet tu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne sothacikitsitaṃ nāma
                        trayoviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||23 ||</l>
                </div>




                <div n="24" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>caturviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.1"> athāto 'nāgatābādhāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.3"> utthāyotthāya satataṃ svasthenārogyam icchatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhīmatā yad anuṣṭheyaṃ tat sarvaṃ saṃpravakṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.4"> tatrādau dantapavanaṃ dvādaśāṅgulamāyatam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaniṣṭhikāparīṇāham ṛjvagranthitam avraṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.5"> ayugmagranthi yac cāpi pratyagraṃ śastabhūmijam |
                        <caesura/>
                         avekṣyartuṃ ca doṣaṃ ca rasaṃ vīryaṃ ca yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.6"> kaṣāyaṃ madhuraṃ tiktaṃ kaṭukaṃ prātar utthitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nimbaś ca tiktake śreṣṭhaḥ kaṣāye khadiras tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.7"> madhūko madhure śreṣṭhaḥ karañjaḥ kaṭuke tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudravyoṣatrivargāktaṃ satailaṃ saindhavena ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.8"> cūrṇena tejovatyāś ca dantān nityaṃ viśodhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekaikaṃ ghrṣayed dantaṃ mṛdunā kūrcakena ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.9"> dantaśodhanacūrṇena dantamāṃsāny abādhayan |
                        <caesura/>
                         tad daurgandhyopadehau tu śleṣmāṇaṃ cāpakarṣati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.10"> vaiśadyam annābhir uciṃ saumanasyaṃ karoti ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         na khāded galatālv oṣṭhajihvārogasamudbhave || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.11"> athāsyapāke śvāse ca kāsahikkāvamīṣu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         durbalo 'jīrṇabhaktaś ca mūrcchārto madapīṣitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.12"> śirorujārtastṛṣitaḥ śrāntaḥ pānaklamānvitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         arditī karṇaśūlī ca dantarogī ca mānavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.13"> jihvānirlekhanaṃ raupyaṃ sauvarṇaṃ vārkṣam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tan malāpaharaṃ śastaṃ mṛdu ślakṣṇaṃ daśāṅgulam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.14"> mukhavair asya daurgandhyaśophajāḍyaharaṃ sukham |
                        <caesura/>
                         dantadārḍhyakaraṃ rucyaṃ snehagaṇḍūṣadhāraṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.15"> kṣīravṛkṣakaṣāyair vā kṣīreṇa ca vimiśritaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhilloṭakakaṣāyeṇa tathaivāmalakasya vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.16"> prakṣālayen mukhaṃ nentre svasthaḥ śītodakena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         nīlikāṃ mukhaśoṣaṃ ca piḍakāṃ vyaṅgam eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.17"> raktapittakṛtān rogān sadya eva vināśayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhaṃ laghu nirīkṣeta dṛḍhaṃ paśyati cakṣuṣā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.18"> mataṃ srotoñjanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ viśuddhaṃ sindhusaṃbhavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhakaṇḍūmalaghnaṃ ca dṛṣṭikledarujāpaham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.19"> tejorūpāvahaṃ caiva sahate mārutātapau |
                        <caesura/>
                         na netrarogā jāyante tasmād añjanam ācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.20"> bhuktavāñ chirasā snātaḥ śrāntaś chardanavāhanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rātrau jāgaritaś cāpi nāñjyājjvarita eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.21"> karpūrajātīkakkolalavaṅgakaṭukāhvayaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sacūrṇapūgaiḥ sahitaṃ patraṃ tāmbulajaṃ śubham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.22"> mukhavaiśadyasaugandhyakāntisauṣṭhavakārakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanudantasvaramalajihvendriyaviśodhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.23"> prasekaśamanaṃ hṛdyaṃ galāmayavināśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pathyaṃ suptotthite bhukte snāte vānte ca mānave || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.24"> raktapittakṣatakṣīṇatṛṣṇāmūrcchāparītinām |
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣadurbalamartyānāṃ na hitaṃ cāsyaśoṣiṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.25"> śirogatāṃs tathā rogāñ chirobhaṅgo 'pakarṣati |
                        <caesura/>
                         keśānāṃ mārdavaṃ dairghyaṃ bahutvaṃ snigdhakṛṣṇatām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.26"> karoti śirasastṛptiṃ sutvakkam api cānanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         santarpaṇaṃ cendriyāṇāṃ śirasaḥ pratipūraṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.27"> madhukaṃ kṣīraśuklā ca saralaṃ devadāru ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣudrakaṃ pañcanāmānaṃ samabhāgāni saṃharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.28"> teṣāṃ kalkakaṣāyābhyāṃ cakrateilaṃ vipācayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadaiva śītalaṃ jantor mūrdhni tailaṃ pradāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.29"> keśaprasādhanī keśyā rajojantumalāpahā |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanumanyāśiraḥkarṇaśūlaghnaṃ karṇapūraṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.30"> abhyaṅgo mārdavakaraḥ kaphavātanirodhanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhātūnāṃ puṣṭijanano mṛjāvarṇabalapradaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.31"> sekaḥ śramaghno 'nilahṛdbhagnasandhiprasādhakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣatāgnidagdhābhihatavighṛṣṭānāṃ rujāpahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.32"> jalasiktasya vardhante yathā mūle 'ṅkurāstaroḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā dhātuvivṛddhirhi snehasiktasya jāyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.33"> sirāmukhai romakūpair dhamanībhiś ca tarpayam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīrabalam ādhatte yuktaḥ sneho 'vagāhane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.34"> tatra prakṛtisātmyartudeśadoṣavikāravit |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā matimān yuñjyād abhyaṅgasekayoḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.35"> kevalaṃ sāmadoṣeṣu na kathañ cana yojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         taruṇajvaryajīrṇī ca nābhyaktavyau kathañ cana || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.36"> tathā virikto vāntaś ca nirūḍho yaś ca mānavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvayoḥ kṛcchratā vyādher asādhyatvam athāpi vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.37"> śeṣāṇāṃ tadahaḥ proktā agnimāndyādayo gadāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         santarpaṇasamutthānāṃ rogāṇāṃ naiva kārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.38"> śarīrāyāsajananaṃ karma vyāyāmasaṃjñitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tat kṛtvā tu sukhaṃ dehaṃ vimṛdgīyāt samantataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.39"> śarīropacayaḥ kāntir gātrāṇāṃ suvibhaktatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dīptāgnitvam anālasyaṃ sthiratvaṃ lāghavaṃ mṛjā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.40"> śramaklamapipāsoṣṇaśītādīnāṃ sahiṣṇutā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ārogyaṃ cāpi paramaṃ vyāyāmād upajāyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.41"> na cāsti sadṛśaṃ tena kiñcit sthaulyāpakarṣaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         na ca vyāyāminaṃ martyamardayanty arayo balāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.42"> na cainaṃ sahasā ''ākramya jarā samadhi rohati |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthirībhavati māṃsaṃ ca vyāyāmābhir atasya ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.43"> vyāyāmasvinnagātrasya padbhyām udvartitasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhayo nopasarpanti siṃhaṃ kṣudramṛgā eva || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.44"> vayor ūpaguṇair hīnam api kuryāt sudarśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāyāmaṃ kurvato nityaṃ viruddham api bhojanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.45"> vidagdham avidagdhaṃ vā nirdoṣaṃ paripacyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāyāmo hi sadā pathyo balināṃ snigdhabhojinām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.46"> sa ca śīte vasante ca teṣāṃ pathyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarveṣv ṛtuṣv aharahaḥ pumbhir ātmahitaiṣibhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.47"> balasyārdhena kartavyo vyāyāmo hantyato 'nyathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdi sthānasthito vāyur yadā vaktraṃ prapadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.48"> vyāyāmaṃ kurvato jantos tad balārdhasya lakṣaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vayobalaśarīrāṇi deśakālāśanāni ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.49"> samīkṣya kuryād vyāyāmam anyathā rogam āpnuyāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣayatṛṣṇārucicchardiraktapittabhramaklamāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.50"> kāsaśoṣajvaraśvāsā ativyāyāmasaṃbhavāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktapittī kṛśaḥ śoṣī śvāsakāsakṣatāturaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.51"> bhuktavān strīṣu ca kṣīṇastṛḍbhramārtaś ca varjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         udvartanaṃ vātaharaṃ kaphamedovilāpanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.52"> sthirīkaraṇam aṅgānāṃ tvakprasthādakaraṃ param |
                        <caesura/>
                         sirāmukhaviviktatvaṃ tvaksthasyāgneś ca tejanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.53"> udgharṣaṇotsādanābhyāṃ jāyeyāt āmasaṃśayam |
                        <caesura/>
                         utsādanād bhavet strīṇāṃ viśeṣāt kāntimad vapuḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.54"> praharṣasaubhāgyamṛjālāghavādiguṇānvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         udgharṣaṇaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ kaṇḍūkoṣṭhānilāpaham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.55"> ūrvoḥ saṃjanayaty āśu phenakaḥ sthair yalāghave |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṇḍūkoṭhānilastambhamalarogāpahaś ca saḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.56"> tejanaṃ tvaggatasyāgneḥ sirāmukhavivecanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         udgharṣaṇaṃ tviṣṭikayā kaṇḍūkoṭhavināśanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.57"> nidrādāhaśramaharaṃ svedakaṇḍūtṛṣāpaham |
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdyaṃ malaharaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvendriyavibodhanam samācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.58"> tandrāpāpmopaśamanaṃ tuṣṭidaṃ puṃstvavardhanam|
                        raktaprasādanaṃ cāpi snānam agneś ca dīpanam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.59"> uṣṇena śirasaḥ snānam ahitaṃ cakṣuṣaḥ sadā| śītena
                        śirasaḥ snānaṃ cakṣuṣyam iti nirdiśet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.60"> śleṣmamārutakope tu jñātvā vyādhibalābalam| kāmamuṣṇaṃ
                        śiraḥsnānaṃ bhaiṣajyārthaṃ samācaret|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.61"> atiśītāmbu śīte ca śleṣmamārutakopanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         atyuṣṇam uṣṇakāle ca pittaśoṇitakopanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.62"> tac cātisārajvaritakarṇaśūlānilārtiṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         ādhmānārocakājīrṇabhuktavatsu ca garhitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.63"> saubhāgyadaṃ varṇakaraṃ prītyojobalavardhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedadaurgandhyavaivarṇyaśramaghnam anulepanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.64"> snānaṃ yeṣāṃ niṣiddhaṃ tu teṣām apy anulepanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣoghnam atha caujasyaṃ saubhāgyakaram uttamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.65"> sumanombararatnānāṃ dhāraṇaṃ prītivardhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mukhālepāddṛḍhaṃ cakṣuḥ pīnagaṇḍaṃ tathā ''ānanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.66"> avyaṅgapiḍakaṃ kāntaṃ bhavaty ambujasannibham |
                        <caesura/>
                         paksmalaṃ viśadaṃ kāntam amalojjvalamaṇḍalam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.67"> netram añjanasaṃyogād bhavec cāmalatārakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaśasyaṃ svargyam āyuṣyaṃ dhanadhānyavivardhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.68"> devatātithiviprāṇāṃ pūjanaṃ gotravardhanam |

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.69"> āyustejaḥsamutsāhasmṛtyojognivivardhanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.70"> cakṣuḥprasādanaṃ vṛṣyaṃ rakṣoghnaṃ prītivardhanam |
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.72"> sukhapracāram ojasyaṃ sadā pādatradhāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         anārogyam anāyuṣyaṃ cakṣuṣor upaghātakṛt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.73"> pādābhyām anupānadbhyāṃ sadā caṅkramaṇaṃ nṛṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāpmopaśamanaṃ keśanakharomāpamārjanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.74"> harṣalāghavasaubhāgyakaram utsāhavardhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         bāṇavāraṃ mṛjāvarṇatejobalavivardhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.75"> pavitraṃ keśyam uṣṇīṣaṃ vātātaparajopaham |
                        <caesura/>
                         varṣānilarajogharmahimādīnāṃ nivāraṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.76"> varṇyaṃ cakṣuṣyam aujasyaṃ śaṅkaraṃ chatradhāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śunaḥ sarīsṛpavyālaviṣāṇibhyo bhayāpaham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.77"> śramaskhalanadoṣaghnaṃ sthavire ca praśasyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         sattvotsāhabalasthair ya dhairyavīryavivardhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.78"> avaṣṭambhakaraṃ cāpi bhayaghnaṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.79"> adhvā varṇakaphasthaulyasaukumāryavināśanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atyadhvā viparīto+āsmājjarādaurbalyakṛc ca saḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.80"> yat tu caṅkramaṇaṃ nātidehapīḍākaraṃ bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tad āyurbalamedhāgnipradamindriyabodhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.81"> śramānilaharaṃ vṛṣyaṃ puṣṭinidrādhṛtipradam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhaṃ śayyāsanaṃ duḥkhaṃ viparītaguṇaṃ matam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.82"> bālavyajanamaujasyaṃ makṣikādīn apohati |
                        <caesura/>
                         śoṣadāhaśramasvedamūrcchāghno vyajanānilaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.83"> prītinidrākaraṃ vṛṣyaṃ kaphavātaśramāpaham |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃvāhanaṃ māṃsaraktatvakprasādakaraṃ sukham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.84"> pravātaṃ raukṣyavaivarṇyastambhakṛddāhapaktinut |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedamūrcchāpipāsāghnamapravātamato 'nyathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.85"> sukhaṃ vātaṃ praseveta grīṣme śaradi mānavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivātaṃ hy āyuṣe sevyam ārogyāya ca sarvadā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.86"> ātapaḥ pittatṛṣṇāgnisvedamūrcchābhramāsrakṛt |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhavaivarṇyakārī ca chāyā caitānapohati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.87"> agnirvātakaphastambhaśītavepathunāśanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmābhiṣyandajaraśo raktapittapradūṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.88"> puṣṭivarṇabalotsāhamagnidīptimatandritām |
                        <caesura/>
                         karoti dhātusāmyaṃ ca nidrā kāle niṣevitā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.89"> tatrādita eva nīcanakharomṇā śucinā śuklavāsasā
                        laghūṣṇīṣacchatropānatkena daṇḍapāṇinā kāle hitamitamadhurapūrvābhibhāṣiṇā
                        bandhubhūtena bhūtānāṃ guruvṛddhānumatena susahāyenānanyamanasā
                        khalūpacaritavyaṃ, tad api na rātrau, na
                        keśāsthikaṇṭakāśmatuṣabhasmotkarakapālāṅgārāmedhyasnānabalibhūmiṣu, na
                        viṣamendrakīlacatuṣpathaśvabhrāṇām upariṣṭāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.90"> na rājadviṣṭaparuṣapaiśunyānṛtāni vadet, na
                        devabrāhmaṇapitṛparivādāṃś ca; na narendradviṣṭonmattapatitakṣudranīcān
                        upāsīta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.91">
                        vṛkṣaparvataprapātaviṣamavalmīkaduṣṭavājikuñjarādyadhirohaṇāni pariharet,
                        pūrṇanadīsamudrāviditapalvalaśvabhrakūpāvataraṇāni,
                        bhinnaśūnyāgāraśmaśānavijanāraṇyavāsāgnisaṃbhramavyālabhujaṅgakīṭasevāś ca,
                        grāmāghātakalahaśastrasannipātavyālasarīsṛpaśṛṅgisannikarṣāṃś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.92"> nāgnigogurubrāhmaṇapreṅkhādampatyantareṇa yāyāt | na
                        śavam anuyāyāt | devagobrāhmaṇacaity adhvajarogipatitapāpakāriṇāṃ ca chāyāṃ
                        nākrameta | nāstaṃ gacchantam udyantaṃ vā ''ādity aṃ vīkṣeta | gāṃ
                        dhāpayantīṃ dhayantīṃ paraśasyaṃ vā carantīṃ na kasmaicid ācakṣīta, na
                        colkāpātotpātendradhanūṃṣi | nāgniṃ mukhenopadhamet | nāpo bhūmiṃ vā
                        pāṇipādenābhihanyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.93"> na vegān dhārayed vātamūtrapurīṣādīnām | na bahirvegān
                        grāmanagaradevatāyatanaśmaśānacatuṣpathasalilāśayapathisannikṛṣṭāv utsṛjen
                        na prakāśaṃ na vāyvagnisalilasomārkagogurupratimukham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.94"> na bhūmiṃ vilikhet, nāsaṃvṛtamukhaḥ sadasi
                        jṛmbhodagārakāsaśvāsakṣavathūnutsṛjet, na paryaṅkikāvaṣṭambhapādaprasāraṇāni
                        gurusannidhau kuryāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.95"> na bālakarṇanāsāsrotodaśanākṣivivarāṇyabhikuṣṇīyāt, na
                        vījayet keśamukhanakhavastragātrāṇi, na gātranakhavaktravāditraṃ kuryāt , na
                        kāṣṭhaloṣṭatṛṇādīn abhihanyāc chindyād bhindyād vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.96"> na prativātātapaṃ seveta, na bhuktamātro 'gnimupāsīta,
                        notkaṭakālpakāṣṭhāsanamadhyāsīta, na grīvāṃ viṣamaṃ dhārayet, na viṣamakāyaḥ
                        kriyāṃ bhajeta bhuñjīta vā, na pratatam īkṣeta
                        viśeṣājjyotirbhāskarasūkṣmacalabhrāntāni, na bhāraṃ śirasā vahet, na
                        svapnajāgaraṇaśayanāsanasthānacaṅkramaṇayānavāhanapradhāvanalaṅghanaplavanaprataraṇahāsyabhāṣyavyavāyavyāyāmādīnucitān
                        apy atiseveta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.97"> ucitād apy ahitāt kramaśo viramet, hitam anucitam apy
                        aseveta kramaśaḥ, na caikāntataḥ pādahīnāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.98"> nāvākśirāḥ śayīta, na bhinnapātre bhuñjīta, na vinā
                        pātreṇa, nāñjalipuṭenāpaḥ pibet, kāle hitamitasnigdhamadhuraprāyamāhāraṃ
                        vaidyapratyavekṣitam aśnīyāt,
                        grāmagaṇagaṇikāpaṇikaśatrusatraśaṭhapatitabhojanāni parikaret, śeṣāṇy api
                        cāniṣṭarūparasagandhasparśaśabdamānasāni, anyāny evaṃ guṇāny api
                        saṃbhramadattāni, (tānyapi) makṣikābālopahatāni, nāprakṣālitapādo bhuñjīta
                        na mūtroccārapīḍito na sandhyayor nānupāśrito nātītakālaṃ hīnam atimātraṃ
                        (noddhṛtasnehaṃ) ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.99"> na bhuñjītoddhṛtasnehaṃ naṣṭaṃ paryuṣitaṃ payaḥ | na
                        naktaṃ dadhi bhuñjīta na cāpy aghṛtaśarkaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.100"> nāmudgayūṣaṃ nākṣaudraṃ noṣṇaṃ nāmalakair vinā |
                        anyathā janayet kuṣṭhavisarpādīn gadān bahūn | nātmānamudake paśyen na
                        nagnaḥ praviśejjalam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.101">
                        dyūtamadyātisevāpratibhutvasākṣitvasamāhvānagoṣṭhīvāditrāṇi na seveta,
                        srajaṃ chatropānakau kanakam atītavāsāṃsi na cānyair dhṛtāni dhārayet,
                        brāhmaṇam agniṃ gāṃ ca nocchiṣṭaḥ spṛśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.102"> bhavanti cātra yasmin yasminn ṛtau ye ye doṣāḥ kupyanti
                        dehinām |
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣu teṣu pradātavyā rasāste te vijānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.103"> varṣāsu na pibet toyaṃ pibec charadi mātrayā |
                        <caesura/>
                         varṣasu caturo māsān mātrāvad udakaṃ pibet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.104"> uṣṇaṃ haime vasante ca kāmaṃ śrīṣme tu śītalam |
                        <caesura/>
                         hemante ca vasante ca sīdhvariṣṭau piben naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.105"> śṛtaśītaṃ payo grīṣme prāvṛṭkāle rasaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         yūṣaṃ varṣati, tasyānte prapicchītalaṃ jalam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.106"> svastha evam ato 'nyas tu doṣāhāragatānugaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehaṃ saindhavacūrṇena pippalībhiś ca saṃyutam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.107"> pibed agnivivṛddhyarthaṃ na ca vegān vidhārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         agnidīptikaraṃ nṝṇāṃ rogāṇāṃ śamanaṃ prati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.108"> prāvṛṭśaradvasanteṣu samyak snehādimācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphe pracchardanaṃ pitte vireko bastirīrane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.109"> śasyate triṣv api sadā vyāyāmo doṣanāśanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhuktaṃ viruddham apy annaṃ vyāyāmānna praduṣyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.110"> utsargamaithunahāraśodhane syāt tu tanmanāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         necched doṣacayāt prājñaḥ pīḍāṃ vā kāyamānasīm || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.111"> atistrīsaṃprayogāc ca rakṣed ātmānam ātmavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         śūlakāsajvaraśvāsakārśyapāṇḍvāmayakṣayāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.112"> ativyavājāj jāyante rogāś cākṣepakādayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āyuṣmanto mandajarā vapur varṇabalānvitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.113"> sthiropacitamāṃsāś ca bhavanti strīṣu saṃyatāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tribhis tribhir ahobhir vā samīyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.114"> sarveṣvṛtuṣu, gharmeṣu pakṣāt pakṣād vrajed budhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rajasvalām akāmāṃ ca malinām apriyāṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.115"> varṇavṛddhāṃ vayovṛddhāṃ tathā vyādhiprapīḍitām |
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnāṅgīṃ garbhiṇīṃ dveṣyāṃ yonidoṣasamanvitām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.116"> sagotrāṃ gurupatnīṃ ca tathā pravrajitām api |
                        <caesura/>
                         sandhyāparvasvagamyāṃ ca nopeyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.117"> gosarge cārdharātre ca tathā madhyandineṣu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         lajjāsamāvahe deśe vivṛte 'śuddha eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.118"> kṣudhito vyādhitaś caiva kṣubdhacittaś ca mānavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātaviṇmūtravegī ca pipāsaratidurbalaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.119"> tiryagyonāv ayonau ca prāptaśukravidhāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         duṣṭayonau visargaṃ tu balavān api varjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.120"> retasaś cātimātraṃ tu mūrdhāvaraṇam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthitāvuttānaśayane viśeṣeṇaiva garhitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.121"> krīḍāyām api medhāvī hitārthī parivarjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         rajasvalāṃ prāptavato narasyāniyatātmanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.122"> dṛṣṭyāyustejasāṃ hānir adharmaś ca tato bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         liṅginīṃ gurupatnīṃ ca sagotrām atha parvasu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.123"> vṛddhāṃ ca sandhyayoś cāpi gacchato jīvitakṣayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         garbhiṇyā garbhapīḍā syād vyādhitāyāṃ balakṣayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.124"> hīnāṅgīṃ malināṃ dveṣyāṃ kāmaṃ vandhyāmasaṃvṛte |
                        <caesura/>
                         deśe 'śuddhe ca śukrasya manasaś ca kṣayo bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.125"> kṣudhitaḥ kṣubdhacittaś ca madhyāhne tṛṣito 'balaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthitaś ca hāniṃ śukrasya vāyoḥ kopaṃ ca vindati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.126"> atiprasaṅgād bhavati śoṣaḥ śukrakṣayāvahaḥ |
                        vyādhitasya rujā plīhni mṛtyur mūrcchā ca jāyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.127"> prayūṣasy ardharātre ca vātapitte prakupyataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tiryagyonāv ayanau ca duṣṭayonau tathaiva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.128"> upadaṃśas tathā vāyoḥ kopaḥ śukrasya ca kṣayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uccārite mūtrite ca retasaś ca vidhāraṇe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.129"> uttāne ca bhavec chīghraṃ śukrāśmaryās tu saṃbhavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvaṃ pariharet tasmād etal lokadvaye 'hitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.130"> śukraṃ copasthitaṃ mohānna sandhāryaṃ kathaṃcana |
                        <caesura/>
                         vayor ūpaguṇopetāṃ tulyaśīlāṃ kulānvitām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.131"> abhikāmo 'bhikāmāṃ tu hṛṣṭo hṛṣṭām alaṅkṛtām |
                        <caesura/>
                         seveta pramadāṃ yuktyā vājīkaraṇabṛṃhitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.132"> bhakṣyāḥ saśarkarāḥ kṣīraṃ sasitaṃ rasa eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         snānaṃ savyajanaṃ svapno vyavāyānte hitāni tu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.133"> mukhamātraṃ samāsena sadvṛttasyaitad īritam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ārogyam āyur artho vāg āsadbhiḥ prāpyate nṛbhiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne 'nāgatābādhacikitsitaṃ nāma
                        caturviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||24 ||</l>
                </div>

                <div n="25" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>pañcaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.1"> athāto miśrakacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.3"> pālyāmayās tu visrāvyā ity uktaṃ prāṅgibodha tān |
                        <caesura/>
                         paripoṭas tathotpāta unmantho duḥkhavardhanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.4"> pañcamaḥ parilehī ca karṇapālyāṃ gadāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saukumāryāc cirotsṛṣṭe sahasā 'bhipravardhite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.5"> karṇaśopho bhavet pālyāṃ sarujaḥ paripoṭavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇāruṇanibhaḥ stabdhaḥ sa vātāt paripoṭakaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.6"> gurvābharaṇasaṃyogāttāḍanād gharṣaṇādapi |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophaḥ pālyāṃ bhavec chyāvo dāhapākaruganvitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.7"> rakto vā raktapittābhyām utpātaḥ sa gado mataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         balādvardhayataḥ karṇaṃ pālyāṃ vāyuḥ prakupyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.8"> gṛhītvā sakaphaṃ kuryāc chophaṃ tadvarṇavedanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         unmanthakaḥ sakaṇḍūko vikāraḥ kaphavātajaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.9"> vardhamāne yadā karṇe kaṇḍūdāharuganvitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śopho bhavati pākaś ca tvakstho 'sau duḥkhavardhanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.10"> kaphāsṛkkṛmayaḥ kuryuḥ sarṣapābhā vikāriṇīḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         srāviṇīḥ piḍakāḥ pālyāṃ kaṇḍūdāharuganvitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.11"> kaphāsṛkkṛmisaṃbhūtaḥ sa visarpannitastataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihyāt saśaṣkulīṃ pālīṃ parilehīti sa smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.12"> pālyāmayā hy amī ghorā narasyāpratikāriṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mithyāhāravihārasya pāliṃ hiṃsyur upekṣitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.13"> tasmād āśu bhiṣak teṣu snehādikramamācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā 'bhyaṅgaparīṣekapradehāsṛgvimokṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.14"> sāmānyato viśeṣāc ca vakṣyāmyabhyañjanaṃ prati |
                        <caesura/>
                         kharamañjariyaṣṭyāhvasaindhavāmaradārubhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.15"> supiṣṭaiḥ sāśvagandhaiś ca mūlakāvalgujaiḥ phalaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpistailavasāmajjamadhūcchiṣṭāni pācayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.16"> sakṣīrāṇyatha taiḥ pāliṃ pradihyāt paripoṭake |
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjiṣṭhātilayaṣṭyāhvasārivotpalapadmakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.17"> sarodhraiḥ sakadambaiś ca balājambvāmrapallavaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ dhānyāmlasaṃyuktaṃ tailamutpātanāśanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.18"> tālapatryaśvagandhārkabākucīphalasaindhavaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ kulīragodhābhyāṃ vasayā saha pācitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.19"> saralālāṅgalībhyāṃ ca hitamunmanthanāśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā 'śmantakajambvāmrapatrakvāthena secanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.20"> prapauṇḍarīkamadhukamañjiṣṭhārajanīdvayaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇair udvartanaiḥ pālīṃ tailāktāmavacūṇayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.21"> lākṣāviḍaṅgakalkena tailaṃ paktvā 'vacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         svinnāṃ gomayapiṇḍena pradihyāt parilehike || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.22"> piṣṭair viḍaṅgair athavā trivṛcchyāmārkasaṃyutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karañjeṅgudibījair vā kuṭajāragvadhāyutaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.23"> sarvair vā sārṣapaṃ tailaṃ siddhaṃ maricasaṃyutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sanimbapatrair abhyaṅge madhūcchiṣṭānvitaṃ hitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.24"> pālīṣu vyādhiyuktāsu tanvīṣu kaṭhināsu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         puṣṭyārthaṃ mārdavārthaṃ ca kuryād abhyañjanaṃ tvidam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.25"> lopākānūpamajjānaṃ vasāṃ tailaṃ navaṃ ghṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         paceddaśaguṇaṃ kṣīramāvāpya madhuraṃ gaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.26"> apāmārgāśvagandhe ca tathā lākṣārasaṃ śubham |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatsiddhaṃ paripūtaṃ ca svanuguptaṃ nidhāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.27"> tenābhyañjyāt sadā pālīṃ susvinnāmtimarditām |
                        <caesura/>
                         etena pālyo vardhante nirujo nirupadravāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.28"> mṛdvyaḥ puṣṭāḥ samāḥ snigdhā jāyante bhūṣaṇakṣamāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nīlīdalaṃ bhṛṅgarajo 'rjunatvak piṇḍītakaṃ kṛṣṇamayor ajaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         bījodbhavaṃ sāhacaraṃ ca puṣpaṃ pathyākṣadhātrīsahitaṃ vicūrṇya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.29"> ekīkṛtaṃ sarvam idaṃ pramāya paṅkena tulyaṃ
                        nalinībhavena |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃyojya pakṣaṃ kalaśe nidhāya lauhe vipacedvimiśraṃ rasena
                        bhṛṅgatriphalābhavena |
                        <caesura/>
                         āsannapāke ca parīkṣaṇārthaṃ patraṃ balākābhavam ākṣipec ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.30"> anena tailaṃ vipaced vimiśraṃ rasena
                        bhṛṅgatriphalābhavena| āsannapāke ca parīkṣaṇārthaṃ patraṃ
                        balākābhavamākṣipecca|| </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.31"> bhaved yadā tadbhramarāṅganīlaṃ tadā vipakvaṃ vinidhāya
                        pātre |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇāyase māsam avasthitaṃ tadabhyaṅgayogāt palitāni hanyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.32"> sairīyajambvarjunakāśmarījaṃ puṣpaṃ tilānmārkavacūtabīje
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         punarnave kardamakaṇṭakāryau kāsīsapiṇḍītakabījasāram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.33"> phalatrayaṃ loharajo 'ñjanaṃ ca yaṣṭyāhvayaṃ
                        nīrajasārive ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭvā 'tha sarvaṃ saha modayanty ā sārāmbhasā bījakasaṃbhavena || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.34"> sārāmbhasaḥ saptabhir eva paś cāt prasthaiḥ samāloḍya
                        daśāhaguptam |
                        <caesura/>
                         lauhe supātre vinidhāya tailamakṣodbhavaṃ tac ca pacet prayatnāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.35"> pakvaṃ ca lauhe 'bhinave nidhāya nasyaṃ vidadhyāt
                        pariśuddhakāyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhyaṅgayogaiś ca niyujyamānaṃ bhuñjīta māṣān kṛśarāmatho vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.36"> māsopariṣṭād ghanakuñjitāgrāḥ keśā bhavanti
                        bhramarāñjanābhāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         keśās tathā 'nye khalatau bhaveyurjarā na cainaṃ sahasā 'bhyupaiti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.37"> balaṃ paraṃ saṃbhavatīndiryāṇāṃ bhavec ca vaktraṃ
                        valibhir vimuktam |
                        <caesura/>
                         nākāmine 'nārthini nākṛtāya naivāraye tailamidaṃ pradeyam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.38"> lākṣā rodhraṃ dve haridre śilāle kuṣṭhaṃ nāgaṃ gair ikā
                        varṇakāś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjiṣṭhogrā syāt surāṣṭrodbhavā ca pattaṅgaṃ vai rocanā cāñjanaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.39"> hemāṅgatvak pāṇḍupatraṃ vaṭasya kālīyaṃ syāt padmakaṃ
                        padmamadhyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktaṃ śvetaṃ candanaṃ pāradaṃ ca kākolyādiḥ kṣīrapiṣṭaś ca vargaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.40"> medo majjā sikthakaṃ goghṛtaṃ ca dugdhaṃ kvāthaḥ
                        kṣīriṇāṃ ca drumāṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         etat sarvaṃ pakvam aikadhyatas tu vaktrābhyaṅge sarpir uktaṃ pradhānam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.41"> hanyād vyaṅgaṃ nīlikāṃ cātivṛddhāṃ vaktre jātāḥ
                        sphoṭikāś cāpi kāś cit |
                        <caesura/>
                         padmākāraṃ nirvalīkaṃ ca vaktraṃ kuryād etat pīnagaṇḍaṃ manojñam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.42"> rājñām etad yoṣitāṃ cāpi nityaṃ kuryād vaidyas tat
                        samānāṃ nṛṇāṃ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuṣṭhaghnaṃ vai sarpiretat pradhānaṃ yeṣāṃ pāde santi vaipādikāś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.43"> harīkakīcūrṇamariṣṭapatraṃ cūtatvacaṃ dāḍimapuṣpavṛntam
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         patraṃ ca dadyān madayantikāyā lepo 'ṅgarāgo naradevayogyaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne miśrakacikitsitaṃ nāma
                        pañcaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||25 ||</l>
                </div>


                <div n="26" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.1"> athātaḥ kṣīṇabalīyaṃ vājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.3"> kalyasyodagravayaso vājīkaraṇasevinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarveṣv ṛtuṣv ahar ahar vyavāyo na nivāritaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.4"> sthavirāṇāṃ riraṃsūnāṃ strīṇāṃ vāllabhyam icchatām |
                        <caesura/>
                         yoṣitprasaṅgāt kṣīṇānāṃ klībānām alparetasām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.5"> vilāsinām arthavatāṃ rūpayauvanaśālinām |
                        <caesura/>
                         nṛṇāṃ ca bahubhāryāṇāṃ yogā vājīkarā hitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.6"> sevamāno yad aucity ād vājīvāty arthavegavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         nārīs tarpayate tena vājīkaraṇam ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.7"> bhojanāni vicitrāṇi pānāni vividhāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vācaḥ śrotrānugāminyas tvacaḥ sparśasukhās tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.8"> yāminī sendutilakā kāminī navayauvanā |
                        <caesura/>
                         gītaṃ śrotramanohāri tāmbūlaṃ madirāḥ srajaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.9"> gandhā manojñā rūpāṇi citrāṇy upavanāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         manasaś cāpratīghāto vājīkurvanti mānavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tais tair bhāvair ahṛdyais tu riraṃsor manasi kṣate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.10"> dveṣyastrīsaṃprayogāc ca klaibyaṃ tan mānasaṃ smṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭukāmloṣṇalavaṇair atimātropasevitaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.11"> saumyadhātukṣayo dṛṣṭaḥ klaibyaṃ tad aparaṃ smṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ativyavāyaśīlo yo na ca vājīkriyārataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.12"> dhvajabhaṅgam avāpnoti tacchukrakṣayahetukam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mahatā meḍhrarogeṇa marmacchedena vā punaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.13"> klaibyam etac caturthaṃ syān nṝṇāṃ puṃstvopaghātajam |
                        <caesura/>
                         janmaprabhṛti yaḥ klībaḥ klaibyaṃ tat sahajaṃ smṛtam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.14"> balinaḥ kṣubdhamanaso nirodhād brahmacaryataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṣṭhaṃ klaibyaṃ mataṃ tat tu kharaśukranimittajam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.15"> asādhyaṃ sahajaṃ klaibyaṃ marmacchedāc ca yad bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyānām itareṣāṃ tu kāryo hetuviparyayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.16"> vidhir vājīkaro yas tu taṃ pravakṣyāmy ataḥ param |
                        <caesura/>
                         tilamāṣavidārīṇāṃ śālīnāṃ cūrṇam eva vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.17"> pauṇḍrakekṣurasairārdraṃ marditaṃ saindhavānvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         varāhamedasā yuktāṃ ghṛtenotkārikāṃ pacet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.18"> tāṃ bhakṣayitvā puruṣo gacchet tu pramadāśatam |
                        <caesura/>
                         bastāṇḍasiddhe payasi bhāvitān asakṛt tilān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.19"> śiśumāravasāpakvāḥ śaṣkulyastistailaiḥ kṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaḥ svādet sa pumān gacchet strīṇāṃ śatam apūrvavat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.20"> pippalīlavaṇopete bastāṇḍe kṣīrasarpiṣi |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhite bhakṣayed yas tu sa gacchet pramadāśatam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.21"> pippalīmāṣaśālīnāṃ yavagodhūmayos tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇabhāgaiḥ samais tais tu ghṛte pūpalikāṃ pacet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.22"> tāṃ bhakṣayitvā pītvā tu śarkarāmadhuraṃ payaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         naraś caṭakavad gacched daśavārān nirantaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.23"> vidāryāḥ sukṛtaṃ cūrṇaṃ svarasenaiva bhāvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpirmadhuyutaṃ līḍhvā daśa strīr adhigacchati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.24"> evam āmalakaṃ cūrṇaṃ svarasenaiva bhāvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarkarāmadhusarpibhir yuktaṃ līḍhvā payaḥ pibet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.25"> etenāśītivarṣo 'pi yuveva parihṛṣyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalīlavaṇopete bastāṇḍe ghṛtasādhite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.26"> śiśumārasya vā khādet te tu vājīkare bhṛśam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kulīrakūrmanakrāṇām aṇḍāny evaṃ tu bhakṣayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.27"> mahiṣarṣabhabastānāṃ pibec chukrāṇi vā naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśvatthaphalamūlatvakśuṅgāsiddhaṃ payo naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.28"> pītvā saśarkarākṣaudraṃ kuliṅga iva hṛṣyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārimūlakalkaṃ tu śṛtena payasā naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.29"> uḍumbarasamaṃ pītvā vṛddho 'pi taruṇāyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         māṣāṇāṃ palam ekaṃ tu saṃyuktaṃ kṣaudrasarpiṣā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.30"> avalihya payaḥ pītvā tena vājī bhaven naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrapakvāṃs tu godhūmān ātmaguptāphalaiḥ saha || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.31"> śītān ghṛtayutān khādet tataḥ paś cāt payaḥ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         nakramūṣikamaṇḍūkacaṭakāṇḍakṛtaṃ ghṛtam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.32"> pādābhyaṅgena kurute balaṃ bhūmiṃ tu na spṛśet |
                        <caesura/>
                         yāvat spṛśati no bhūmiṃ tāvad gacchen nirantaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.33"> svayaṃguptekṣurakayoḥ phalacūrṇaṃ saśarkaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhāroṣṇena naraḥ pītvā payasā na kṣayaṃ vrajet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.34"> uccaṭācūrṇaṃ peyam evaṃ balārthinā |
                        <caesura/>
                         svayaṃguptāphalair yuktaṃ māṣasūpaṃ piben naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.35"> guptāphalaṃ gokṣurakāc ca bījaṃ tathoccaṭāṃ gopayasā
                        vipācya |
                        <caesura/>
                         khajāhataṃ śarkarayā ca yuktaṃ pītvā naro hṛṣyati sarvarātram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.36"> māṣān vidārīm api soccaṭāṃ ca kṣīre gavāṃ
                        kṣaudraghṛtopapannām |
                        <caesura/>
                         pītvā naraḥ śarkarayā suyuktāṃ kuliṅgavad dhṛṣyati sarvarātram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.37"> gṛṣṭīnāṃ vṛddhavatsānāṃ māṣaparṇabhṛtāṃ gavām |
                        <caesura/>
                         yat kṣīraṃ tat praśaṃsanti balakāmeṣu jantuṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.38"> kṣīramāṃsagaṇāḥ sarve kākolyādiś ca pūjitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vājīkaraṇahetor hi tasmāt tut tu prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.39"> ete vājīkarā yogāḥ prītyapatyabalapradāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sevyā viśuddhopacitadehaiḥ kālādyapekṣayā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ kṣīṇabalīyavājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ nāma
                        ṣaḍviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||26 ||</l>
                </div>



                <div n="27" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>saptaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.1"> athātaḥ sarvopaghātaśamanīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.3"> pūrve vayasi madhye vā manuṣyasya rasāyanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājñaḥ snigdhaśuddhatanoḥ sadā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.4"> nāviśuddhaśarīrasya yukto rāsāyano vidhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na bhāti vāsasi kliṣṭe raṅgayoga ivāhitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.5"> śarīrasyopaghātā ye doṣajā mānasās tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         upadiṣṭāḥ pradeśeṣu teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi vāraṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.6"> śītodakaṃ payaḥ kṣaudraṃ sarpirity ekaśo dviśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         triśaḥ samastamathavā prāk pītaṃ sthāpayed vayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.7"> tatra viḍaṅgataṇḍulacūrṇamāhṛtya yaṣṭīmadhukamadhuyuktaṃ
                        yathābalaṃ śītatoyenopayuñjīta śītatoyaṃ cānupibed evam aharahar māsaṃ, tad
                        eva madhuyuktaṃ bhallātakakvāthena vā, madhudrākṣākvāthayuktaṃ vā,
                        madhvāmalakarasābhyāṃ vā, guḍūcīkvāthena vā, evam ete pañca prayogā
                        bhavanti; jīrṇe mudgāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇenālpasnehena ghṛtavantam odanam
                        aśnīyāt; ete svalvarśāṃsi kṣapayanti, kṛmīn upaghnanti, grahaṇadhāraṇaśaktiṃ
                        janayanti, māse māse ca prayoge varṣaśataṃ varṣaśatamāyuṣo 'bhivṛddhir
                        bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.8"> viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṃ droṇaṃ piṣṭapacane piṣṭavadupasvedya
                        vigatakaṣāyaṃ svinnamavatārya dṛṣadi piṣṭamāyase dṛḍhe kumbhe
                        madhūdakottaraṃ prāvṛṣi bhasmarāśāvantargṛhe caturo māsānnidadhyāt,
                        varṣāvigame coddhṛtyopasaṃskṛtaśarīraḥ sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā
                        prātaḥprātar yathābalam upayuñjīta, jīrṇe mudgāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇena
                        ghṛtavantam odanam aśnīyāt, pāṃśuśayyāyāṃ śayīta, tasya māsādūrdhvaṃ
                        sarvāṅgebhyaḥ kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, tān aṇutailenābhyaktasya
                        vaṃśavidalenāpaharet, dvitīye pipīlikāstṛtīye yūkāstathaivāpaharet, caturthe
                        dantanakharomāṇyavaśīryante; pañcame praśastaguṇalakṣaṇāni jāyante, amānuṣaṃ
                        cādity aprakāśaṃ vapuradhigacchati, dūrācchravaṇāni darśanā nicāsya
                        bhavanti, rajastamasī cāpohya sattvam adhitiṣṭhati, śrutanigādyapūrvotpādī
                        gajabalo 'śvajavaḥ punaryuvā 'ṣṭau varṣaśatānyāyuravāpnoti;
                        tasyāṇutailamabhyaṅgārthe, candanam upalepanārthe,
                        bhallātakavidhānavadāhāraḥ parihāraś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.9"> kāśmaryāṇāṃ niṣkulīkṛtānāmeṣa eva kalpaḥ
                        pāṃśuśayyābhojanavarjaṃ; atra hi payasā śṛtena bhoktavyaṃ, samānamanyat
                        pūrveṇāśiṣaś ca | śoṇitapittanimitteṣu vikāreṣveteṣām upayogaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.10"> yathoktamāgāraṃ praviśya balāmūlārdhapalaṃ palaṃ vā
                        payasā ''āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ, evaṃ
                        dvādaśarātram upayujya dvādaśa varṣāṇi vayastiṣṭhati; evaṃ divasaśatam
                        upayujya varṣaśataṃ vayastiṣṭhati | evam evātibalānāgabalāvidārīśatāvarīṇām
                        upayogaḥ | viśeṣatastvatibalāmudakena, nāgabalācūrṇaṃ madhunā, vidārīcūrṇaṃ
                        kṣīreṇa, śatāvarīmapyevaṃ, pūrveṇānyat samānamāśiṣaś ca samāḥ |
                        etāstvauṣadhayo balakāmānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ raktapittopasṛṣṭānāṃ śoṇitaṃ chardayatāṃ
                        viricyamānānāṃ copadiśyante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.11"> vārāhīmūlatulācūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tato mātrāṃ madhuyuktāṃ
                        payasā ''āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ, pratibedho 'tra
                        pūrvavat; prayogamimam upasevamāno varṣaśatamāyuravāpnoti strīṣu cākṣayatām,
                        etenaiva cūrṇena payo 'vacūrṇya śṛtaśītam abhimathyājyamutpādya madhuyutam
                        upayuñjīta sāyaṃprātar ekakālaṃ vā, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ, evaṃ
                        māsam upayujya sauparṇaṃ bhavaty analpabalaḥ strīṣu cākṣayo
                        varṣaśatāyurbhavatīti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.12"> cakṣuḥkāmaḥ prāṇakāmo vā bījakasārāgnimanthamūlaṃ
                        niṣkvāthya māṣaprasthaṃ sādhayet, tasmin sidhyati citrakamūlānām akṣamātraṃ
                        kalkaṃ dadyād āmalakarasacaturthabhāgaṃ, tataḥ svinnam avatārya
                        sahasrasṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā śītībhūtaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ saṃsṛjyopayuñjīta
                        yathābalaṃ, yathāsātmyaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ pariharan bhakṣayet| jīrṇe
                        mudgāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇena ghṛtavantamodanamaśnīyāt payasā vā māsatrayam;
                        evamābhyāṃ prayogābhyāṃ cakṣuḥ sauparṇaṃ bhavaty analpabalaḥ strīṣu cākṣayo
                        varṣaśatāyur bhavatīti|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.13"> bhavati cātra payasā saha siddhāni naraḥ śaṇaphalāni yaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhakṣayet payasā sārdhaṃ vayas tasya na śīryate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne sarvopaghātaśamanīyaṃ
                        rasāyanacikitsitaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||27 ||</l>
                </div>


                <div n="28" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>aṣṭaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.1"> athāto medhāyuṣkāmīyaṃ rasāyanacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvanatariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.3"> medhāyuḥkāmaḥ śvetāvalgujaphalānyātapapariśuṣkāṇyādāya
                        sūkṣmacūrṇāni kṛtvā guḍena sahāloḍya snehakumbhe saptarātraṃ dhānyarāśau
                        nidadhyāt, saptarātrād uddhṛtya hṛtadoṣasya yathābalaṃ piṇḍaṃ prayacched
                        anudite sūrye, uṣṇodakaṃ cānupibet; bhallātakavidhānavac cāgārapraveśaḥ,
                        jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe himābhir adbhiḥ pariṣiktagātraḥ śālīnāṃ ṣaṣṭikānāṃ ca
                        payasā śarkarāmadhureṇaudanam aśnīyāt; evaṃ ṣaṇmāsān upayujya vigatapāpmā
                        balavarṇopetaḥ śrutanigādī smṛtimān arogo varṣaśatāyur bhavati | kuṣṭhinaṃ
                        pāṇḍurogiṇam udariṇaṃ vā kṛṣṇāyā gomūtreṇāloḍyārdhapalikaṃ piṇḍaṃ
                        vigatalauhitye savitari pāyayet, parāhṇe cālavaṇenāmalakayūṣeṇa sarpiṣmantam
                        odanam aśnīyāt, evaṃ māsam upayujya smṛtimān arogo varṣaśatāyur bhavati |
                        eṣa evopayogaś citrakamūlānāṃ rajanyāś ca; citrakamūle viśeṣo dvipalikaṃ
                        piṇḍaṃ paraṃ pramāṇaṃ, śeṣaṃ pūrvavat || </l>
