                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.4"> hṛtadoṣa eva pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto yathākramamāgāraṃ
                        praviśya maṇḍūkaparṇīsvarasam ādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā yathābalaṃ
                        payasā ''āloḍya pibet payo 'nupānaṃ vā, tasyāṃ jīrṇāyāṃ yavānnaṃ
                        payasopayuñjīta; tilair vā saha bhakṣayet trīn māsān payo 'nupānaṃ, jīrṇe
                        payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ; evam upayuñjāno brahmavarcasī śrutanigādī
                        bhavati varṣaśatam āyur avāpnoti | trirātropoṣitaś ca trirātram enāṃ
                        bhakṣayet, trirātrādūrdhvaṃ payaḥ sarpir iti copayuñjīta | bilvamātraṃ
                        piṇḍaṃ vā payasā ''āloḍya pibet, evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayujya medhāvī
                        varṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.5"> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto
                        brāhmīsvarasamādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā yathābalampayuñjīta,
                        jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe yavāgūmalavaṇaṃ pibet, kṣīrasātmyo vā payasā
                        bhuñjīta, evaṃ saptarātram upayujya brahmavarcasī medhāvī bhavati, dvitīyaṃ
                        saptarātram upayujya grantham īpsitam utpādayati naṣṭaṃ cāsya prādur
                        bhavati, tṛtīyaṃ saptarātram upayujya dviruccāritaṃ śatam apy avadhārayati,
                        evam ekaviṃśatirātram upayujyālakṣmīr apakrāmati; mūrtimatī cainaṃ vāgdevy
                        anupraviśati, sarvāś cainaṃ śrutaya upatiṣṭhanti, śrutadharaḥ
                        pañcavarṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.6"> brāhmīsvarasaprasthadvaye ghṛtaprasthaṃ viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṃ
                        kuḍavaṃ dve dve pale vacāmṛtayor dvādaśa harītakyāmalakabibhītakāni
                        ślakṣṇapiṣṭānyāvāpyaikadhyaṃ sādhayitvā svanuguptaṃ nidadhyāt, tataḥ
                        pūrvavidhānena mātrāṃ yathābalam upayuñjīta, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ity
                        āhāraḥ, pūrvavac cātra parīhāraḥ, etenordhvam adhas tiryak kṛmayo
                        niṣkrāmanti, alakṣmīr apakrāmati, puṣkaravarṇaḥ sthiravayāḥ śrutanigādī
                        trivarṣaśatāyur bhavati; etad eva
                        kuṣṭhaviṣamajvarāpasmāronmādaviṣabhūtagraheṣv anyeṣu ca mahāvyādhiṣu
                        saṃśodhanam ādiśanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.7"> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya haimavatyā vacāyāḥ
                        piṇḍamāmalakamātram abhihutaṃ payasā ''āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana
                        ity āhāraḥ, evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayuñjīta, tato 'sya śrotraṃ vivriyate,
                        dvirabhyāsāt smṛtimān bhavati, trirabhyāsācchrutamādatte, caturdvādaśarātram
                        upayujya sarvaṃ tarati kilbiṣaṃ, tārkṣyadarśanamutpadyate, śatāyuś ca
                        bhavati | dve dve pale itarasyā vacāyā viṣkvāthya pibet payasā, samānaṃ
                        bhojanaṃ, samāḥ pūrveṇāśiṣaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.8"> vacāśatapākaṃ vā sarpirdroṇam upayujya
                        pañcavarṣaśatāyurbhavati, galagaṇḍāpacīślīpadasvaramedāṃś cāpahantīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.9"> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi āyuṣkāmarasāyanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mantrauṣadhasamāyuktaṃ saṃvatsaraphalapradam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.10"> bilvasya cūrṇaṃ puṣye tu hutaṃ vārān sahasraśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śrīsūktena naraḥ kalye sasuvarṇaṃ dine dine || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.11"> sarpir madhuyutaṃ lihyād alakṣmīnāśanaṃ param |
                        <caesura/>
                         tvacaṃ vihāya bilvasya mūlakvāthaṃ dine dine || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.12"> prāśnīyāt payasā sārdhaṃ snātvā hutvā samāhitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         daśasāhasram āyuṣyaṃ smṛtaṃ yuktarathaṃ bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.13"> hutvā bisānāṃ kvāthaṃ tu madhulājaiś ca saṃyutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         amoghaṃ śatasāhasraṃ yuktaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.14"> suvarṇaṃ padmabījāni madhu lājāḥ priyaṅgavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gavyena payasā pītam alakṣmīṃ pratiṣedhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.15"> nīlotpaladalakvātho gavyena payasā śṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sasuvarṇastilaiḥ sārdham alakṣmīnāśanaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.16"> gavyaṃ payaḥ suvarṇaṃ ca madhūcchiṣṭaṃ ca mākṣikam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pītaṃ śatasahasrābhihutaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.17"> vacāghṛtasuvarṇaṃ ca bilvacūrṇam iti trayam |
                        <caesura/>
                         medhyam āyuṣyam ārogyapuṣṭisaubhāgyavardhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.18"> vāsāmūlatulākvāthe tailam āvāpya sādhitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         hutvā sahasram aśnīyān medhyam āyuṣyam ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.19"> yāvakāṃstāvakān khāded abhibhūya yavāṃs tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalīmadhusaṃyuktān śikṣā caraṇavad bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.20"> madhvāmalakacūrṇāni suvarṇam iti ca trayam |
                        <caesura/>
                         prāśyāriṣṭagṛhīto 'pi mucyate prāṇasaṃśayāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.21"> śatāvarīghṛtaṃ samyag upayuktaṃ dine dine |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakṣaudraṃ sasuvarṇaṃ ca narendraṃ sthāpayed vaśe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.22"> gocandanā mohanikā madhukaṃ mākṣikaṃ madhu |
                        <caesura/>
                         suvarṇam iti saṃyogaḥ peyaḥ saubhāgyam icchatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.23"> padmanīlotpalakvāthe yaṣṭīmadhukasaṃyute |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpir āsāditaṃ gavyaṃ sasuvarṇaṃ sadā pibet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.24"> payaś cānupibet siddhaṃ teṣām eva samudbhave |
                        <caesura/>
                         alakṣmīghnaṃ sadā ''āyuṣyaṃ rājyāya subhagāya ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.25"> yatra nodīrito mantro yogeṣv eteṣu sādhane |
                        <caesura/>
                         śabditā tatra sarvatra gāyatrī tripadā bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.26"> pāpmānaṃ nāśayanty etā dadyuś cauṣadhayaḥ śriyam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryur nāgabalaṃ cāpi manuṣyam amaropamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.27"> satatādhyayanaṃ vādaḥ paratantrāvalokanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadvidyā cāryasevā ca buddhimedhākaro guṇaḥ(gaṇaḥ) || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.28"> āyuṣyaṃ bhojanaṃ jīrṇe vegānāṃ cāvidhāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         brahmacaryam ahiṃsā ca sāhasānāṃ ca varjanam ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne medhāyuṣkāmīyaṃ
                        rasāyanaṃ nāmāṣṭāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||28 ||</l>
                </div>



                <div n="29" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>ekonatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.1"> athātaḥ svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.3"> brahmādayo 'sṛjan pūrvam amṛtaṃ somasaṃjñitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         jarāmṛtyuvināśāya vidhānaṃ tasya vakṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.4"> eka eva khalu bhagavān somaḥ sthānanāmākṛtivīryaviśeṣaiś
                        caturviṃśatidhābhidyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.5"> aṃśumān muñjavāṃś caiva candramā rajataprabhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dūrvāsomaḥ kanīyāṃś ca śvetākṣaḥ kanakaprabhaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.6"> pratānavāṃstālavṛntaḥ karavīro 'ṃśavān api |
                        <caesura/>
                         svayaṃprabho mahāsomo yaś cāpi garuḍāhṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.7"> gāyatras traiṣṭubhaḥ pāṅkto jāgataḥ śākvaras tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         agniṣṭomo raivataś ca yathokta iti saṃjñitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.8"> gāyatryā tripadā yukto yaś coḍupatir ucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         ete somāḥ samākhyātā vedoktair nām abhiḥ śubhaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.9"> sarveṣām eva caiteṣām eko vidhir upāsane |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarve tulyaguṇāś caiva vidhānaṃ teṣu vakṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.10"> ato 'nyatamaṃ somam upayuyukṣuḥ
                        sarvopakaraṇaparicārakopetaḥ praśaste deśe trivṛtam āgāraṃ kārayitvā
                        hṛtadoṣaḥ pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhaktaḥ praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu
                        aṃśumantam ādāyādhvarakalpenāhṛtam abhiṣutam abhihutaṃ cāntarāgāre
                        kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanaḥ somakandaṃ suvarṇasūcyā vidārya payo gṛhṇīyāt
                        sauvarṇe (rājate vā) pātre 'ñjalimātraṃ, tataḥ sakṛd evopayuñjīta
                        nāsvādayan, tata upaspṛśya śeṣam apsv avasādya yamaniyamābhyām ātmānaṃ
                        saṃyojya vāgyato 'bhyantarataḥ suhṛdbhir upāsyamāno viharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.11"> rasāyanaṃ pītavāṃs tu nivāte tanmanāḥ śuciḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āsīta tiṣṭhet krāmec ca na kathaṃcana saṃviśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.12"> sāyaṃ vā bhuktavān upaśrutaśāntiḥ kuśaśayyāyāṃ
                        kṛṣṇājinottarāyāṃ suhṛdbhir upāsyamānaḥ śayīta, tṛṣito vā śītodakamātrāṃ
                        pibet (aśanāyito vā kṣīraṃ); tataḥ prātar utthāyopaśrutaśāntiḥ kṛtamaṅgalo
                        gāṃ spṛṣṭvā tatahaivāsīta, tasya jīrṇe some chardir utpadyate, tataḥ
                        śoṇitāktaṃ kṛmivyāmiśraṃ charditavate sāyaṃ śṛtaśītaṃ kṣīraṃ vitaret; tatas
                        tṛtīye 'hani kṛmivyāmiśram atisāryate, sa
                        tenāniṣṭapratigrahabhuktaprabhṛtibhir viśeṣair vinirmuktaḥ śuddhatanur
                        bhavati, tataḥ sāyaṃ snātāya pūrvavad eva kṣīraṃ vitaret,
                        kṣaumavastrāstṛtāyāṃ cainaṃ śayyāyāṃ śāyayet; tataś caturthe 'hani tasya
                        śvayathur utpadyate, tataḥ sarvāṅgebhyaḥ kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, tadahaś ca
                        śayyāyāṃ pāṃśubhir avakīryamāṇaḥ śayīta, tataḥ sāyaṃ pūrvavad eva kṣīraṃ
                        vitaret; evaṃ pañcamaṣaṣṭhayor divasayor varteta, kevalam ubhayakālam asmai
                        kṣīraṃ vitaret; tataḥ saptame 'hani nirmāṃsas tv agasthibhūtaḥ kevalaṃ
                        somaparigrahād evocchvasiti, tad ahaś ca kṣīreṇa sukhoṣṇena pariṣicya
                        tilamadhukacandanānuliptadehaṃ payaḥ pāyayet; tato 'ṣṭame 'hani prātar eva
                        kṣīrapariṣiktaṃ candanapradigdhāgātraṃ payaḥ pāyayitvā pāṃśuśayyāṃ
                        samutsṛjya kṣaumavastrāstṛtāyāṃ śayyāyāṃ śāyayet, tato 'sya māṃsam
                        āpyāyyate, tvak cāvadalati, dantanakharomāṇi cāsya patanti; tasya
                        navamadivasāt prabhṛty aṇutailābhyaṅgaḥ somavalkakaṣāyapariṣekaḥ; tato
                        daśame 'hany etad eva vitaret, tato 'sya tvak sthiratām upaiti; evam
                        ekādaśadvādaśayor varteta; tatas trayodaśāt prabhṛti
                        somavalkakaṣāyapariṣekaḥ, evam āṣoḍaśād varteta; tataḥ saptadaśāṣṭādaśayor
                        divasayor daśanā jāyante śikhariṇaḥ snigdhavajravaidūryasphaṭikaprakāśāḥ
                        samāḥ sthirāḥ sahiṣṇavaḥ, tadā prabhṛti cānavaiḥ śālitaṇḍulaiḥ kṣīrayavāgūm
                        upaseveta yāvat pañcaviṃśatiriti; tato 'smai dadyāc chālyodanaṃ
                        mṛdūbhayakālaṃ payasā, tato 'sya nakhā jāyante vidrumendragopakataruṇādity
                        aprakāśāḥ, sthirāḥ snigdhā lakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ keśāś ca sūkṣmā jāyante, tvak ca
                        nīlotpalātasīpuṣpavaidūryaprakāśā; ūrdhvaṃ ca māsāt keśān vāpayet, vāpayitvā
                        cośīracandanakṛṣṇatilakalkaiḥ śiraḥ pradihyāt payasā vā snāpayet; tato
                        'syānantaraṃ saptarātrāt keśā jāyante bhramarāñjananibhāḥ kuñcitāḥ sthirāḥ
                        snigdhāḥ; tatas trirātrāt prathamāvasathaparisarān niṣkramya muhūrtaṃ
                        sthitvā punar evāntaḥ praviśet, tato 'sya balātailam abhyaṅgārthe 'vacāryaṃ,
                        yavapiṣṭam udvartanārthe, sukhoṣṇaṃ ca payaḥ pariṣekārthe, ajakarṇakaṣāyam
                        utsādanārthe, sośīraṃ kūpodakaṃ snānārthe, candanam anulepārthe,
                        āmalakarasavimiśrāś cāsya yūṣasūpavikalpāḥ, kṣīramadhukasiddhaṃ ca
                        kṛṣṇatilam avacāraṇārthe, evaṃ daśarātraṃ; tato 'nyad daśarātraṃ dvitīye
                        parisare varteta; tatas tṛtīye parisare sthirīkurvann ātmānam
                        anyaddaśarātram āsīta, kiñcid ātapapavanān vā seveta, punaś cāntaḥ praviśet,
                        na cātmānam ādarśe 'psu vā nirīkṣeta rūpaśālitvāt ; tato 'nyad daśarātraṃ
                        krodhādīn pariharet, evaṃ sarveṣām upayogavikalpaḥ | viśeṣatas tu
                        vallīpratānakṣupakādayaḥ somā brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyair bhakṣayitavyāḥ |
                        teṣāṃ tu pramāṇam ardhacatuṣkamuṣṭayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.13"> aṃśumantaṃ sauvarṇe pātre 'bhiṣuṇuyāt, candramasaṃ
                        rājate; tāv upayujyāṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam avāpyeśānaṃ devam anupraviśati,
                        śeṣāṃs tu tāmramaye mṛnmaye vā rohite vā carmaṇi vitate; śūdravarjaṃ tribhir
                        varṇaiḥ somā upayoktavyāḥ | tataś caturthe māse paurṇamāsyāṃ śucau deśe
                        brāhmaṇānarcayitvā kṛtamaṅgalo niṣkramya yathoktaṃ vrajed iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.14"> oṣadhīnāṃ patiṃ somam upayujya vicakṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         daśavarṣasahasrāṇi navāṃ dhārayate tanum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.15"> nāgnir na toyaṃ na viṣaṃ na śastraṃ nāstram eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyālam āyuḥkṣapaṇe samarthāni bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.16"> bhadrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇāṃ prasrutānām anekadhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuñjarāṇāṃ sahasrasya balaṃ samadhigacchati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.17"> kṣīrodaṃ śakrasadanam uttarāṃś ca kurūn api |
                        <caesura/>
                         yatrecchati sa gantuṃ vā tatrāpratihatā gatiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.18"> kandarpa iva rūpeṇa kāntyā candra ivāparaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prahlādayati bhūtānāṃ manāṃsi sa mahādyutiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.19"> sāṅgopāṅgāṃś ca nikhilān vedān vindati tattvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caraty amoghasaṅkalpo devavac cākhilaṃ jagat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.20"> sarveṣām eva somānāṃ patrāṇi daśa pañca ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāni śukle ca kṛṣṇe ca jāyante nipatanti ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.21"> ekaikaṃ jāyate patraṃ somasyāharahas tadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuklasya paurṇamāsyāṃ tu bhavet pañcadaśacchadaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.22"> śīryate patram ekaikaṃ divase divase punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇapakṣakṣaye cāpi latā bhavati kevalā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.23"> aṃśumān ājyagandhas tu kandavān rajataprabhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kadalyākārakandas tu muñjavāṃ llaśunacchadaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.24"> candramāḥ kanakābhāso jale carati sarvadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         garuḍāhṛtanāmā ca śvetākṣaś cāpi pāṇḍurau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.25"> sarpanirmokasadṛśau tau vṛkṣāgrāvalambinau |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā 'nye maṇḍalaiś citraiś citritā iva bhānti te || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.26"> sarva eva tu vijñeyāḥ somāḥ pañcadaśacchadāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrakandalatāvantaḥ patrair nānāvidhaiḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.27"> himavaty arbude sahye mahendre malaye tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śrīparvate devagirau girau devasahe tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.28"> pāriyātre ca vindhye ca devasunde hrade tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         uttareṇa vitastāyāḥ pravṛddhā ye mahīdharāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.29"> haṣṭhavat plavate tatra candramāḥ somasattamaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyoddeśeṣu cāpy anti muñjavān aṃśumān api || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.30"> tasyoddeśeṣu cāpy asti muñjavānaṃśumān api |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāśmīreṣu saro divyaṃ nāmnā kṣudrakamānasam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.31"> gāyatras traiṣṭubhaḥ pāṅkto jāgataḥ śākvaras tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         atra santy apare cāpi somāḥ somasamaprabhāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.32"> yaiś cātra mandabhāgyais te bhiṣajaś cāpamānitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na tān paśyanty adharmiṣṭhāḥ kṛtaghnāś cāpi mānavāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bheṣajadveṣiṇaś cāpi brāhmaṇadveṣiṇas tathā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
                        svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ rasāyanacikitsitaṃ nāmaikonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
                        ||29 ||</l>
                </div>

                <div n="30" type="level2" subtype="adhyāya">
                    <head>triṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ|</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.1"> athāto nivṛttasantāpīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.3"> yathā nivṛttasantāpā modante divi devatāḥ|
                        tathauṣadhīrimāḥ prāpya modante bhuvi mānavāḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.4"> atha khalu sapta puruṣā rasāyanaṃ nopayuñjīran; tad yathā
                        anātmavānalaso daridraḥ pramādī vyasanīpāpakṛd bheṣajāpamānī ceti| saptabhir
                        eva kāraṇairna saṃpadyate; tad yathā ajñānādanārambhādasthiracittatvād
                        dāridvyādanāyattatvād adharmādauṣadhālābhācceti|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.5"> athauṣadhīvyākhyāsyāmaḥ tatrājagarī, śvetakāpotī,
                        kṛṣṇakāpotī, gonasī, vārāhī, kanyā, chatrā, aticchatrā, kareṇuḥ, ajā,
                        cakrakā, ādity aparṇī, brahmasuvarcalā, śrāvaṇī, mahāśrāvaṇī, golomī,
                        ajalomī, mahāvegavatī, cetyaṣṭādaśa somasamavīryā mahauṣadhayo vyākhyātāḥ|
                        tāsāṃ somavat kriyāśīḥstutayaḥ śāstre+abhihitāḥ| tāsāmāgāre+abhihutānāṃ yāḥ
                        kṣīravatyastāsāṃ kṣīrakuḍavaṃ sakṛdevopayuñjīta, yāstvakṣīrā mūlavatyastāsāṃ
                        pradeśinīpramāṇāni trīṇi kāṇḍāni pramāṇam upayoge, śvetakāpotī samūlapatrā
                        bhakṣayitavyā, gonasyajagarīkṛṣṇakāpotīnāṃ sanakhamuṣṭiṃ khaṇḍaśaḥ
                        kalpayitvā kṣīreṇa vipācya parisrāvyābhighāritamabhihutaṃ ca
                        sakṛdevopayuñjīta, cakrakāyāḥ payaḥ sakṛdeva, brahmasuvarcalā saptarātram
                        upayoktavyā bhakṣyakalpena, śeṣāṇāṃ pañca pañca palāni kṣīrāḍhakakvathitāni
                        prasthe+avaśiṣṭe+avatārya parisrāvya sakṛdevopayuñjīta| somavadāhāravihārau
                        vyākhyātau, kevalaṃ navanītamabhyaṅgārthe, śeṣaṃ somavadānirgamāditi|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.6"> bhavanti cātra yuvānaṃ siṃhavikrāntaṃ kāntaṃ
                        śrutanigādinam| kuryuretāḥ krameṇaiva dvisahasrāyuṣaṃ naram|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.7"> aṅgadī kuṇḍalī maulī divyasrakcandanāmbaraḥ|
                        caratyamoghasaṅkalpo nabhasyambudadurgame|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.8"> vrajanti pakṣiṇo yena jalalambāś ca toyadāḥ| gatiḥ
                        sauṣadhisiddhasya somasiddhe gatiḥ parā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.9"> atha vakṣyāmi vijñānamauṣadhīnāṃ pṛthak pṛthak| maṇḍalaiḥ
                        kapilaiścitraiḥ sarpābhā pañcaparṇinī|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.10"> pañcāratnipramāṇā ca vijñeyā+ajagarī budhaiḥ| niṣpatrā
                        kanakābhāsā mūle dvyaṅgulasaṃmitā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.11"> sarpākārā lohitāntā śvetakāpotirucyate| dviparṇinīṃ
                        mūlabhavāmaruṇāṃ kṛṣṇamaṇḍalām|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.12"> dvyaratnimātrāṃ jānīyād gonasīṃ gonasākṛtim| sakṣīrāṃ
                        romaśāṃ mṛdvīṃ rasenekṣurasopamām|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.13"> evaṃrūparasāṃ cāpi kṛṣṇakāpotimādiśet|
                        kṛṣṇasarpasvarūpeṇa vārāhī kandasaṃbhavā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.14"> ekapatrā mahāvīryā bhinnāñjanasamaprabhā|
                        chatrāticchatrake vidyādrakṣoghne kandasaṃbhave|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.15"> jarāmṛtyunivāriṇyau śvetakāpotisaṃsthite|
                        kāntairdvādaśabhiḥ patrairmayūrāṅgaruhopamaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.16"> kandajā kāñcanakṣīrī kanyā nāma mahauṣadhī| kareṇuḥ
                        subahukṣīrā kandena gajarūpiṇī|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.17"> hastikarṇapalāśasya tulyaparṇā dviparṇinī|
                        ajāstanābhakandā tu sakṣīrā śruparūpiṇī|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.18"> ajā mahauṣadhī jñeyā śaṅkhakundendupāṇḍurā| śvetāṃ
                        vicitrakusumāṃ kākādanyā samāṃ kṣupām|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.19"> cakrakāmoṣadhīṃ vidyājjarāmṛtyunivāriṇīm| mūlinī
                        pañcabhiḥ patraiḥ suraktāṃśukakomalaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.20"> ādity aparṇinī jñeyā sadā++ādity ānuvartinī| kanakābhā
                        jalānteṣu sarvataḥ parisarpati|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.21"> sakṣīrā padminīprakhyā devī brahmasuvarcalā|
                        aratnimātrakṣupakā patrairdvyaṅgulasaṃmitaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.22"> puṣpairnīlotpalākāraiḥ phalaiś cāñjanasannibhaiḥ|
                        śrāvaṇī mahatī jñeyā kanakābhā payasvinī|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.23"> śrāvaṇī pāṇḍurābhāsā mahāśrāvaṇilakṣaṇā| golomī cājalomī
                        ca romaśe kandasaṃbhave|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.24"> haṃsapādīva vicchinnaiḥ patrairmūlasamudbhavaiḥ| athavā
                        śaṅkhapuṣpyā ca samānā sarvarūpataḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.25"> vetena mahatā++āviṣṭā sarpanirmokasannibhā| eṣā vegavatī
                        nāma jāyate hy ambudakṣaye|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.26"> saptādau sarparūpiṇyo hy auṣadhyo yāḥ prakīrtitāḥ|
                        tāsāmuddharaṇaṃ kāryaṃ mantreṇānena sarvadā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.27"> mahendrarāmakṛṣṇānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ gavāmapi| tapasā tejasā
                        vā+api praśāmyadhvaṃ śivāya vai|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.28"> natreṇānena matimān sarvā evābhimantrayet|
                        aśraddadhānairalasaiḥ kṛtaghnaiḥ pāpakarmabhiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.29"> naivāsādayituṃ śakyāḥ somāḥ somasamāstathā|
                        pītāvaśeṣamamṛtaṃ devairbrahmapurogamaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.30"> nihitaṃ somavīryāsu some cāpy oṣadhīpatau| devasunde
                        hradavare tathā sindhau mahānade|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.31"> dṛśyate ca jalānteṣu medhyā brahmasuvarcalā| ādity
                        aparṇinī jñeyā tathaiva himasaṃkṣaye|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.32"> dṛśyate+ajagarī nityaṃ gonasī cāmbudāgame| kāśmīreṣu
                        saro divyaṃ nāmnā kṣudrakamānasam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.33"> kareṇus tatra kanyā ca chatrāticchatrake tathā| golomī
                        cājalomī ca mahatī śrāvaṇī tathā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.34"> vasante kṛṣṇasarpākhyā gonasī ca pradṛśyate| kauśikīṃ
                        saritaṃ tīrtvā sañjayanty ās tu pūrvataḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.35"> kṣitipradeśo valmīkairācito yojanatrayam| vijñeyā tatra
                        kāpotī śvetā valmīkamūrdhasu|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.36"> malaye nalasetau ca vegavatyauṣadhī dhruvā| kārtikyāṃ
                        paurṇamāsyāṃ ca bhakṣayettāmupoṣitaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.37"> somavaccātra varteta phalaṃ tāvac ca kīrtitam| sarvā
                        viceyāstvopadhyaḥ somāś cāpy arbude girau|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.38"> sa śṛṅgairdevacaritairambudānīkabhedibhiḥ|
                        vyāptastīrthaiś ca vikhyātaiḥ siddharṣisurasevitaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.39"> guhābhir bhīmarūpābhiḥ siṃhonnāditakukṣibhiḥ|
                        vividhairdhātubhiścitraiḥ sarvatraivopaśobhitaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.40"> nadīṣu śaileṣu saraḥsu cāpi puṇyeṣv araṇyeṣu
                        tathā++āśrameṣu| sarvatra sarvāḥ parimārgitavyāḥ sarvatra bhūmirhi vasūni
                        dhatte||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne nivṛttasaṃtāpīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ nāma
                        triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||30||</l>
                </div>
                <div n="31" type="level2" subtype="adhyāya">
                    <head>ekatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ|</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.1"> athātaḥ snehopayaugikacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.3"> snehasāro 'yaṃ puruṣaḥ, prāṇāśca snehabhūyiṣṭāḥ
                        snehasādhyāś ca bhavanti| sneho hi
                        pānānuvāsanamastiṣkaśirovastyuttarabastinasyakarṇapūraṇagātrābhyaṅgabhojaneṣūpayojyaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.4"> tatra dviyoniś caturvikalpo 'bhihitaḥ snehaḥ snehaguṇāś ca|
                        tatra jaṅgamebhyo gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ pradhānaṃ, sthāvarebhyas tilatailaṃ
                        pradhānam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.5"> ata ūrdhvaṃ yathāprayojanaṃ yathāpradhānaṃ ca
                        sthāvarasnehānupadekṣyāmaḥ tatra
                        tilvakairaṇḍakośāmradantīdravantīsaptalāśaṅkhinīpalāśaviṣāṇikāgavākṣīkampillakaśampākanīlinīsnehā
                        virecayanti, jīmūtakakuṭajakṛtavedhanekṣvākudhāmārgavamadanasnehā vāmayanti,
                        viḍaṅgakharamañjarīmadhuśigrusūryavallīpīlusiddhārthakajyotiṣmatīsnehāḥ śiro
                        virecayanti, karañjapūtīkakṛtamālamātuluṅgeṅgudīkirātatiktakasnehā
                        duṣṭavraṇeṣūpayujyante, tuvarakakapitthakampillakabhallātakapaṭolasnehā
                        mahāvyādhiṣu, trapusair vārukakarkārukatumbīkūṣmāṇḍasnehā mūtrasaṅgeṣu,
                        kapotavaṅkāvalgujaharītakīsnehāḥ śarkarāśmarīṣu,
                        kusumbhasarṣapātasīpicumardātimuktakabhāṇḍīkaṭutumbīkaṭabhīsnehāḥ prameheṣu,
                        tālanārikelapanasamocapriyālabilvamadhūkaśleṣmātakāmrātakaphalasnehāḥ
                        pittasaṃsṛṣṭe vāyau, bibhītakabhallātakapiṇḍītakasnehāḥ kṛṣṇīkaraṇe,
                        śravaṇakaṅgukaṭuṇṭukasnehāḥ pāṇḍūkaraṇe, saralapītadāruśiṃśapāgurusārasnehā
                        dadrukuṣṭhakiṭimeṣu, sarva eva snehā vātam upaghnanti, tailaguṇāś ca
                        samāsena vyākhyātāḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.6"> ata ūrdhvaṃ kaṣāyasnehapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ| tatra
                        kecidāhuḥ tvakpatraphalamūlādīnāṃ bhāgastaccaturguṇaṃ jalaṃ
                        caturbhāgāvaśeṣaṃ niṣkvāthyāpaharedity eṣa kaṣāyapākakalpaḥ; snehaprasṛteṣu
                        ṣaṭsu caturguṇaṃ dravamāvapya caturaś cākṣasamān bheṣajapiṇḍānity eṣa
                        snehapākakalpaḥ| etat tu na samyak; kasmāt āgamāsiddhatvāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.7"> palakuḍavādīnāmato mānaṃ tu vyākhyāsyāmaḥ tatra dvādaśa
                        dhānyamāṣā madhyamāḥ suvarṇamāṣakaḥ, te ṣoḍaśa suvarṇam; athavā
                        madhyamaniṣpāvā ekonaviṃśatirdharaṇaṃ, tāvyardhatṛtīyāni karṣaḥ;
                        tataścordhvaṃ caturguṇamabhivardhayantaḥ palakuḍavaprasthāḍhakadroṇā ity
                        abhiniṣpadyante, tulā punaḥ palaśataṃ, tāḥ punarviṃśatirbhāraḥ; śuṣkāṇāmidaṃ
                        mānam, ārdradravāṇāṃ ca dviguṇamiti|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.8"> tatrānyatamaparimāṇasaṃmitānāṃ yathāyogaṃ
                        tvakpatraphalamūlādīnāmātapapariśoṣitānāṃ chedyāni khaṇḍaśaśchedayitvā
                        bhedyānyaṇuśo bhedayitvā+avakuṭyāṣṭaguṇena ṣoḍaśaguṇena
                        vā+ambhasā+abhiṣicyasthālyāṃ caturbhāgāvaśiṣṭaṃ kvāthayitvā+apaharedity eṣa
                        kaṣāyayākakalpaḥ| snehāccaturbhāgāvaśiṣṭaṃ kvāthayitvā+apaharedity eṣa
                        kaṣāyapākakalpaḥ| snehāccaturguṇo dravaḥ, snehacaturthaṃśo bheṣajakalkaḥ,
                        tadaikadhyaṃ saṃṛjya vipacedity eṣa snehapākakalpaḥ| athavā tatrodakadroṇe
                        tvakpatraphalamūlādīnāṃ tulāmāvāpya caturbhāgāvaśiṣṭaṃ niṣkvāthyāpaharedity
                        eṣa kaṣāyapākakalpaḥ; snehakuḍave bheṣajapalaṃ piṣṭaṃ kalkaṃ caturguṇaṃ
                        dravamāvāpya vipacedity eṣa snehapākakalpaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.9"> bhavataś cātra snehabheṣajatoyānāṃ pramāṇaṃ yatra
                        neritam| tatrāyaṃ vidhirāstheyo nirdiṣṭe tadvadeva tu|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.10"> anukte dravakārye tu sarvatra salilaṃ matam|
                        kalkakvāthāvanirdeśe gaṇāttasmāt prayojayet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.11"> ata ūrdhvaṃ snehapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ| sa tu
                        trividhaḥ; tad yathā mṛduḥ, madhyamaḥ, khara iti| tatra
                        snehauṣadhivivekamātraṃ yatra bheṣajaṃ sa mṛduriti, madhūcchiṣṭamiva
                        viśadamavilepi yatra bheṣajaṃ sa madhyamaḥ, kṛṣṇamavasannamīṣadviśadaṃ
                        cikkaṇaṃ ca yatra bheṣajaṃ sa khara iti; ata ūrdhvaṃ dagdhasneho bhavati,
                        taṃ punaḥ sādhu sādhayet| tatra pānābhyavahārayor mṛduḥ, nasyābhyaṅgayor
                        madhyamaḥ, bastikarṇapūraṇayostu khara iti|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.12"> bhavataś cātra śabdasyoparame prāpte phenasyopaśame
                        tathā| gandhavarṇarasādīnāṃ saṃpattau siddhimādiśet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.13"> ghṛtasyaivaṃ vipakvasya jānīyāt kuśalo bhiṣak| pheno
                        'timātraṃ tailasya śeṣaṃ ghṛtavadādiśet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.14"> ata ūrdhvaṃ snehapānakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ atha khalu
                        laghukoṣṭhāyāturāya kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanāyodayagiriśikharasaṃsthite
                        prataptakanakanikarapītalohite savitari yathābalaṃ tailasya ghṛtasya vā
                        mātrāṃ pātuṃ prayacchet| pītamātre coṣṇodakenopaspṛśya sopānatko yathāsukhaṃ
                        viharet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.15"> rūkṣakṣataviṣārtānāṃ vātapittavikāriṇām|
                        hīnamedhāsmṛtīnāṃ ca sarpiḥpānaṃ praśasyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.16"> kṛmikoṣṭhānilāviṣṭāḥ pravṛddhakaphamedasaḥ|
                        pibeyustailasātmyāś ca tailaṃ dārḍhyārthinaś ca ye|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.17"> vyāyāmakarśitāḥ śuṣkaretoraktā mahārujaḥ|
                        mahāgnimārutaprāṇā vasāyogyā narāḥ smṛtāḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.18"> krūrāśayāḥ kleśasahā vātārtā dīptavahnayaḥ|
                        majjānamāpnuyuḥ sarve sarpirvā svauṣadhānvitam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.19"> kevalaṃ paittike sarpirvātike lavaṇānvitam| deyaṃ
                        bahukaphe cāpi vyoṣakṣārasamāyutam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.20"> doṣāṇāmalpabhūyastvaṃ saṃsargaṃ samavekṣya ca|
                        yuñjyāttriṣaṣṭidhābhinnaiḥ samāsavyāsato rasaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.21"> snehasātmyaḥ kleśasahaḥ kāle nātyuṣṇaśītale| accham eva
                        pibet snehamacchapānaṃ hi pūjitam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.22"> śītakāle divā snehamuṣṇakāle pibenniśi| vātapittādhiko
                        rātrau vātaśleṣmādhiko divā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.23"> vātapittādhikasyoṣṇe tṛṇamūrcchonmādakārakaḥ| śīte
                        vātakaphārtasya gauravāruciśūlakṛt|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.24"> snehapītasya cettṛṣṇā pibeduṣṇodakaṃ naraḥ| evaṃ
                        cānupaśāmyantyāṃ snehamuṣṇāmbunā vamet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.25ab"> dihyācchītaiḥ śiraḥ śītaṃ toyaṃ cāpy avagāhayet| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.25cd"> yā mātrā parijīryeta caturbhāgagate+ahani|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.26"> sā mātrā dīpayatyagnimalpadoṣe ca pūjitā| yā mātrā
                        parijīryeta tathā+ardhadivase gate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.27"> sā vṛṣyā bṛṃhaṇī yā ca madhyadoṣe ca pūjitā| yā mātrā
                        parijīryeta caturbhāgāvaśeṣite|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.28"> snehanīyā ca sā mātrā bahudoṣe ca pūjitā| yā mātrā
                        parijīryet tu tathā pariṇate+ahani|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.29"> glānimūrcchāmadān hitvā sā mātrā pūjitā bhavet|
                        ahorātrādasaṃduṣṭā yā mātrā parijīryati|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.30"> sā tu kuṣṭhavoṣonmādagrahāpasmāranāśinī| yathāgni
                        prathamāṃ mātrāṃ pāyayeta vicakṣaṇaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.31"> pīto hy atibahuḥ sneho janayet prāṇasaṃśayam|
                        mithyācārādbahutvād vā yasya sneho na jīryati|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.32"> viṣṭabhya cāpi jīryettaṃ vāriṇoṣṇena vāmayet| tataḥ
                        snehaṃ punardadyāllaghukoṣṭhāya dehine| jīrṇājīrṇaviśaṅkāyāṃ
                        snehasyoṣṇodakaṃ pibet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.33ab"> tenodgāro bhavec chuddho bhaktaṃ rucistathā| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.33cd">syuḥ pacyamāne tṛḍdāhabhramasādāratiklamāḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.34"> pariṣicyādbhir uṣṇābhir jīrṇasnehaṃ tato naram| yavāgūṃ
                        pāyayeccoṣṇāṃ kāmaṃ klinnālpataṇḍulām|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.35"> deyau yūṣarasau vā+api sugandhī snehavarjitau| kṛtau
                        vā+atyalpasarpiṣkau vilepī vā vidhīyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.36"> pibettryahaṃ caturahaṃ pañcāhaṃ ṣaḍahaṃ tathā|
                        saptarātrāt paraṃ snehaḥ sātmyībhavati sevitaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.37"> sukumāraṃ kṛśaṃ vṛddhaṃ śiśuṃ snehadviṣaṃ tathā|
                        tṛṣṇārtamuṣṇakāle ca saha bhaktena pāyayet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.38"> pippalyo lavaṇaṃ snehāścatvāro dadhimastukaḥ|
                        pītamaikadhyametaddhi sadyaḥsnehanamucyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.39"> bhṛṣṭā māṃsarase snigdhā yavāgūḥ sūpakalpitā| prakṣudrā
                        pīyamānā tu sadyaḥsnehanamucyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.40"> sarpiṣmatī payaḥsiddhā yavāgūḥ svalpataṇḍulā| sasvoṣṇā
                        sevyamānā tu sadyaḥsnehanamucyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.41"> pippalyo lavaṇaṃ sarpistilapiṣṭaṃ varāhajā| vasā ca
                        pītamaikadhyaṃ sadyaḥsnehanamucyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.42"> śarkarācūrṇasaṃsṛṣṭe dohanasthe ghṛte tu gām| dugdhvā
                        kṣīraṃ pibedrūkṣaḥ sadyaḥsnehanamucyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.43"> yavakolakulatthānāṃ kvātho māgadhikānvitaḥ| payo dadhi
                        surā ceti ghṛtamapyaṣṭamaṃ bhavet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.44"> siddhametairghṛtaṃ pītaṃ sadyaḥsnehanam uttamam| rājñe
                        rājasamebhyo vā deyametadghṛtottamam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.45"> balahīneṣu vṛddheṣu mṛdvagnistrīhatātmasu| alpadoṣeṣu
                        yojyāḥ syurye yogāḥ samyagīritāḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.46"> vivarjayet snehapānamajīrṇī taruṇajvarī| durbalo 'rocakī
                        sthūlo mūrcchārto madapīḍitaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.47"> chardyarditaḥ pipāsārtaḥ śrāntaḥ pānaklamānvitaḥ|
                        dattabastir viriktaś ca vānto yaś cāpi mānavaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.48ab"> akāle durdine caiva na ca snehaṃ piben naraḥ|</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.48cd"> akāle ca prasūtā strī snehapānaṃ vivarjayet|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.49"> snehapānād bhavanty eṣāṃ nṝṇāṃ nānāvidhā gadāḥ| gadā vā
                        kṛcchratāṃ yānti na sidhyanty athavā punaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.50"> garbhāśaye+avaśeṣāḥ syū raktakledamalās tataḥ| snehaṃ
                        jahyān niṣeveta pācanaṃ rūkṣam eva ca|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.51ab"> daśarātrāt tataḥ snehaṃ yathāvad avacārayet| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.51cd">purīṣaṃ grathitaṃ rūkṣaṃ kṛcchrād annaṃ vipacyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.52ab"> uro vidahate vāyuḥ koṣṭhādupari dhāvati| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.52cd">durvarṇo durbalaś caiva rūkṣo bhavati mānavaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.53"> susnigdhā tvagviṭśaithilyaṃ dīpto 'gnirmṛdugātratā|
                        glānirlāghavamaṅgānāmadhastāt snehadarśanam| samyaksnigdhasya liṅgāni
                        snehodvegas tathaiva ca|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.54"> bhaktadveṣo mukhasrāvo gudadāhaḥ pravāhikā|
                        purīṣātipravṛttiś ca bhṛśasnigdhasya lakṣaṇam|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.55"> rūkṣasya snehanaṃ snehairatisnigdhasya rūkṣaṇam|
                        śyāmākakoradūṣānnatakrapiṇyākaśaktubhiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.56"> dīptāntaragniḥ pariśuddhakoṣṭhaḥ
                        pratyagradhāturbalavarṇayuktaḥ| dṛḍhendriyo mandajaraḥ śatāyuḥ snehopasevī
                        puruṣo bhavettu|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.57"> sneho hito durbalahnidehasandhukṣaṇe vyādhinipīḍitasya|
                        balānvitau bhojanadoṣajātaiḥ pramardituṃ tau sahasā na sādhyau||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne snehopayaugikacikitsitaṃ
                        nāmaikatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||31||</l>
                </div>

                <div n="32" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>dvātriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.1"> athātaḥ svedāvacāraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.3"> caturvidhaḥ svedaḥ tad yathā tāpasveda, ūṣmasveda,
                        upanāhasvedo, dravasveda iti atra sarvasvedavikalpāvarodhaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.4"> tatra tāpasvedaḥ pāṇikāṃsyakandukakapālavālukāvastraiḥ
                        prayujyate, śayānasya cāṅgatāpo bahuśaḥ khādirāṅgārair iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.5"> ūṣmasvedastu kapālapāṣāśeṣṭakālohapiṇḍānagnivarṇānadbhir
                        āsiñcedamladravyair vā, tairārdrālaktakapariveṣṭitair aṅgapradeśaṃ svedayet
                        | māṃsarasapayodadhisnehadhānyāmlavātaharapatrabhaṅgakvāthapūrṇāṃ vā
                        kumbhīmanutaptāṃ prāvṛtyoṣmāṇaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | pārśvacchidreṇa vā
                        kumbhenādhomukhena tasyā mukham abhis andhāya tasmiñchidrehastiśuṇḍākārāṃ
                        nāḍīṃ praṇidhāya taṃ svedayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.6"> sukhopaviṣṭaṃ svabhyaktaṃ guruprāvaraṇāvṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         hastiśuṇḍikayā nāḍyā svedayed vātarogiṇam | sukhā sarvāṅgagā hyeṣā na ca
                        kliśnāti mānavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.7"> vyāmārdhamātrā trirvakrā hastihastasamākṛtiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedanārthe hitā nāḍī kailiñjī hastiśuṇḍikā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.8ab"> puruṣāyāmamātrāṃ ca bhūmimutkīrya khādiraiḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.8cd">kāṣṭhair dagdhvā tathā 'bhyukṣya kṣīradhānyāmlavāribhiḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.9"> patrabhaṅgair avacchādya śayānaṃ svedayet tataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvavat svedayed dagdhvā bhasmāpohyāpi vā śilām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.10"> pūrvavat kuṭīṃ vā caturdvārāṃ kṛtvā tasyām
                        upaviṣṭasyāntaś caturdvāre 'ṅgārānupasandhāya taṃ svedayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.11"> kośadhānyāni vā samyagupasvedyāstīrya kiliñje 'nyasmin
                        vā tatpratirūpake śayānaṃ prāvṛtya svedayet; evaṃ
                        pāṃśugośakṛttuṣabusapalāloṣm abhiḥ svedayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.12"> upanāhasvedas tu vātaharamūlakalkair amlapiṣṭair
                        lavaṇapragāḍhaiḥ susnigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇaiḥ pradihya svedayet | evaṃ
                        kākolyādibhir elādibhiḥ surasādibhis tilātasīsarṣapakalkaiḥ
                        kṛśarāpāyasotkārikābhir veśavāraiḥ sālvaṇair vā tanuvastrāvanaddhaiḥ
                        svedayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.13"> dravasvedas tu vātaharadravyakvāthapūrṇe koṣṇakaṭāhe
                        droṇyāṃ vā 'vagāhya svedayet, evaṃ
                        payomāṃsarasayūṣatailadhānyāmlaghṛtavasāmūtreṣv avagāheta; etair eva
                        sukhoṣṇaiḥ kaṣāyaiś ca pariṣiñcediti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.14"> tatra tāpoṣmasvedau viśeṣataḥ śleṣmaghnau, upanāhasvedo
                        vātaghnaḥ, anyatarasmin pittasaṃsṛṣṭe dravasveda iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.15"> kaphamedonvite vāyau
                        nivātātapaguruprāvaraṇaniyuddhādhvavyāyāmabhāraharaṇāmarṣaiḥ svedamutpādayed
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.16"> bhavanti cātra caturvidho yo 'bhihito dvidhā svedaḥ
                        prayujyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvasminn eva dehe tu dehasyāvayave tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.17"> yeṣāṃ nasyaṃ vidhātavyaṃ bastiś caiva hi dehinām |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanīyāś ca ye kecit pūrvaṃ svedyās tu te matāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.18"> paś cāt svedyā hṛte śalye mūḍhagarbhā 'nupadravā |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyak prajātā kāle yā paś cāt svedyā vijānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.19"> svedyaḥ pūrvaṃ ca paś cācca bhagandaryarśasas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmaryā cāturo jantuḥ śeṣāñchāstre pracakṣmahe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.20"> nānabhyakte nāpi cāsnigdhadehe svedo yojyaḥ svedavidbhiḥ
                        kathañcit |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭaṃ loke kāṣṭhamasnigdhamāśu gacchedbhaṅgaṃ svedayogair gṛhītam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.21"> snehaklinnā dhātusaṃsthāś ca doṣāḥ svasthānasthā ye ca
                        mārgeṣu līnāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyak svedair yojitais te dravatvaṃ prāptāḥ koṣṭhaṃ śodhanair yāntyaśeṣam
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.22"> agnerdīptiṃ mārdavaṃ tvakprasādaṃ bhaktaśraddhāṃ
                        srotasāṃ nirmalatvam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryāt svedo hanti nidrāṃ satandrāṃ sandhīn stabdhāṃśceṣṭayed āśu yuktaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.23"> svedāsrāvo vyādhihānirlaghutvaṃ śītārthitvaṃ mārdavaṃ
                        cāturasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyaksvinne lakṣaṇaṃ prāhuretanmithyāsvinne vyatyayenaitad eva || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.24"> svinne 'tyarthaṃ sandhipīḍā vidāhaḥ sphoṭotpattiḥ
                        pittaraktaprakopaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchā bhrāntirdāhatṛṣṇe klamaś ca kuryāt tūrṇaṃ tatra śītaṃ vidhānam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.25"> pāṇḍurmehī pittaraktī kṣayārtaḥ kṣāmo 'jīrṇī codarārto
                        viṣārtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛḍcchardyārto garbhiṇī pītamadyo naite svedyā yaś ca martyoatisārī |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedādeṣāṃ yānti dehā vināśaṃ nosādhyatvaṃ yānti caiṣāṃ vikārāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         svedaiḥ sādhyo durbalo 'jīrṇabhaktaḥ syātāṃ ceddvau svedanīyau tatastau
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.26">
                        <caesura/>
                         eteṣāṃ svedasādhyā ye vyādhayas teṣu buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdūn svedān prayuñjīta tathā hṛnmuṣkadṛṣṭiṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.27"> sarvān svedānnivāte ca jīrṇānnasyāvacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehābhyaktaśarīrasya śītairācchādya cakṣuṣī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.28"> svidyamānasya ca muhurhṛdayaṃ śītalaiḥ spṛśet |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyaksvinnaṃ vimṛditaṃ snātamuṣṇāmbubhiḥ śanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.29ab"> svabhyaktaṃ prāvṛtāṅgaṃ ca nivātaśaraṇasthitam | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.29cd">bhojayed anabhiṣyandi sarvaṃ cācāram ādiśet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne svedāvacāraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ
                        nāma dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||32 ||</l>
                </div>
                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>trayastriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.1"> athāto vamanavirecanasādhyopadravacikitsitaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.3"> doṣāḥ kṣīṇā bṛṃhayitavyāḥ, kupitāḥ praśamayitavyāḥ,
                        vṛddhā nirhartavyāḥ, samāḥ paripālyā iti siddhāntaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.4"> prādhānyena vamanavirecane vartate nirharaṇe doṣāṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt tayor vidhānam ucyamānam upadhāraya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.5"> athāturaṃ snigdhaṃ svinnam abhiṣyandibhir āhārair
                        anavabaddhadoṣamavalokya śvo vamanaṃ pāyayitā 'smīti saṃbhojayet tīkṣṇāgniṃ
                        balavantaṃ bahudoṣaṃ mahāvyādhiparītaṃ vamanasātmyaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.6"> bhavati cātra peśalair vividhair annair doṣānutkleśya
                        dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhasvinnāya vamanaṃ dattaṃ samyak pravartate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.7"> athāparedyuḥ pūrvāhṇe sādhāraṇe kāle
                        vamanadravyakaṣāyakalkacūrṇasnehānām anyatamasya mātrāṃ pāyayitvā vāmayed
                        yathāyogaṃ koṣṭhaviśeṣamavekṣya; asātmyabībhatsadurgandhadurdarśanāni ca
                        vamanāni vidadhyāt, ato viparītāni virecanāni; tatra sukumāraṃ kṛśaṃ bālaṃ
                        vṛddhaṃ bhīruṃ vā vamanasādhyeṣu vikāreṣu
                        kṣīradadhitakrayavāgūnāmanyatamamākaṇṭhaṃ pāyayet, pītauṣadhaṃ ca pāṇibhir
                        agnitaptaiḥ pratāpyamānaṃ muhūrtamupekṣeta; tasya ca svedaprādurbhāveṇa
                        śithilatāmāpannaṃ svebhyaḥ sthānebhyaḥ pracalitaṃ kukṣimanusṛtaṃ jānīyāt,
                        tataḥ pravṛttahṛllāsaṃ jñātvā jānumātrāsanopaviṣṭamāptair lalāṭe pṛṣṭhe
                        pārśvayoḥ kaṇṭhe ca pāṇibhiḥ suparigṛhītamaṅgulīgandharvahastotpalanālānām
                        anyatamena kaṇṭham abhis pṛśantaṃ vāmayet tāvad yāvat samyagvāntaliṅgānīti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.8"> bhavataś cātra kaphaprasekaṃ hṛdyāviśuddhiṃ kaṇḍūṃ ca
                        duścharditaliṅgam āhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittātiyogaṃ ca cisaṃjñatāṃ ca hṛtkaṇṭhapīḍām api cātivānte || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.9"> pitte kaphasyānu sukhaṃ pravṛtte śuddheṣu
                        hṛtkaṇṭhaśiraḥsu cāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghau ca dehe kaphasaṃsrave ca sthite suvāntaṃ puruṣaṃ vyavasyet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.10"> samyagvāntaṃ cainam abhis amīkṣya
                        snehanavirecanaśamanānāṃ dhūmānām anyatamaṃ sāmarthyataḥ pāyayitvā
                        ''ācārikam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.11"> bhavanti cātra tato 'parāhṇe śuciśuddhadehamuṣṇābhir
                        addbhiḥ pariṣiktagātram |
                        <caesura/>
                         kulatthamudgāḍhakijāṅgalānāṃ yūṣai rasair vā 'pyupabhojayet tu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.12">
                        kāsopalepasvarabhedanidrātandrāsyadaurgandhyaviṣopasargāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphaprasekagrahaṇīpradoṣā na santi jantorvamataḥ kadācit || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.13"> chinne tarau puṣpaphalaprarohā yathā vināśaṃ sahasā
                        vrajanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā hṛte śleṣmaṇi śodhanena tajjā vikārāḥ praśamaṃ prayānti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.14"> na vāmayet taimirikordhvavātagulmodaraplīhakṛmiśramārtān
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthūlakṣatakṣīṇakṛśātivṛddhamūtrāturān kevalavātarogān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.15">
                        svaropaghātādhyayanaprasaktaduśchardiduḥkoṣṭhatṛḍārtabālām |
                        <caesura/>
                         ūrdhvāsrapittikṣudhitātirūkṣagarbhiṇyudāvartirūhitāṃś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.16"> avamyavamanādrogāḥ kṛcchratāṃ yānti dehinām |
                        <caesura/>
                         asādhyatāṃ vā gacchanti naite vāmyāstataḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.17"> ete 'pyajīrṇavyathitā vāmyā ye ca viṣāturāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atīva colbaṇakaphāste ca syur madhukāmbunā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.18"> vāmyāstu
                        viṣaśoṣastanyadoṣamandāgnyunmādāpasmāraślīpadārbudavidārikāmedomehagarajvarārucyapacyāmātīsārahṛdrogacittavibhramavisarpavidradhyajīrṇamukhaprasekahṛllāsaśvāsakāsapīnasapūtīnāsakaṇṭhauṣṭhavaktrapākakarṇasrāvādhijihvopajihvikāgalaśuṇḍikādhaḥśoṇitapittinaḥ
                        kaphasthānajeṣu vikāreṣv anye ca kaphavyādhiparītā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.19"> virecanam api snigdhasvinnāya vāntāya ca deyam;
                        avāntasya hi samyagviriktasyāpi sato 'dhaḥ srastaḥ śleṣmā grahaṇīṃ
                        chādayati, gauravam āpādayati, pravāhikāṃ vā janayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.20"> athāturaṃ śvo virecanaṃ pāyayitā 'smīti pūrvāhṇe laghu
                        bhojayet , phalāmlamuṣṇodakaṃ cainamanupāyayet | athāpare 'hani
                        vigataśleṣmadhātumāturopakramaṇīyādavekṣyāturamathāsmai auṣadhamātrāṃ pātuṃ
                        prayacchet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.21"> tatra mṛduḥ, krūro, madhyama iti trividhaḥ koṣṭho
                        bhavati | tatra bahupitto mṛduḥ, sa dugdhenāpi viricyate; bahuvātaśleṣmā
                        krūraḥ, sa durvirecyaḥ; samadoṣo madhyamaḥ, sa sādhāraṇa iti | tatra mṛdau
                        mātrā mṛdvī, tīkṣṇā krūre, madhye madhyā kartavyeti | pītauṣadhaś ca
                        tanmanāḥ śayyābhyāśe virecyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.22"> virecanaṃ pītavāṃs tu na vegān dhārayed budhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivātaśāyī śītāmbu na spṛśenna pravāhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.23"> yathā ca vamane prasekauṣadhakaphapittānilāḥ krameṇa
                        gacchanti, evaṃ virecane mūtrapurīṣapittauṣadhakaphā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.24"> bhavanti cātra hṛtkukṣyaśuddhiḥ
                        paridāhakaṇḍūviṇmūtrasaṅgāś ca na sadvirikte |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchāgudabhraṃśakaphātiyogāḥ śūlodgamaś cātiviriktaliṅgam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.25"> gateṣu doṣeṣu kaphānviteṣu nābhyā laghutve manasaś ca
                        tuṣṭau |
                        <caesura/>
                         gate 'nile cāpy anulomabhāvaṃ samyagviriktaṃ manujaṃ vyavasyet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.26"> mandāgnimakṣīṇamasadviriktaṃ na pāyayetāhani tatra peyām
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇaṃ tṛṣārtaṃ suvirecitaṃ ca tanvīṃ sukhoṣṇāṃ laghu pāyayec ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.27"> buddheḥ prasādaṃ balamindiryāṇāṃ dhātusthiratvaṃ
                        balamagnidīptim |
                        <caesura/>
                         cirāc ca pākaṃ vayasaḥ karoti virecanaṃ samyagupāsyamānam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.28"> yathaudakānāmudake 'panīte carasthirāṇāṃ bhavati
                        praṇāśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte hṛte tvevam upadravāṇāṃ pittātmakānāṃ bhavati praṇāśaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.29"> mandāgnyatisnehitabālavṛddhasthūlāḥ
                        kṣatakṣīṇabhayopataptāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śrāntastṛṣārto 'parijīrṇabhakto garbhiṇyadho gacchati yasya cāsṛk || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.30"> navapraviśyāyamadātyayī ca navajravī yā ca navaprasūtā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śalyārditāś cāpy avirecanīyāḥ snehādibhir ye tvanupaskṛtāś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.31"> virecanair yānti narā vināśamajñaprayuktair avirecanīyāḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.32"> virecyās tu jvaragarārucyarśo
                        'rbudodaragranthividradhipāṇḍurogāpasmārahṛdrogavātaraktabhagandaracchardiyonirogavisarpagulmapakvāśayarugvibandhavisūcikālasakamūtrāghātakuṣṭhavisphoṭakapramehānāhaplīhaśophavṛddhiśastrakṣatakṣārāgnidagdhaduṣṭavraṇākṣipākakācatimirābhiṣyandaśiraḥkarṇākṣināsāsyagudameḍhradāhordhvaraktapittakṛmikoṣṭhinaḥ
                        pittasthānajeṣv anyeṣu ca vikāreṣv anye ca paittikavyādhiparītā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.33"> saratvasaukṣmyataikṣṇyauṣṇyavikāśitvair virecanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vamanaṃ tu hareddoṣaṃ prakṛtyā gatamanyathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.34"> yātyadho doṣamādāya pacyamānaṃ virecanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇotkarṣāhvrajatyūrdhvamapakvaṃ vamanaṃ punaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.35"> mṛdukoṣṭhasya dīptāgneratitīkṣṇaṃ virecanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         na samyaṅnirhareddoṣānativegapradhāvitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.36"> pītaṃ yadauṣadhaṃ prātar bhuktapākasame kṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         paktiṃ gacchati doṣāṃś ca nirharettat praśasyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.37"> durbalasya calān doṣānalpānalpān punaḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         haret prabhūtānakpāṃs tu śamayet pracyutānapi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.38"> hareddoṣāṃś calān pakvān balino durbalasya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         calā hy upekṣitā doṣāḥ kleśayeyuściraṃ naram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.39"> mandāgniṃ krūrakoṣṭhaṃ ca sakṣāralavaṇair ghṛtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sandhukṣitāgniṃ snigdhaṃ ca svinnaṃ caiva virecayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.40"> snigdhasvinnasya bhaiṣajyair doṣastūtkleśito balāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         nilīyate na mārgeṣu snigdhe bhāṇḍa ivodakam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.41"> na cātisnehapītas tu pibet snehavirecanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ pracalitāḥ sthānādbhūyaḥ śliṣyanti vartmasu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.42"> viṣābhighātapiḍakāśophapāṇḍuvisarpiṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nātisnigdhā viśodhyāḥ syus tathā kuṣṭhipramehiṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.43"> virūkṣya snehasātmyaṃ tu bhūyaḥ saṃsnehya śodhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tena doṣā hṛtās tasya bhavanti balavardhanāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.44"> prāgapītaṃ naraṃ śodhyaṃ pāyayetauṣadhaṃ mṛdu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato vijñātakoṣṭhasya kāryaṃ saṃśodhanaṃ punaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.45"> sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaphalaṃ hṛdyamalpamātraṃ mahāguṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāpatsvalpātyayaṃ cāpi pibennṛpatirauṣadham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.46"> snehasvedāvanabhyasya yas tu saṃśodhanaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāru śuṣkamivānāme dehas tasya viśīryate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.47"> snehasvedapracalitā rasaiḥ snigdhair udīritāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ koṣṭhagatā jantoḥ sukhā hartuṃ viśodhanaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
                        vamanavirecanasādhyopadravacikitsitaṃ nāma trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||33 ||</l>
                </div>


                <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>catustriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.1"> athāto vamanavirecanavyāpaccikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.3"> vaidyāturanimittaṃ vamanaṃ virecanaṃ ca pañcadaśadhā
                        vyāpadyate | tatra vamanasyādho gatirūrdhvaṃ virecanasyeti pṛthak;
                        sāmānyamubhayoḥ sāvaśeṣaudhatvaṃ, jīrṇauṣadhatvaṃ, hīnadoṣāpahṛtatvaṃ,
                        vātaśūlam, ayogo, atiyogo, jīvādānam, ādhmānaṃ, parikartikā, parisrāvaḥ,
                        pravāhikā, hṛdayopasaraṇaṃ, vibandha, aṅgapragraha iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.4"> tatra bubhukṣāpīḍitasyātitīkṣṇāgnermṛdukoṣṭhasya
                        cāvatiṣṭhamānaṃ durvamasya vā guṇasāmānyabhāvādvamanamadho gacchati,
                        tatrepsitānavāptirdoṣotkleśaś ca; tamāśu snehayitvā bhūyastīkṣṇatarair
                        vāmayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.5"> apariśuddhāmāśayasyotkliṣṭaśleṣmaṇaḥ saśeṣānnasya vā
                        'hṛdyamatiprabhūtaṃ vā virecanaṃ pītamūrdhvaṃ gacchati,
                        tatrepsitānavāptirdoṣokleśaś ca; tatrāśuddhāmāśayamulbaṇaśleṣmāṇamāśu
                        vāmayitvā bhūyastīkṣṇatarair virecayet, āmānvaye tvāmavat saṃvidhānam,
                        ahṛdye 'tiprabhūte ca hṛdyaṃ pramāṇayuktaṃ ca; ata ūrdhvamuttiṣṭhatyauṣadhe
                        na tṛtīyaṃ pāyayet, tatastvenaṃ madhughṛtaphāṇitayuktair lehair virecayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.6">
                        doṣavigrathitamalpamauṣadhamavasthitamūrdhvabhāgikamadhobhāgikaṃ vā na
                        sraṃsayati doṣān, tatra tṛṣṇā pārśvaśūlaṃ chardirmūrcchā parvabhedo hṛllāso
                        'ratirudgārāviśuddhiś ca bhavati; tamuṣṇābhir adbhir āśu vāmayed
                        ūrdhvabhāgike, adhobhāgike 'pi ca
                        sāvaśeṣauṣadhamatipradhāvitadoṣamatibalamasamyagviriktalakṣaṇamapyevaṃ
                        vāmayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.7"> krūrakoṣṭhasyātitīkṣṇāgneralpamauṣadhamalpaguṇaṃ vā
                        bhaktavat pākam upaiti, tatra samudīrṇā doṣā yathākālamanirhrīyamāṇā
                        vyādhivibhramaṃ balavibhraṃśaṃ cāpādayanti, tamanalpamamandamauṣadhaṃ ca
                        pāyayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.8"> asnigdhasvinnenālpaguṇaṃ vā bheṣajam upayuktamalpān doṣān
                        hanti; tatra vamane doṣaśeṣo gauravamutkleśaṃ hṛdayāviśuddhiṃ vyādhivṛddhiṃ
                        ca karoti, tatra taṃ yathāyogaṃ pāyayitvā vāmayed dṛḍhataraṃ; virecane tu
                        gudaparikartanamādhmānaṃ śirogauravamaniḥsaraṇaṃ vā vāyor vyādhivṛddhiṃ ca
                        karoti; tam upapādya bhūyaḥ snehasvedābhyāṃ virecayed dṛḍhataraṃ, dṛḍhaṃ
                        bahupracalitadoṣaṃ vā tṛtīye divase 'lpaguṇaṃ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.9"> asnigdhasvinnena rūkṣauṣadham upayuktamabrahmacāriṇā vā
                        vāyuṃ kopayati, tatra vāyuḥ prakupitaḥ pārśvapṛṣṭhaśroṇimanyāmarmaśūlaṃ
                        mūrcchāṃ bhramaṃ madaṃ saṃjñānāśaṃ ca karoti, taṃ vātaśūlamity ācakṣate;
                        tamabhyajya dhāvyasvedena svedayitvā yaṣṭīmadhukavipakvena tailenānuvāsayet
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.10"> snehasvedābhyām avibhāvitaśarīreṇālpamauṣadhamalpaguṇaṃ
                        vā pītamūrdhvamadho vā nābhyeti doṣāṃścotkleśya taiḥ saha balakṣayam
                        āpādayati, tatrādhmānaṃ hṛdayagrahastṛṣṇā mūrcchā dāhaś ca bhavati, tam
                        ayogamity ācakṣate; tamāśu vāmayenmadanaphalalavaṇāmbubhir virecayet
                        tīkṣṇataraiḥ kaṣāyaiś ca | durvāntasya tu samutkliṣṭādoṣā vyāpya śarīraṃ
                        kaṇḍūśvayathukuṣṭhapiḍakājvarāṅgamardanistodanāni kurvanti,
                        tatastānaśeṣānmadauṣadhenāpaharet | asnigdhasvinnasya durviriktasyādhonābheḥ
                        stabdhapūrṇodaratā śūlaṃ vātapurīṣasaṅgaḥ kaṇḍūmaṇḍalaprādurbhāvo vā
                        bhavati, tamāsthāpya punaḥ saṃsrehya virecayet tīkṣṇena | nātipravartamāne
                        tiṣṭhati vā duṣṭasaṃśodhane tatsantejanārthamuṣṇodakaṃ pāyayet, pāṇitāpaiś
                        ca pārśvodaram upasvedayet, tataḥ pravartante doṣāḥ | anupravṛtte cālpadoṣe
                        jīrṇauṣadhaṃ bahudoṣamahaḥśeṣaṃ daśarātrādūrdhvam upasaṃskṛtadehaṃ
                        snehasvedābhyāṃ bhūyaḥ śodhayet | durvirecyamāsthāpya punaḥ saṃsnehya
                        virecayet | hrībhayalobhair vegāghātaśīlāḥ prāyaśaḥ striyo rājasamīpasthā
                        vaṇijaḥ śrotriyāś ca bhavanti, tasmād ete durvirecyāḥ, bahuvātatvāt ; ata
                        eva tānatisnigdhān svedopapannāñ śodhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.11"> sngidhasvinnasyātimātramatimṛdukoṣṭhasya vā
                        'titīkṣṇamadhikaṃ vā dattamauṣadhamatiyogaṃ kuryāt | tatra vamanātiyoge
                        pittātipravṛttirbalavisraṃso vātakopaś ca balavān bhavati, taṃ
                        ghṛtenābhyajyāvagāhya śītāsvapsu śarkarāmadhumiśrair lehair
                        upacaredyathāsvaṃ; virecanātiyoge kaphasyātipravṛttiruttarakālaṃ ca
                        saraktasya, tatrāpi balavisraṃso vātakopaś ca balavān bhavati,
                        tamatiśītāmbubhiḥ pariṣicyāvagāhya vā śītais taṇḍulāmbubhir
                        madhumiśraiśchardayet, picchābastiṃ cāsmai dadyāt, kṣīrasarpiṣā
                        cainamanuvāsayet, priyaṅgvādiṃ cāsmai taṇḍulāmbunā pātuṃ prayacchet,
                        kṣīrarasayoś cānyatareṇa bhojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.12"> tasiminn eva vamanātiyoge pravṛddhe śoṇitaṃ ṣṭhīvati
                        chardayati vā, tatra jihvāniḥsaraṇamapasaraṇamakṣṇorvyāvṛttirhanusaṃhananaṃ
                        tṛṣṇā hikkā jvaro vaisaṃjñyamity aupadravā bhavanti;
                        tamajāsṛkcandanośīrāñjanalājacūrṇaiḥ saśarkarodakair manthaṃ pāyayet,
                        phalarasair vā saghṛtakṣaudraśarkaraiḥ śuṅgābhir vā vaṭādīnāṃ peyāṃ siddhāṃ
                        sakṣaudrāṃ varcogrāhibhir vā, payasā jāṅgalarasena vā bhojayet ,
                        atisrutaśoṇitavidhānenopacaret; jihvāmatisarpitāṃ
                        kaṭukalavaṇacūrṇapraghṛṣṭāṃ tiladrākṣāpraliptāṃ vā 'ntaḥ pīḍayet, antaḥ
                        praviṣṭāyāmamlamanye tasya purastāt khādayeyuḥ; vyāvṛtte cākṣiṇī
                        ghṛtābhyakte pīḍayet, tṛṣṇādiṣu ca yathāsvaṃ pratikurvīta, visaṃjñe
                        veṇuvīṇāgītasvanaṃ śrāvayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.13"> virecanātiyoge ca sacandrakaṃ salilamadhaḥ sravati tato
                        māṃsadhāvanaprakāśamuttarakālaṃ jīvaśoṇitaṃ ca, tato gudaniḥsaraṇaṃ
                        vepathurvamanātiyogopadravāś cāsya bhavanti; tam api
                        niḥsrutaśoṇitavidhānenopacaret, niḥsarpitagudasya gudamabhyajya
                        parisvedyāntaḥ pīḍayet kṣudrarogacikitsitaṃ vā vīkṣeta, vepathau
                        vātavyādhividhānaṃ kurvīta, jihvāniḥsaraṇādiṣūktaḥ pratīkāraḥ, atipravṛtte
                        vā jīvaśoṇite kāśmarīphalabadarīdūrvośīraiḥ śṛtena payasā
                        ghṛtamaṇḍāñjanayuktena suśītenāsthāpayet,
                        nyagrodhādikaṣāyekṣurasaghṛtaśoṇitasaṃsṛṣṭaiś cainaṃ bastibhir upācaret,
                        śoṇitaṣṭhīvane raktapittaraktātīsārakriyāś cāsya vidhadhyāt, nyagrodhādiṃ
                        cāsya vidadhyāt pānabhojaneṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.14"> jīvaśoṇitaraktapittayoś ca jijñāsārthaṃ tasmin picuṃ
                        plotaṃ vā kṣipet, yadyuṣṇodakaprakṣālitam api vastraṃ rañjayati
                        tajjīvaśoṇitamavagantavyaṃ; sabhaktaṃ ca śune dadyācchaktusaṃmiśraṃ vā, sa
                        yadyupabhuñjīta tajjīvaśoṇitamavagantavyam; anyathā raktapittam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.15"> saśeṣānnena bahudoṣeṇa
                        rūkṣeṇānilaprāyakoṣṭhenānuṣṇamasnigdhaṃ vā pītamauṣadhamādhmāpayati,
                        tatrānilamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaḥ samunnaddhodaratā pārśvabhaṅgo
                        gudabastinistodanaṃ bhaktāruciś ca bhavati, taṃ cādhmānamity ācakṣate; tam
                        upasvedyānāhavartidīpanabastikriyābhir upacaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.16"> kṣāmeṇātimṛdukoṣṭhena mandāgninā rūkṣeṇa vā
                        'titīkṣṇoṣṇātilavaṇamatirūkṣaṃ vā pītamauṣadhaṃ pittānilau pradūṣya
                        parikartikām āpādayati, tatra gudanābhimeḍhrebastiśiraḥsu sadāhaṃ
                        parikartanam anilasaṅgo vāyuviṣṭambho bhaktāruciś ca bhavati; tatra
                        picchābastir yaṣṭīmadhukakṛṣṇatilakalkamadhughṛtayuktaḥ, śītāmbupariṣiktaṃ
                        cainaṃ payasā bhuktavantaṃ ghṛtamaṇḍena yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tailena vā
                        'nuvāsayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.17"> krūrakoṣṭhasyātiprabhūtadopasya mṛdvauṣadhamavacāritaṃ
                        samutkliśya doṣānna niḥśeṣānapaharati, tataste doṣāḥ parisrāvam āpādayanti,
                        tatra daurbalyodaraviṣṭambhārucigātrasadanāni bhavanti, savedanau cāsya
                        pittaśleṣmāṇau parisravataḥ, taṃ parisrāvamity ācakṣate;
                        tamajakarṇadhavatiniśapalāśabalākaṣāyair madhusaṃyuktair āsthāpayet,
                        upaśāntadoṣaṃ snigdhaṃ ca bhūyaḥ saṃśodhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.18"> atirūkṣe 'tisnigdhe vā bheṣajamavacāritamaprāptaṃ
                        vātavarca udīrayati vegāghātena vā, tadā pravāhikā bhavati; tatra savātaṃ
                        sadāhaṃ saśūlaṃ guru picchilaṃ śvetaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ saraktaṃ vā bhṛśaṃ pravāhamāṇaḥ
                        kapham upaviśati; tāṃ parisrāvavidhānenopacaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.19"> yastūrdhvamadho vā bheṣajavegaṃ pravṛttamajñatvād
                        vinihanti tasyopasaraṇaṃ hṛdi kurvanti doṣāḥ, tatra
                        pradhānamarmasantāpādvedanābhir atyarthaṃ pīḍyamāno dantān kiṭakiṭāyate
                        udgatākṣo jihvāṃ svādati pratāmyatyacetāś ca bhavati, taṃ parivarjayanti
                        mūrkhāḥ; tamabhyajya dhānyasvedena svedayet, yaṣṭimadhukasiddhena ca
                        tailenānuvāsayet, śirovirecanaṃ cāsmai tīkṣṇaṃ vidadhyāt, tato
                        yaṣṭimadhukamiśreṇa taṇḍulāmbunā chardayet, yathādoṣocchrāyeṇa cainaṃ
                        bastibhir upācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.20"> yas tūrdhvam adho vā pravṛttadoṣaḥ śītāgāram udakam
                        anilam anyad vā seveta, tasya doṣāḥ srotaḥsv avalīyamānā ghānībhāvam āpannā
                        vātamūtraśakṛdgraham āpādya vibadhyante, tasyāṭopo dāho jvaro vedanāś ca
                        tīvrā bhavanti; tam āśu vāmayitvā prāptakālāṃ kriyāṃ kurvīta; adhobhāge tv
                        adhobhāgadoṣaharadravyaṃ saindhavāmlamūtrasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ virecanāya pāyayet,
                        āsthāpanam anuvāsanaṃ ca yathādoṣaṃ vidadhyāt, yathādoṣam āhārakramaṃ ca;
                        ubhayato bhāge tūpadravaviśeṣān yathāsvaṃ pratikurvīta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.21"> yā tu virecane gudaparikartikā tad vamane
                        kaṇṭhakṣaṇanaṃ, yad adhaḥ parisravaṇaṃ sa ūrdhvabhāge śleṣmaprasekaḥ, yā tv
                        adhāḥ pravāhikā sā tūrdhvaṃ śuṣkodgārā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.22"> bhavati cātra
                        <caesura/>
                         yās tv etā vyāpadaḥ proktā daśa pañca ca tattvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etā virekātiyogaduryogāyogajāḥ smṛtāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
                        vamanavirecanavyāpaccikitsitaṃ nāma catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||34 ||</l>
                </div>


                <div n="35" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>pañcatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <milestone unit="folio" n="dscn3276 fol 297"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.1"> athāto netrabastipramāṇapravibhāgacikitsitaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.3"> tatra snehādīnāṃ karmaṇāṃ bastikarma
                        pradhānatamamāhurācāryāḥ | kasmāt anekakarmakaratvād basteḥ; iha khalu
                        bastir nānāvidhadravyasaṃyogāddoṣāṇāṃ saṃśodhanasaṃśamanasaṃgrahaṇāni
                        karoti, kṣīṇaśukraṃ vājīkaroti, kṛśaṃ bṛṃhayati, sthūlaṃ karśayati, cakṣuḥ
                        prīṇayati, valīpalitamapahanti, vayaḥ sthāpayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.4"> śarīropacayaṃ varṇaṃ balamārogyamāyuṣaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                        <caesura/>
                         kurute parivṛddhiṃ ca bastiḥ samyagupāsitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.5"> tathā
                        jvarātīsāratimirapratiśyāyaśirorogādhimanthārditākṣepakapakṣāghātaikāṅgasarvāṅgarogādhmānodarayoniśūlaśarkarāśūlavṛddhyupadaṃśānāhamūtrakṛcchragulmavātaśoṇitavātamūtrapurīṣodāvartaśukrārtavastanyanāśahṛddhanumanyāgrahaśarkarāśmarīmūḍhagarbhaprabhṛtiṣu
                        cāsyartham upayujyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.6"> bhavati cātra
                        <caesura/>
                         bastir vāte ca pitte ca kaphe rakte ca śasyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃsarge sannipāte ca bastir eva hitaḥ sadā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.7"> tatra sāṃvatsarikāṣṭadviraṣṭavarṣāṇāṃ
                        ṣaḍaṣṭadaśāṅgulapramāṇāni kaniṣṭhikānāmikāmadhyamāṅgulipariṇāhānyagre
                        'dhyardhāṅguladvyaṅgulārdhatṛtīyāṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇikāni
                        kaṅkaśyenabarhiṇapakṣanāḍītulyapraveśāni mudgamāṣakalāyamātrasrotāṃsi
                        vidadhyānnetrāṇi | teṣu cāsthāpanadravyapramāṇamāturahastasaṃmitena
                        prasṛtena saṃmitau prasṛtau dvau catvāro 'ṣṭau ca vidheyāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.8"> varṣāntareṣu netrāṇāṃ bastimānasya caiva hi |
                        <caesura/>
                         vayobalaśarīrāṇi samīkṣyotkarṣayed vidhim || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.9"> pañcaviṃśaterūrdhvaṃ dvādaśāṅgulaṃ, mūle
                        'ṅguṣṭhodaraparīṇāham, agre kaniṣṭhikodaraparīṇāham, agre
                        tryaṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇikaṃ, gṛdhrapakṣanāḍīṃtulyapraveśaṃ,
                        kolāsthimātrachidraṃ, klinnakalāyamātrachidramity eke; sarvāṇi mūle
                        bastinibandhanārthaṃ dvikarṇikāni | āsthāpanadravyapraṇāṇaṃ tu vihitaṃ
                        dvādaśaprasṛtāḥ | saptatestūrdhvaṃ netrapramāṇametadeva, dravyapramāṇaṃ tu
                        dviraṣṭavarṣavat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.10"> mṛdurbastiḥ prayoktavyo viśeṣādbālavṛddhayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tayostīkṣṇaḥ prayuktas tu bastir hiṃsyād balāyuṣī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.11"> (vraṇanetramaṣṭāṅgulaṃ mudgavāhisrotaḥ; vraṇamavekṣya
                        yathāsvaṃ snehakaṣāye vidadhīta ||) </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.12"> tatra netrāṇi suvarṇarajatatāmrāyor
                        ītidantaśṛṅgamaṇitarusāramayāni ślakṣṇāni dṛḍhāni gopucchākṛtīnyṛjūni
                        guṭikāmukhāni ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.13"> bastayaś ca bandhyā mṛdavo nātivahalā dṛḍhāḥ
                        pramāṇavanto gomahiṣavarāhājorabhrāṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.14"> netrālābhe hitā nāḍī nalavaṃśāsthisaṃbhavā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bastyalābhe hitaṃ carma sūkṣmaṃ vā tāntavaṃ ghanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.15"> bastiṃ nirupadigdhaṃ tu śuddhaṃ suparimārjitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdvanuddhatahīnaṃ ca muhuḥ snehavimarditam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.16"> netrāmūle pratiṣṭhāpya nyubjaṃ tu vivṛtānanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         baddhvā lohena taptena carmasrotasi nirdahet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.17"> parivartya tato bastiṃ baddhvā guptaṃ nidhāpayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         āsthāpanaṃ ca tailaṃ ca yathāvattena dāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.18"> tatra dvividho bastiḥ nairūhikaḥ, snaihikaś ca |
                        āsthāpanaṃ, nirūha ity anarthāntaraṃ; tasya vikalpo mādhutailikaḥ; tasya
                        prayāyaśabdo yāpano, yuktarathaḥ, siddhabastir iti | sa
                        doṣanirharaṇāccharīranīrohaṇādvā nirūhaḥ, bayaḥsthāpanādāyuḥsthāpanādvā
                        āsthāpanam | mādhutailikavidhānaṃ ca nirūhopakramacikitsite vakṣyāmaḥ |
                        yathāpramāṇaguṇavihitaḥ snehabastivikalpo 'nuvāsanaḥ pādāva(pādāpa)kṛṣṭaḥ |
                        anuvasannapi na duṣyatyanudivasaṃ vā dīyata ity anuvāsanaḥ | tasyāpi vikalpo
                        'rdhārdhamātrāvakṛṣṭo 'parihāryo mātrābastir iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.19"> nirūhaḥ śodhano lekhī snaihiko bṛṃhaṇo mataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirūhaśodhitānmārgān samyak sneho 'nugacchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         apetasarvadoṣāsu nāḍīṣv iva vahajjalam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.20"> sarvadoṣaharaś cāsau śarīrasya ca jīvanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād viśuddhadehasya snehabastir vidhīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.21"> tatronmāda<pc> </pc>bhaya<pc> </pc>śoka<pc
                            > </pc>pipāsārocakājīrṇārśaḥ<pc> </pc>pāṇḍuroga<pc
                            > </pc>bhrama<pc> </pc>mada<pc> </pc>mūrcchā<pc> </pc>cchardi<pc
                            > </pc>kuṣṭha<pc> </pc>mehodarasthaulya<pc> </pc>śvāsa<pc
                            > </pc>kāsa<pc> </pc>kaṇṭhaśoṣa<pc> </pc>śophopasṛṣṭa<pc
                            > </pc>kṣata<pc> </pc>kṣīṇa<pc> </pc>catustrimāsagarbhiṇīdurbalāgnyasahā
                        bālavṛddhau ca vātarogādṛte kṣīṇā nānuvāsyā nāsthāpayitavyāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.22"> udarī ca pramehī ca kuṣṭhī sthūlaś ca mānavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         avaśyaṃ sthāpanīyāste nānuvāsyāḥ kathañcana || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.23"> asādhyatā vikārāṇāṃ syād eṣāmanuvāsanāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         asādhyatve 'pi bhūyiṣṭhaṃ gātrāṇāṃ sadanaṃ bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.24"> pakvāśaye tathā śroṇyāṃ nābhyadhastāc ca sarvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyakpraṇihito bastiḥ sthāneṣveteṣu tiṣṭhati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.25"> pakvāśayādbastivīryaṃ khair deham anusarpati |
