                        <caesura/>
                         vṛkṣamūle niṣiktānāmapāṃ vīryamiva drumam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.26"> sa cāpi sahasā bastiḥ kevalaḥ samalo 'pi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyeti vīryaṃ tvanilair apānādyair vinīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.27"> vīryeṇa bastirādatte doṣānāpādamastakāt(n) |
                        <caesura/>
                         pakvāśayastho 'mbarago bhūmerarko rasāniva || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.28"> sa kaṭīpṛṣṭhakoṣṭhasthān vīryeṇāloḍya saṃcayān |
                        <caesura/>
                         utkhātamūlān harati doṣāṇāṃ sādhuyojitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.29"> doṣatrayasya yasmāc ca prakope vāyurīśvaraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt tasyātivṛddhasya śarīram abhinighnataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.30"> vāyor viṣahate vegaṃ nānyā basterṛte kriyā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pavanāviddhatoyasya velā vegamivodadheḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.31"> śarīropacayaṃ varṇaṃ balamārogyamāyuṣaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kurute parivṛddhiṃ ca bastiḥ samyagupāsitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.32"> ata ūrdhvaṃ vyāpado vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra netraṃ vicalitaṃ,
                        vivartitaṃ, pārśvāvapīḍitam, atyutkṣiptam, avasannaṃ, tiryakprakṣiptam iti
                        ṣaṭ praṇidhānadoṣāḥ; atisthūlaṃ, karkaśam, avanataṃ, aṇubhinnaṃ,
                        sannikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭakarṇikaṃ, sūkṣmāticchidram, atidīrgham, atihrasvam,
                        asrimadity ekādaśa netradoṣāḥ; bahalatā, alpatā, sacchidratā, prastīrṇatā,
                        durbaddhateti pañca bastidoṣāḥ; atipīḍitatā, śithilapīḍitatā, bhūyo bhūyo
                        'vapīḍanaṃ, kālātikrama iti catvāraḥ pīḍanadoṣāḥ; āmatā, hīnatā, atimātratā,
                        atiśītatā, atyuṣṇatā, atitīkṣṇatā, atimṛdutā, atisnigdhatā, atirūkṣatā,
                        atisāndratā, atidravatā, ity ekādaśa dravyadoṣāḥ;
                        avākśīrṣocchīrṣanyubjottānasaṅkucitadehasthitadakṣiṇapārśvaśāyinaḥ pradānam
                        iti sapta śayyādoṣāḥ; evam etāś catuś catvāriṃśadvyāpado vaidyanimittāḥ |
                        āturanimittāḥ pañcadaśa āturopadravacikitsite vakṣyante | snehastvaṣṭabhiḥ
                        kāraṇaiḥ pratihato na pratyāgacchati tribhir doṣaiḥ, aśanābhibhūto,
                        malavyāmiśro, dūrānupraviṣṭo, asvinnasya, anuṣṇo, alpambhuktavato, alpaś
                        ceti vaidyāturanimittā bhavanti | ayogastūbhayoḥ, ādhmānaṃ, parikartikā,
                        parisrāvaḥ, pravāhikā, hṛdayopasaraṇam, aṅgapragraho, atiyogo, jīvādānam iti
                        nava vyāpado vaidyanimittā bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.33"> bhavati cātra ṣaṭsaptatiḥ samāsena vyāpadaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi vijñānaṃ siddhiṃ ca tadanantaram ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
                        netrabastipramāṇapravibhāgacikitstitaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||35 ||</l>

                </div>



                <div n="36" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>ṣaṭtriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.1"> athāto netrabastivyāpaccikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>
                    
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.3"> atha netre vicalite tathā caiva vivartite |
                        <caesura/>
                         gude kṣataṃ rujā vā syāttatra sadyaḥkṣatakriyāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.4"> atyutkṣipte 'vasanne ca netre pāyau bhaved rujā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhir atrāpi pittaghnaḥ kāryaḥ snehaiś ca secanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.5"> tiryakpraṇihite netre tathā pārśvāvapīḍite |
                        <caesura/>
                         mukhasyāvaraṇād bastir na samyak pratipadyate | ṛju netraṃ vidheyaṃ syāt
                        tatrara samyagvijānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.6"> atisthūle karkaśe ca netre 'strimati gharṣaṇāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         gude bhavet kṣataṃ ruk ca sādhanaṃ tasya pūrvavat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.7"> āsannakarṇike netre bhinne 'ṇau vā 'py apārthakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         avaseko bhaved bastes tasmād doṣān vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.8"> prakṛṣṭakarṇike raktaṃ gudamarmaprapīḍanāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaraty atrāpi pittaghno vidhirbastiś ca picchilaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.9"> hrasve tvaṇusrotasi ca kleśo bastiś ca pūrvavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyāgacchaṃs tataḥ kuryād rogān bastivighātajān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.10"> dīrghe mahāsrotasi ca jñeyamatyavapīḍavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         prastīrṇe bahale cāpi bastau durbaddhadoṣavat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.11"> bastāv alpe 'lpatā vā 'pi dravyasyālpā guṇā matāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         durbaddhe cāṇubhinne ca vijñeyaṃ bhinnanetravat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.12"> atiprapīḍito bastiḥ prayātyāmāśayaṃ tataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāterito nāsikābhyāṃ mukhato vā prapadyate || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.13"> tatra tūrṇaṃ galāpīḍaṃ kuryāc cāpy avadhūnanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śiraḥkāyavirekau ca tīkṣṇau sekāṃś ca śītalān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.14"> śanaiḥ prapīḍito bastiḥ pakvādhānaṃ ca gacchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         na ca saṃpādayaty arthaṃ tasmād yuktaṃ prapīḍayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.15"> bhūyo bhūyo 'vapīḍena vāyur antaḥ prapīḍyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tenādhmānaṃ rujaś cogrā yathāsvaṃ tatra bastayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.16"> kālātikramaṇāt kleśo vyādhiś cābhipravardhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vyādhibalaghnaṃ tu bhūyo bastiṃ nidhāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.17"> godopadehaśophau tu sneho 'pakvaḥ karoti hi |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra saṃśodhano bastir hitaṃ cāpi virecanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.18"> hīnamātrāvubhau bastī nātikāryakarau matau |
                        <caesura/>
                         atimātrau tathā ''ānāhaklamātīsārakārakau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.19"> mūrcchāṃ dāhamatīsāraṃ pittaṃ cātyuṣṇatīkṣṇakau |
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛduśītāvubhau vātavibandhādhmānakārakau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.20"> tatra hīnādiṣu hitaḥ pratyanīkaḥ kriyāvidhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gudabastyupadehaṃ tu kuryāt sāndro nirūhaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.21"> pravāhikāṃ vā janayet tanuralpaguṇāvahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra sāndre tanuṃ bastiṃ tanau sāndraṃ ca dāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.22"> snigdho 'tijāḍyakṛd rūkṣaḥ stambhādhmānakṛd ucyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         bastiṃ rūkṣamatisnigdhe snigdhaṃ rūkṣe ca dāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.23"> atipīḍitavaddoṣān viddhi cāpy avaśīrṣake |
                        <caesura/>
                         ucchīrṣake samunnāhaṃ bastiḥ kuryāc ca mehanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.24"> tatrottaro hito bastiḥ susvinnasya sukhāvahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nyubjasya bastir nāpnoti pakvādhānaṃ vimārgagaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.25"> hṛdgudaṃ bādhate cātra vāyuḥ koṣṭhamathāpi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         uttānasyāvṛte mārge bastir nāntaḥ prapadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.26"> netrasaṃvejanabhrānto vāyuś cāntaḥ prakupyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         dehe saṅkucite dattaḥ sakthnorapyubhayos tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.27ab"> na samyag anilāviṣṭo bastiḥ pratyeti dehinaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.27cd"> sthitasya bastir dattas tu kṣipramāyātyavāṅmukhaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.28"> na cāśayaṃ tarpayati tasmān nārthakaro hi saḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāpnoti bastir dattas tu kṛtsnaṃ pakvāśayaṃ punaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.29"> dakṣiṇāśritapārśvasya vāmapārśvānugo yataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nyubjādīnāṃ pradānaṃ ca basternaiva praśasyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.30"> paś cād anilakopo 'tra yathāsvaṃ tatra kārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāpadaḥ snehabastes tu vakṣyante taccikitsite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.31"> ayogādyās tu vakṣyāmi vyāpadaḥ sacikitsitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anuṣṇo 'lpauṣadho hīno bastir naiti prayojitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.32"> viṣṭambhādhmānaśūlaiś ca tam ayogaṃ pracakṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra tīkṣṇo hito bastis tīkṣṇaṃ cāpi virecanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.33"> saśeṣānne 'thavā bhukte bahudoṣe ca yojitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atyāśitasyātibahurbastir mandoṣṇa eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.34ab"> anuṣṇalavaṇasneho hy atimātro 'thavā punaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.34cd"> tathā bahupurīṣaṃ ca kṣipramādhmāpayennaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.35"> hṛtkaṭīpārśvapṛṣṭheṣu śūlaṃ tatrātidāruṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra tīkṣṇataro bastir hitaṃ cāpy anuvāsanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.36"> atitīkṣṇotilavaṇo rūkṣo bastiḥ prayojitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sapittaṃ kopayed vāyuṃ kuryāc ca parikartikām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.37"> nābhibastigudaṃ tatra chinattīvātidehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         picchābastir hitas tasya snehaś ca madhuraiḥ śṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.38"> atyamlalavaṇastīkṣṇaḥ parisrāvāya kalpate |
                        <caesura/>
                         daurbalyamaṅgasādaś ca jāyate tatra dehinaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.39"> parisravettataḥ pittaṃ dāhaṃ sañjanayed gude |
                        <caesura/>
                         picchābastir hitas tatra bastiḥ kṣīraghṛtena ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.40"> pravāhikā bhavettīkṣṇānnirūhāt sānuvāsanāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadāhaśūlaṃ kṛcchreṇa kaphāsṛgupaveśyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.41"> picchābastir hitas tatra payasā caiva bhojanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpirmadhurakaiḥ siddhaṃ tailaṃ cāpy anuvāsanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.42"> atitīkṣṇo nirūho vā savāte cānuvāsanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdayasyopasaraṇaṃ kurute vā savāte cānuvāsanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.43"> doṣais tatra rujastāstā mado mūrcchā 'ṅgagauravam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvadoṣaharaṃ bastiṃ śodhanaṃ tatra dāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.44"> rūksasya bahuvātasya tathā duḥśāyitasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         bastir aṅgagrahaṃ kuryād rūkso mṛdvalpabheṣajaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.45"> tatrāṅgasādaḥ prastambho jṛmbhodveṣṭanavepakāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         parvabhedaś ca tatreṣṭāḥ svedābhyañjanabastayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.46"> atyuṣṇatīkṣṇo 'tibahurdatto 'tisveditasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         alpadoṣasya vā bastir atiyogāya kalpate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.47"> virecanātiyogena samānaṃ tasya lakṣaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         picchābastiprayogaś ca tatra śītaḥ sukhāvahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.48"> atiyogāt paraṃ yatra jīvādānaṃ viriktavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         deyas tatra hitaś cāpsu picchābastiḥ saśoṇitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.49"> navaitā vyāpado yās tu nirūhaṃ pratyudāhṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehabastiṣv api hi tā vijñeyāḥ kuśalair iha || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.50"> ity uktā vyāpadaḥ sarvāḥ salakṣaṇacikitsitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhiṣajā ca tathā kāryaṃ yathaitā na bhavanti hi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.51"> paksādvireko vāntasya tataś cāpi nirūhaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadyo nirūḍho 'nuvāsyaḥ saptarātrādvirecitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne netrabastivyāpaccikitsitaṃ
                        nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||36 ||</l>

                <div n="37" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>saptatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.1"> athāto 'nuvāsanottarabasticikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.3"> virecanāt saptarātre gate jātabalāya vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛtānnāyānuvāsyāya samyagdeyo 'nuvāsanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.4"> yathāvayo nirūhāṇāṃ yā mātrāḥ parikīrtitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pādāvakṛṣṭāstāḥ kāryāḥ snehabastiṣu dehinām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.5"> utsṛṣṭānilaviṇmūtre nare bastiṃ vidhāpayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         etair hi vihataḥ sneho naivāntaḥ pratipadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.6"> snehavastir vidheyas tu nāviśuddhasya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehavīryaṃ tathā datte dehaṃ cānuvisarpati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.7"> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi tailānīha yathākramam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pānānvāsananasyeṣu yāni hanyurgadān bahūn || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.8"> śaṭīpuṣkarakṛpṇāhvāmadanāmaradārubhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śatāhvākuṣṭhayaṣṭyāhvavacābilvahutāśanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.9"> supiṣṭair dviguṇakṣīraṃ tailaṃ toyacaturguṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         paktvā bastau vidhātavyaṃ mūḍhavātānulomanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.10"> arśāṃsi grahaṇīdoṣamānāhaṃ viṣamajvaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭhyūrupṛṣṭhakoṣṭhasthān vātarogāṃś ca nāśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.11"> vacāpuṣkarakuṣṭhailāmadanāmarasindhujaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kākolīdvayayaṣṭyāhvamedāyugmanarādhipaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.12"> pāṭhājīvakajīvantībhārgīcandanakaṭophalaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saralāgurubilvāmbuvājigandhāgnivṛddhibhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.13"> viḍaṅgāragvadhaśyāmātrivṛnmāgadhikardhibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭais tailaṃ pacet kṣīrapañcamūlarasānvitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.14"> gulmānāhāgniṣaṅgārśograhaṇīmūtrasaṅginām |
                        <caesura/>
                         anvāsasnavidhau yuktaṃ śasyate 'nilarogiṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.15"> citrakātiviṣāpāṭhādantībilvavacāmipaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saralāṃśumatīrāsnānīlinīcaturaṅgulaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.16"> cavyājamodakākolīmedāyugmasuradrumaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jīvakarṣabhavarṣābhūvastagandhāśatāhvayaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.17"> reṇvaśvagandhāmañjiṣṭhāśaṭīpuṣkarataskaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakṣīraṃ vipacettailaṃ mārutāmayanāśanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.18"> gṛdhrasīkhañjakubjāṭhyamūtrodāvartarogiṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         śasyate 'lpabalāgnīnāṃ bastāvāśu niyojitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.19"> bhūtikair aṇḍavarṣābhūrāsnāvṛṣakarohiṣaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         daśamūlasahābhārgīṣaḍgranthāmaradārubhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.20"> balānāgabalāmūrvāvājigandhāmṛtādvayaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sahācaravarīviśvākākanāsāvidāribhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.21"> yavamāṣātasīkolakulatthaiḥ kvathitaiḥ śṛtam |
                        <caesura/>
                         jīvanīyapratīvāpaṃ tailaṃ kṣīracaturguṇam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.22"> jaṅghorutrikapārśvāṃsabāhumanyāśiraḥsthitān |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanyādvātavikārāṃs tu bastiyogair niṣevitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.23"> jīvantyatibalāmedākākolīdvayajīvakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṛṣabhātiviṣākṛṣṇākākanāsāvacāmaraiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.24"> rāsnāmadanayaṣṭyāhvasaralābhīrucandanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svayaṅguptāśaṭīśṛṅgīkalasīsārivādvayaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.25"> piṣṭais tailaghṛtaṃ pakvaṃ kṣīreṇāṣṭaguṇena tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         taccānuvāsane deyaṃ śukrāgnibalavardhanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.26"> bṛṃhaṇaṃ vātapittaghnaṃ gulmānāhaharaṃ param |
                        <caesura/>
                         nasye pāne ca saṃyuktamūrdhvajatrugadāpaham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.27"> madhukośīrakāśmaryakaṭukotpalacandanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāmāpadmakajīmūtaśakrāhvātiviṣāmbubhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.28"> tailapādaṃ pacet sarpiḥ payasā 'ṣṭaguṇena ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         nyagrodhādigaṇakvāthayuktaṃ bastiṣu yojitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.29"> dāhāsṛgdaravīsarpavātaśoṇitavidradhīn |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaraktajvarādyāṃś ca hanyāt pittakṛtān gadān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.30"> mṛṇālotpalaśālūkasārivādvayakeśaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         candanadvayabhūnimbapadmabījakaserukaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.31"> paṭolakaṭukāraktāgundrāparpaṭavāsakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭais tailaghṛtaṃ pakvaṃ tṛṇamūlarasena ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.32"> kṣīradviguṇasṃyuktaṃ bastikarmaṇi yojitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         nasye 'bhyañjanapāne vā hanyāt pittagadān bahūn || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.33"> triphalātiviṣāmūrvātrivṛccitrakavāsakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nimbāragvadhaṣaṭgranthāsaptaparṇaniśādvayaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.34"> guḍūcīndrasurākṛṣṇākuṣṭhasarṣapanāgaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailamebhiḥ samaiḥ pakvaṃ surasādirasāplutam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.35"> pānābhyañjanagaṇḍūṣanasyabastiṣu yojitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthūlatālasyakaṇḍvādīn jayetkaphakṛtān gadān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.36"> pāṭhājamodāśārṅgeṣṭāpippalīdvayanāgaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saralāgurukālīyabhārgīcavyāmaradrumaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.37"> maricailābhayākaṭvīśaṭīgranthikakaṭphalaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailameraṇḍatailaṃ vā pakvamebhiḥ samāyutam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.38"> vallīkaṇṭakamūlābhyāṃ kvāthena dviguṇena ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanyādanvāsanair dattaṃ sarvān kaphakṛtān gadān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.39"> viḍaṅgodīcyasindhūtthaśaṭīpuṣkaracitrakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭphalātiviṣābhārgīvacākuṣṭhasurāhvayaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.40"> medāmadanayaṣṭyāhvaśyāmāniculanāgaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śatāhvānīlinīrāsnākalasīvṛṣareṇubhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.41"> bilvājamodakṛṣṇāhvādantīcavyanarādhipaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailameraṇḍatailaṃ vā muṣkakādirasāplutam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.42"> plīhodāvartavātāsṛggulmānāhakaphāmayān |
                        <caesura/>
                         pramehaśarkarārśāṃsi hanyādāśvanuvāsanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.43"> aśuddham api vātena kevalenātipīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ahorātrasya kāleṣu sarveṣvevānuvāsayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.44"> rūkṣasya bahūvātasya dvau trīnapyanuvāsanān |
                        <caesura/>
                         dattvā snigdhatanuṃ jñātvā tataḥ paś cānnirūhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.45"> asnigdham api vātena kevalenātipīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehapragāḍhair matimānnirūhaiḥ samupācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.46"> atha samyaṅgirūḍhaṃ tu vātādiṣvanuvāsayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         bilvayaṣṭyāhvamadanaphalatailair yathākramam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.47"> rātrau bastiṃ na dadyāt tu doṣotkleśo hi rātrijaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehavīryayutaḥ kuryād ādhmānaṃ gauravaṃ jvaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.48"> ahni sthānasthite doṣe vahnau cānnarasānvite |
                        <caesura/>
                         sphuṭasrotomukhe dehe snehaujaḥ parisarpati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.49"> pitte 'dhike kaphe kṣīṇe rūkṣe vātarugardite |
                        <caesura/>
                         nare rātrau tu dātavyaṃ kāle coṣṇe 'nuvāsanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.50"> uṣṇe pittādhike vā 'pi divā dāhādayo gadāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃbhavanti yatas tasmāt pradoṣe yojayed bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.51"> śīte vasante ca divā grīṣmaprāvṛṅghanātyaye |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehyo dinānte pānoktān doṣān parijihīrṣatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.52"> ahorātrasya kāleṣu sarveṣvevānilādhikam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīvrāyāṃ ruji jīrṇānnaṃ bhojayitvā 'nuvāsayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.53"> na cābhuktavataḥ snehaḥ praṇidheyaḥ kathañcana |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhatvāc chūnyakoṣṭhasya sneha ūrdhvaṃ samutpatet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.54"> sadā 'nuvāsayeccāpi bhojayitvā ''ārdrapāṇinam |
                        <caesura/>
                         jvaraṃ vidagdhabhuktasya kuryāt snehaḥ prayojitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.55"> na cātisnigdhamaśanaṃ bhojayitvā 'nuvāsayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         madaṃ mūrcchāṃ ca janayed dvidhā snehaḥ prayojitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.56"> rūkṣaṃ bhuktavato hy annaṃ balaṃ varṇaṃ ca hāpayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktasnehamato jantuṃ bhojayitvā 'nuvāsayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.57"> yūṣakṣīrarasais tasmād yathāvyādhi samīkṣya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathocitāt pādahīnaṃ bhojayitvā 'nuvāsayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.58"> athānuvāsyaṃ svabhyaktamuṣṇāmbusveditaṃ śanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhojayitvā yathāśāstraṃ kṛtacaṅkramṇaṃ tataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.59"> visṛjya ca śakṛnmūtraṃ yojayet snehabastinā |
                        <caesura/>
                         praṇidhānavidhānaṃ tu nirūhe saṃpravakṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.60"> tataḥ praṇihitasneha uttāno vākśataṃ bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasāritaiḥ sarvagātrais tathā vīryaṃ visarpati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.61"> tāḍayet talayor enaṃ trīṃstrīn vārāñchanaiḥ śanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sphicoś cainaṃ tataḥ śayyāṃ trīn vārānutkṣipettataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.62"> evaṃ praṇihite bastau mandāyāso 'tha mandavāk |
                        <caesura/>
                         svāstīrṇe śayane kāmamāsītācārike rataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.63"> sa tu saindhavacūrṇena śatāhvena ca yojitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         deyaḥ sukhoṣṇaś ca tathā nireti sahasā sukham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.64"> yasyānuvāsano dattaḥ sakṛdanvakṣamāvrajet |
                        <caesura/>
                         atyauṣṇyādatitaikṣṇyādvā vāyunā vā prapīḍitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.65"> savāto 'dhikamātro vā gurutvād vā sabheṣajaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyānyo 'lpataro deyo na hi snihyatyatiṣṭhati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.66"> viṣṭabdhānilaviṇmūtraḥ snehahīne 'nuvāsane |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhaklamapravāhārtikaraś cātyanuvāsanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.67"> sānilaḥ sapurīṣaś ca snehaḥ pratyeti yasya tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         oṣacoṣau vinā śīghraṃ sa samyaganuvāsitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.68"> jīrṇānnamatha sāyāhne snehe pratyāgate punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghvannaṃ bhojayet kāmaṃ dīptāgnis tu naro yadi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.69"> prātar uṣṇodakaṃ deyaṃ dhānyanāgarasādhitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tenāsya dīpyate vahnirbhaktākāṅkṣā ca jāyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.70"> snehabastikrameṣvevaṃ vidhimāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anena vidhinā ṣaḍ vā sapta vā 'ṣṭau navaiva vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.71"> vidheyā bastayasteṣāmantarā tu nirūhaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         dattas tu prathamo bastiḥ snehayed bastivaṅkṣaṇau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.72"> samyagdatto dvitīyas tu mūrdhasthamanilaṃ jayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         janayed balavarṇau ca tṛtīyas tu prayojitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.73"> rasaṃ caturtho raktaṃ tu pañcamaḥ snehayet tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṣṭhas tu snehayenmāṃsaṃ medaḥ saptama eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.74"> aṣṭamo navamaś cāsthi majjānaṃ ca yathākramam |
                        <caesura/>
                         evaṃ śukragatān doṣān dviguṇaḥ sādhu sādhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.75"> aṣṭādaśāṣṭādaśakān bastīnāṃ yo niṣevate |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathokena vidhānena parihārakrameṇa ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.76"> sa kuñjarabalo 'śvasya javais tulyo 'maraprabhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vītapāpmā śrutadharaḥ sahasrāyurnaro bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.77"> snehabastiṃ nirūhaṃ vā naikamevātiśīlayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehādagnivadhotkleśau nirūhāt pavanādbhayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.78"> tasmānnirūḍho 'nuvāsyo nirūhyaś cānuvāsitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         naivaṃ pittakaphotkleśau syātāṃ na pavanādbhayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.79"> rūkṣāya bahuvātāya snehavastiṃ dine dine |
                        <caesura/>
                         dadyādvaidyas tato 'nyeṣāmagnyābādhabhayāttryahāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.80"> sneho 'lpamātro rūkṣāṇāṃ dīrghakālamanatyayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā nirūhaḥ snigdhānāmalpamātraḥ praśasyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.81"> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi vyāpadaḥ snehabastijāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         balavanto yadā doṣāḥ koṣṭhe syur anilādayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.82"> alpavīryaṃ tadā sneham abhibhūya pṛthagvidhān |
                        <caesura/>
                         kurvantyupadravān snehaḥ sa cāpi na nivartate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.83"> tatra vātābhibhūte tu snehe mukhakaṣāyatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         jṛmbhā vātarujastāstā vepathurviṣamajvaraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.84"> pittābhibhūte snehe tu mukhasya kaṭutā bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhastṛṣṇā jvaraḥ svedo netramūtrāṅgapītatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.85"> śleṣmābhibhūte snehe tu praseko madhurāsyatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         gauravaṃ chardirucchvāsaḥ kṛcchrācchītajvaro 'ruciḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.86"> tatra doṣābhibhūte tu snehe bastiṃ nidhāpayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathāsvaṃ doṣaśamanānyupayojyāni yāni ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.87"> atyāśite 'nnābhibhavāt sneho naiti yadā tadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         gururāmāśayaḥ śūlaṃ vāyoś cāpratisaṃcaraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.88"> hṛtpīḍā mukhavair asyṃa śvāso mūrcchā bhramo 'ruciḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāpatarpaṇasyānte dīpano vidhiriṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.89"> aśuddhasya malonmiśraḥ sneho naiti yadā punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadā 'ṅgasadanādhmāne śvāsaḥ śūlaṃ ca jāyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.90"> pakvāśayagurutvaṃ ca tatra dadyān nirūhaṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇaṃ tīkṣṇauṣadhair eva siddhaṃ cāpy anuvāsanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.91"> śuddhasya dūrānusṛte snehe snehasya darśanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         gātreṣu sarvendriyāṇām upalepo 'vasādanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.92"> snehagandhi mukhaṃ cāpi kāsaśvāsāvarocakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atipīḍitavattatra siddhirāsthāpanaṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.93"> asvinnasyāviśuddhasya sneho 'lpaḥ saṃprayojitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śīto mṛduśca nābhyeti tato mandaṃ pravāhate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.94"> vibandhagauravādhmānaśūlāḥ pakvāśayaṃ prati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāsthāpanam evāśu prayojyaṃ sānuvāsanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.95"> alpaṃ bhuktavato 'lpo hi sneho mandaguṇas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         datto naiti klamotkleśau bhṛśaṃ cāratimāvahet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.96"> tatrāpyāsthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ śodhanīyena bastinā |
                        <caesura/>
                         (anvāsanaṃ ca snehena śodhanīyena śasyate) || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.97"> ahorātrādapi snehaḥ pratyāgacchanna duṣyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryād bastiguṇāṃś cāpi jīrṇastvalpaguṇo bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.98"> yasya nopadravaṃ kuryāt snehabastir aniḥsṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvo 'lpo vā ''āvṛto raukṣyādupekṣyaḥ sa vijānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.99"> anāyāntaṃ tvahorātrāt snehaṃ saṃśodhanair haret |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehabastāvanāyāte nānyaḥ sneho vidhīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.100"> ity uktā vyāpadaḥ sarvā salakṣaṇacikitsitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         basteruttarasaṃjñasya vidhiṃ vakṣyāmyataḥ param || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.101"> caturdaśāṅgulaṃ netramāturāṅgulasaṃmitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mālatīpuṣpavṛntāgraṃ chidraṃ sarṣapanirgamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.102"> snehapramāṇaṃ paramaṃ prakuñcaś cātra kīrtitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcaviṃśādadho mātrāṃ vidadhyādbuddhikalpitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.103"> niviṣṭakarṇikaṃ madhye nārīṇāṃ caturaṅgule |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtrasrotaḥparīṇāhaṃ mudgavāhi daśāṅgulam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.104"> meḍhrāyāmasamaṃ kecidicchanti khalu tadvidaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāsāmapatyamārge tu nidadhyāccaturaṅgulam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.105"> dvyaṅgulaṃ mūtramārge tu kanyānāṃ tvekamaṅgulam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidheyaṃ cāṅgulaṃ tāsāṃ vidhivadvakṣyate yathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.106"> snehasya prasṛtaṃ cātra svāṅgulīmūlasaṃmitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         deyaṃ pramāṇaṃ paramamarvāg buddhivikalpitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.107"> aurabhraḥ śaukaro vā 'pi bastirājaś ca pūjitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadalābhe prayuñjīta galacarma tu pakṣiṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.108"> (tasyālābhe dṛteḥ pādo mṛducarma tato 'pi vā) |
                        <caesura/>
                         athāturam upasnigdhaṃ svinnaṃ praśithilāśayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.109"> yavāgūṃ saghṛtakṣīrāṃ pītavantaṃ yathābalam |
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣaṇṇamājānusame pīṭhe sopāśraye samam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.110"> svabhyaktabastimūrdhānaṃ tailenoṣṇena mānavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ samaṃ sthāpayitvā nālamasya praharṣitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.111"> pūrvaṃ śalākayā 'nviṣya tato netramanantaram |
                        <caesura/>
                         śanaiḥ śanair ghṛtābhyaktaṃ vidadhyādaṅgulāni ṣaṭ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.112"> meḍhrayāmasamaṃ kecidicchanti praṇidhānakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato 'vapīḍayed bastiṃ śanair netraṃ ca nirharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.113"> tataḥ pratyāgatasnehamaparāhṇe vicakṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhojayet payasā mātrāṃ yūṣeṇātha rasena vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.114"> anena vidhinā dadyādbastīṃstrīṃś caturo 'pi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ūrdhvajānvai striyai dadyāduttānāyai vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.115"> samyak prapīḍayed yoniṃ dadyāt sumṛdupīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         trikarṇikena netreṇa dadyādyonimukhaṃ prati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.116"> garbhāśayaviśuddhyarthaṃ snehena dviguṇena tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         kvāthapramāṇaṃ prasṛtaṃ striyā dviprasṛtaṃ bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.117"> kanyetarasyāḥ kanyāyāstadvadbastipramāṇakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         apratyāgacchati bhiṣag bastāvuttarasaṃjñite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.118"> bhūyo bastiṃ nidadhyāt tu saṃyuktaṃ śodhanair gaṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gude vartiṃ nidadhyādvā śodhanadravyasaṃbhṛtām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.119"> praveśayed vā matimān bastidvāramathaiṣaṇīm |
                        <caesura/>
                         pīḍayed vā 'pyadho nābherbalenottaramuṣṭinā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.120"> āragvadhasya patrais tu nirguṇḍyāḥ svarasena ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryād gomūtrapiṣṭeṣu vartīrvā 'pi sasaindhavāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.121"> mudgailāsarṣapasamāḥ pravibhajya vayāṃsi tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         basterāgamanārthāya tā nidadhyāchalākayā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.122"> āgāradhūmabṛhatīpippalīphalasaindhavaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛtā vā śuktagomūtrasurāpiṣṭaiḥ sanāgaraiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.123"> anuvāsanasiddhiṃ ca vīkṣya karma prayojayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarkarāmadhumiśreṇa śītena madhukāmbunā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.124"> dahyamāne tadā bastau dadyādbastiṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīravṛkṣakaṣāyeṇa payasā śītalena ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.125"> śukraṃ duṣṭaṃ śoṇitaṃ cāṅganānāṃ puṣpodrekaṃ tasya
                        nāṇaṃ ca kaṣṭam |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtrāghātānmūtradoṣān pravṛddhān yonivyādhiṃ saṃsthitiṃ cāparāyāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.126"> śukrotsekaṃ śarkarāmaśmarīṃ ca śūlaṃ bastau vaṅkṣaṇe
                        mehane ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghorānanyān bastijāṃś cāpi rogān hitvā mehānuttaro hanti bastiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.127"> samyag dattasya liṅgāni vyāpadaḥ krama eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         baster uttarasaṃjñasya samānaṃ snehabastinā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
                        'nuvāsanottarabasticikitsitaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||37 || </l>
                </div>
                <div n="38" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>aṣṭatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.1"> athāto nirūhakramacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.3"> athānuvāsitam āsthāpayet;
                        svabhyaktasvinnaśarīramutsṛṣṭabahirvegamavāte śucau veśmani madhyāhne
                        pratatāyāṃ śayyāyāmadhaḥsuparigrahāyāṃ
                        śroṇipradeśaprativyūḍhāyāmanupadhānāyāṃ
                        vāmapārśvaśāyinamākuñcitadakṣiṇasakthimitaraprasāritasakthiṃ sumanasaṃ
                        jīrṇānnaṃ vāgyataṃ suniṣaṇṇadehaṃ viditvā, tato vāmapādasyopari netraṃ
                        kṛtvetarapādāṅguṣṭhāṅgulibhyāṃ karṇikām upari niṣpīḍya,
                        savyapāṇikaniṣṭhikānāmikābhyāṃ bastermukhārdhaṃ saṅkocya,
                        madhyamāpradeśinyaṅguṣṭhair ardhaṃ tu vivṛtāsyaṃ kṛtvā, bastāvauṣadhaṃ
                        prakṣipya, dakṣiṇahastāṅguṣṭhena pradeśinīmadhyamābhyāṃ
                        cānusiktamanāyatamabudbudamasaṅkucitamavātamauṣadhāsannam upasaṃgṛhya,
                        punarupari taditareṇa gṛhītvā dakṣiṇenāvasiñcet, tataḥ sūtreṇaivauṣadhānte
                        dvistrirvā ''āveṣṭya badhnīyāt, atha dakṣiṇenottānena pāṇinā bastiṃ gṛhītvā
                        vāmahastamadhyamāṅgulipradeśinībhyāṃ netram upasaṃgṛhyāṅguṣṭena netradvāraṃ
                        pidhāya, ghṛtābhyaktāgranetraṃ ghṛtāktamupādāya prayacched anupṛṣṭhavaṃśaṃ
                        samamunmukhamākarṇikaṃ netraṃ praṇidhatsveti brūyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.4"> bastiṃ savye kare kṛtvā dakṣiṇenāvapīḍayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekenaivāvapīḍena na drutaṃ na vilambitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.5"> tato netramapanīya triṃśanmātrāḥ pīḍanakālād
                        upekṣyottiṣṭhetyāturaṃ brūyāt | athāturam upaveśayed utkuṭukaṃ
                        bastyāgamanārtham | nirūhapratyāgamanakālas tu muhūrto bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.6"> anena vidhinā bastiṃ dadyādbastiviśāradaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dvitīyaṃ vā tṛtīyaṃ vā caturthaṃ vā yathārthataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.7"> samyaṅnirūḍhaliṅge tu prāote bastiṃ nivārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣāt sukumārāṇāṃ hīna eva kramo hitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.8"> api hīnakramaṃ kuryānna tu kuryād atikramam |
                        <caesura/>
                         yasya syādbastir alpo 'lpavego hīnamalānilaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.9"> durnirūḍhaḥ sa vijñeyo mūtrārtyarucijāḍyavān
                        <caesura/>
                         | yānyeva prāṅmayoktāni liṅgānyativirecite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.10"> tānyevātinirūḍhe 'pi vijñeyāni vipaścitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yasya krameṇa gacchanti viṭpittakaphavāyavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.11"> lāghavaṃ copajāyeta sunirūḍhaṃ tam ādiśet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sunirūḍhaṃ tato jantuṃ snātavantaṃ tu bhojayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.12"> pittaśleṣmānilāviṣṭaṃ kṣīrayūṣarasaiḥ kramāt ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvaṃ vā jāṅgalarasair bhojayed avikāribhiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.13"> tribhāgahīnam ardhaṃ vā hīnamātram athāpi vā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yathāgnidoṣaṃ mātreyaṃ bhojanasya vidhīyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.14"> anantaraṃ tato yuñjyād yathāsvaṃ snehabastinā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         viviktatā manastuṣṭiḥ snigdhatā vyādhinigrahaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.15"> āsthāpanasnehabastyoḥ samyag dāne tu lakṣaṇam ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tadahas tasya pavanād bhayaṃ balavad iṣyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.16"> rasaudanastena śastas tadahaś cānuvāsanam ||
                        <caesura/>
                         paś cād agnibalaṃ matvā pavanasya ca ceṣṭitam ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.17"> annopastambhite koṣṭhe snehabastir vidhīyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         anāyāntaṃ muhūrttāt tu nirūhaṃ śodhanair haret ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.18"> tīkṣṇair nirūhair matimān kṣāramūtrāmlasaṃyutaiḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         viguṇānilaviṣṭabdhaṃ ciraṃ tiṣṭhannirūhaṇam ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.19"> śūlāratijvarānāhān maraṇaṃ vā pravartayet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         na tu bhuktavato deyam āsthāpanam iti sthitiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.20"> visūcikāṃ vā janayecchardiṃ vā 'pi sudāruṇām ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kopayet sarvadoṣān vā tasmād dadyād abhojine ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.21"> jīrṇānnasyāśaye doṣāḥ puṃsaḥ pravyaktim āgatāḥ |.
                        <caesura/>
                         niḥśeṣāḥ sukhamāyānti bhojanenāprapīḍitāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.22"> navā''sthāpanavikṣiptam annam agniḥ pradhāvati |.
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād āsthāpanaṃ deyaṃ nirāhārāya jānatā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.23"> āvasthikaṃ kramaṃ cāpi buddhvā kāryaṃ nirūhaṇam |.
                        <caesura/>
                         male 'pakṛṣṭe doṣāṇāṃ balavattvaṃ na vidyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.24"> kṣīrāṇyamlāni mūtrāṇi snehāḥ kvāthā rasās tathā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         lavaṇāni phalaṃ kṣaudraṃ śatāhvā sarṣapaṃ vacā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.25"> elā trikaṭukaṃ rāsnā saralo devadāru ca ||
                        <caesura/>
                         rajanī madhukaṃ hiṅgu kuṣṭhaṃ saṃśodhanāni ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.26"> kaṭukā śarkarā mustam uśīraṃ candanaṃ śaṭī ||
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjiṣṭhā madanaṃ caṇḍā trāyamāṇā rasāñjanam ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.27"> bilvamadhyaṃ yavānī ca phalinī śakrajā yavāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kākolī kṣīrakākolī jīvakarṣabhakāvubhau ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.28"> tathā bhedā mahābhedā ṛddhir vṛddhir madhūlikā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nirūheṣu yathālābham eṣa vargo vidhīyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.29"> svasthe kvāthasya catvāro bhāgāḥ snehasya pañcamaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kruddhe 'nile caturthas tu ṣaṣṭhaḥ pitte kaphe 'ṣṭamaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.30"> sarveṣu cāṣṭamo bhāgaḥ kalkānāṃ lavaṇaṃ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudraṃ mūtraṃ phalaṃ kṣīramamlaṃ māṃsarasaṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.31"> yuktyā prakalpayed dhīmān nirūh kalpanā tviyam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.32"> kalkasnehakaṣāyāṇāmavivekādbhiṣagvaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         basteḥ sukalpanā proktā tasya dānaṃ yathārthakṛt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.33"> dattvā ''ādau saindhavasyākṣaṃ madhunaḥ prasṛtadvayam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pātre talena mathnīyāttadvat snehaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.34"> samyak sumathite dadyāt phalakalkamataḥ param |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato yathocitān kalkān bhāgaiḥ svaiḥ ślakṣṇapeṣitān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.35"> gambhīre bhājane 'nyasminmaśnīyāttaṃ khajena ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā vā sādhu manyeta na sāndro na tanuḥ samaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.36"> rasakṣīrāmlamūtrāṇāṃ doṣāvasthāmavekṣya tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyaprasṛtān pañca supūtāṃs tatra dāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.37"> ata ūrdhvaṃ dvādaśaprasṛtān vakṣyāmaḥ | dattvā ''ādau
                        saindhavasyākṣaṃ madhunaḥ prasṛtidvayam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vinirmathya tato dadyāt snehasya prasṛtitrayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.38"> ekībhūte tataḥ snehe kalkasya prasṛtiṃ kṣipet |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃmūrcchite kaṣāyaṃ tu catuḥprasṛtisaṃmitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.39"> vitarec ca tadāvāpamante dviprasṛtonmitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         evaṃ prakalpito bastir dvādaśaprasṛto bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.40"> jyeṣṭhāyāḥ khalu mātrāyāḥ pramāṇamidamīritam |
                        <caesura/>
                         apahrāse bhiṣak kuryāt tadvat prasṛtihāpanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.41"> yathāvayo nirūhāṇāṃ kalpaneyamudāhṛtā |
                        <caesura/>
                         saindhavādidravāntānāṃ siddhikāmair bhiṣagvaraiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.42"> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyante bastayo 'tra vibhāgaśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathādoṣaṃ prayuktā ye hanyurnānāvidhān gadān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.43"> śampākorubuvarṣābhūvājigandhāniśācchadaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcamūlībalārāsnāguḍūcīsuradārubhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.44"> kvathitaiḥ pālikair ebhir madanāṣṭakasaṃyutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkair māgadhikāmbhodahapuṣāmisisaindhavaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.45"> vatsāhvayapriyaṅgūgrāyaṣṭyāhvayarasāñjanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dadyādāsthāpanaṃ koṣṇaṃ kṣaudrādyair abhisaṃskṛtam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.46"> pṛṣṭhorutrikaśūlāśmaviṇmūtrānilasaṅginām |
                        <caesura/>
                         grahaṇīmārutārśoghnaṃ raktamāṃsabalapradam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.47"> guḍūcītriphalārāsnādaśamūlabalāpalaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kvathitaiḥ ślakṣṇapiṣṭas tu priyaṅgughanasaindhavaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.48"> śatapuṣpāvacākṛṣṇāyavānīkuṣṭhabilvajaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saguḍair akṣamātrais tu madanārdhapalānvitaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.49"> kṣaudratailaghṛtakṣīraśuktakāñjikamastubhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samāloḍya ca mūtreṇa dadyādāsthāpanaṃ param || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.50"> tejovarṇabalotsāhavīryāgniprāṇavardhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvamārutarogaghnaṃ vayaḥsthāpanam uttamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.51"> kuśādipañcamūlābdatriphalotpalavāsakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sārivośīramañjiṣṭhārāsnāreṇuparūṣakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.52"> pālikaiḥ kvathitaiḥ samyag dravyair ebhiś ca peṣitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śṛṅgāṭakātmaguptebhakesarāgurucandanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.53"> vidārīmisimañjiṣṭhāśyāmendrayavasindhujaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         phalapadmakayaṣṭyāhvaiḥ kṣaudrakṣīraghṛtāplutaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.54"> dattamāsthāpanaṃ śītamamlahīnais tathā dravaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhāsṛgdarapittāsṛkpittagulmajvarāñjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.55"> rodhracandanamañjiṣṭhārāsnānantābalardhibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sārivāvṛṣakāśmaryamedāmadhukapadmakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.56"> sthirāditṛṇamūlaiś ca kvāthaḥ karṣatrayonmitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭair jīvakakākolīyugardhimadhukotpalaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.57"> prapauṇḍarīkajīvantīmedāreṇuparūṣakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhīrumisisindhūtthavatsakośīrapadmakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.58"> kaseruśarkarāyuktaiḥ sarpirmadhupayaḥplutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dravais tīkṣṇāmlavarjyaiś ca datto bastiḥ suśītalaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.59"> gulmāsṛgdarahṛtpāṇḍurogān saviṣamajvarān |
                        <caesura/>
                         asṛkpittātisārau ca hanyātpittakṛtān gadān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.60"> bhadrānimbakulatthārkakośātakyamṛtāmaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sārivābṛhatīpāṭhāmūrvāragvadhavatsakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.61"> kvāthaḥ kalkas tu kartavyo vacāmadanasarṣapaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saindhavāmarakuṣṭhailāpippalībilvanāgaraiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.62"> kaṭutailamadhukṣāramūtratailāmlasaṃyutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāryamāsthāpanaṃ tūrṇaṃ kāmalāpāṇḍumehinām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.63"> medasvināmanagnīnāṃ kapharogāśanadviṣām |
                        <caesura/>
                         galagaṇḍagaraglāniślīpadodararogiṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.64"> daśamūlīniśābilvapaṭolatriphalāmaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kvathitaiḥ kalkapiṣṭais tu mustasaindhavadārubhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.65"> pāṭhāmāgadhikendrāhvais tailakṣāramadhuplutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryād āsthāpanaṃ samyaṅmūtrāmlaphalayojitaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.66"> kaphapāṇḍugadālasyamūtramārutasaṃginām |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmāṭopāpacīśleṣmagulmakrimivikāriṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.67"> vṛṣāśmabhedavarṣābhūdhānyagandharvahastakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         daśamūlabalāmūrvāyavakolaniśācchadaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.68"> kulatthabilvabhūnimbaiḥ kvāthitaiḥ palasaṃmitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkair madanayaṣṭyāhvaṣaḍgranthāmarasarṣapaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.69"> pippalīmūlasindhūtthayavānīmisivatsakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudrekṣukṣīragomūtrasarpistailarasāplutaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.70"> tūrṇamāsthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ saṃsṛṣṭabahurogiṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         gṛdhrasīśarkarāṣṭhīlātūnīgulmagadāpaham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.71"> rāsnāragvadhavarṣābhūkaṭukośīravāridaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         trāyamāṇāmṛtāraktāpañcamūlībibhītakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.72"> sabalaiḥ pālikaiḥ kvāthaḥ kalkas tu madanānvitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaṣṭyāhvamisisindhūtthaphalinīndrayavāhvayaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.73"> rasāñjanarasakṣaudradrākṣāsauvīrasaṃyutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yukto bastiḥ sukhoṣṇo 'yaṃ māṃsaśukrabalaujasām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.74"> āyuṣo 'gneś ca saṃskartā hanti cāśu gadānimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         gulmāsṛgdaravīsarpamūtrakṛcchrakṣatakṣayān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.75"> viṣamajvaramarśāsi grahaṇīṃ vātakuṇḍalīm |
                        <caesura/>
                         jānujaṅghāśirobastigrahodāvartamārutān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.76"> vātāsṛkśarkarāṣṭhīlākukṣiśūlodarārucīḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         raktapittakaphonmādapramehādhmānahṛdgrahān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.77"> vātaghnauṣadhaniṣkvāthāḥ saindhavatrivṛtāyutāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāmlāḥ sukhoṣṇā yojyāḥ syur bastayaḥ kupite 'nile || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.78"> nyagrodhādigaṇakvāthāḥ kākolyādisamāyutāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidheyā bastayaḥ pitte sasarpiṣkāḥ saśarkarāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.79"> āragvadhādiniṣkvāthāḥ pippalyādisamāyutāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakṣaudramūtrā deyāḥ syur bastayaḥ kupite kaphe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.80"> śarkarekṣurasakṣīraghṛtayuktāḥ suśītalāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīravṛkṣakaṣāyāḍhyā bastayaḥ śoṇite hitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.81"> śodhanadravyaniṣkvāthāstatkalkasnehasaindhavaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktāḥ khajena mathitabastayaḥ śodhanāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.82"> triphalākvāthagomūtrakṣaudrakṣārasamāyutāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ūṣakādipratīvāpā bastayo lekhanāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.83"> bṛṃhaṇadravyaniṣkvāthāḥ kalkair madhurakair yutāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpirmāṃsarasopetā bastayo bṛṃhaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.84"> caṭakāṇḍoccaṭākvāthāḥ sakṣīraghṛtaśarkarāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ātmaguptāphalāvāpāḥ smṛtā vājīkarā nṛṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.85"> badaryairāvatīśeluśālmalīdhanvanāṅkurāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrasiddhāḥ kṣaudrayutāḥ sāsrāḥ picchilasaṃjñitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.86"> vārāhamāhiṣaurabhrabaiḍālaiṇeyakaukkuṭam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadyaskamasṛgājaṃ vā deyaṃ picchilabastiṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.87"> priyaṅgvādigaṇakvāthā ambaṣṭhādyena saṃyutāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakṣaudrāḥ saghṛtāś caiva grāhiṇo bastayaḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.88"> eteṣv eva ca yogeṣu snehāḥ siddhāḥ pṛthak pṛthak |
                        <caesura/>
                         samasteṣv athavā samyagvidheyāḥ snehabastayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.89"> vandhyānāṃ śatapākena śodhitānāṃ yathākramam |
                        <caesura/>
                         balātailena deyāḥ syur bastayastraivṛtena ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.90"> narasyottamasattvasya tīkṣṇaṃ bastiṃ nidhāpayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhyamaṃ madhyasattvasya viparītasya vai mṛdum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.91"> evaṃ kālaṃ balaṃ doṣaṃ vikāraṃ ca vikāravit |
                        <caesura/>
                         bastidravyabalaṃ caiva vīkṣya bastīn prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.92"> dadyādutkleśanaṃ pūrvaṃ madhye doṣaharaṃ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paś cāt saṃśamanīyaṃ ca dadyādbastiṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.93"> eraṇḍabījaṃ madhukaṃ pippalī saindhavaṃ vacā |
                        <caesura/>
                         hapuṣāphalakalkaś ca bastir utkleśanaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.94"> śatāhvā madhukaṃ bījaṃ kauṭajaṃ phalam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakāñjikaḥ sagomūtro bastir doṣaharaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.95"> priyaṅgurmadhukaṃ mustā tathaiva ca rasāñjanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakṣīraḥ śasyate bastir doṣāṇāṃ śamanaḥ paraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.96"> nṛpāṇāṃ tatsamānānāṃ tathā sumahatām api |
                        <caesura/>
                         nārīṇāṃ sukumārāṇāṃ śiśusthavirayor api || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.97"> doṣanirharaṇārthāya balavarṇodayāya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         samāsenopadekṣyāmi vidhānaṃ mādhutailikam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.98"> yānastrībhojyapāneṣu niyamaś cātra nocyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         phalaṃ ca vipulaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vyāpadāṃ cāpy asaṃbhavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.99"> yojyastvataḥ sukhenaiva nirūhakramamicchatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yadecchati tadaivaiṣa prayoktavyo vipaścitā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.100"> madhutaile same syātāṃ kvāthaś cair aṇḍamūlajaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         palārdhaṃ śatapuṣpāyāstato 'rdhaṃ saindhavasya ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.101"> phalenaikena saṃyuktaḥ khajena ca viloḍitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         deyaḥ sukhoṣṇo bhiṣajā mādhutailikasaṃjñitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.102"> vacāmadhukatailaṃ ca kvāthaḥ sarasasaindhavaḥ |
                        pippalīphalasaṃyukto bastir yuktarathaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.103"> suradāru varā rāsnā śatapuṣpā vacā madhu |
                        <caesura/>
                         hiṅgusaindhavasaṃyukto bastir doṣaharaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.104"> pañcamūlīkaṣāyaṃ ca tailaṃ māgadhikā madhu |
                        <caesura/>
                         bastir eṣa vidhātavyaḥ saśatāhvaḥ sasaindhavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.105"> yavakolakulatthānāṃ kvātho māgadhikā madhu |
                        <caesura/>
                         sasaindhavaḥ sayaṣṭyāhvaḥ siddhabastir iti smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.106"> mustāpāṭhāmṛtātiktābalārāsnāpunarnavāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjiṣṭhāragvadhośīratrāyamāṇākhyagokṣurān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.107"> pālikān pañcamūlālpasahitānmadanāṣṭakam |
                        <caesura/>
                         jalāḍhake pacet kvāthaṃ pādaśeṣaṃ punaḥ pacet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.108"> kṣīrārdhāḍhakasaṃyuktamākṣīrāt suparisrutam |
                        <caesura/>
                         apadena jāṅgalarasastatahā madhughṛtaṃ samam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.109"> śatāhvāphalinīyaṣṭīvatsakaiḥ sarasāñjanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kārṣikaiḥ saindhavonmiśraiḥ kalkair bastiḥ prayojitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.110"> vātāsṛṅmehaśophārśogulmamūtravibandhanut |
                        <caesura/>
                         visarpajvaraviḍbhaṅgaraktapittavināśanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.111"> balyaḥ saṃjīvano vṛṣyaś cakṣuṣyaḥ śūlanāśanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yāpanānāmayaṃ rājā bastir mustādiko mataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.112"> avekṣya bheṣajaṃ buddhyā vikāraṃ ca vikāravit |
                        <caesura/>
                         bījenānena śāstrajñaḥ kuryād bastiśatāny api || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.113"> ajīrṇe na prayuñjīta divāsvapnaṃ ca varjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         āhārācārikaṃ śeṣamanyat kāmaṃ samācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.114"> yasmānmadhu ca tailaṃ ca prādhānyena pradīyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         mādhutailika ity evaṃ bhiṣagbhir bastir ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.115"> ratheṣv api ca yukteṣu hastyaśve cāpi kalpite |
                        <caesura/>
                         yasmānna pratiṣiddho 'yamato yuktarathaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.116"> balopacayavarṇānāṃ yasmād vyādhiśatasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavaty etena siddhis tu siddhabastir ato mataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.117"> sukhināmalpadoṣāṇāṃ nityaṃ snigdhāś ca ye narāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdukoṣṭhāś ca ye teṣāṃ vidheyā mādhutailikāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.118"> mṛdutvāt pādahīnatvād akṛtsnavidhisevanāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekabastipradānāc ca siddhabastiṣvayantraṇā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne nirūhakramacikitsitaṃ
                        nāmāṣṭatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||38 ||</l>

                <div n="39" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>ekonacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.1"> athāta āturopadravacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.3"> snehapītasya vāntasya viriktasya srutāsṛjaḥ | nirūḍhasya
                        ca kāyāgnir mando bhavati dehinaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.4"> so 'gnair atyarthagurubhir upayuktaiḥ praśāmyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         alpo mahadbhir bahubhiś chādito 'gnir ivendhanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.5"> sa cālpair laghubhiś cānnair upayuktair vivardhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāṣṭhair aṇubhir alpaiś ca sandhukṣita ivānalaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.6"> hṛtadoṣapramāṇena sadāhāravidhiḥ smṛtaḥ | trīṇi cātra
                        pramāṇāni prastho 'rdhāḍhakam āḍhakam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.7"> tatrāvaraṃ prasthamātraṃ dve śeṣe madhyamottame |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasthe parisrute deyā yavāgūḥ khalpataṇḍulā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.8"> dve caivārdhāḍhake deye tisraś cāpy āḍhake gate |
                        <caesura/>
                         vilepīmucitādbhaktāc caturthāṃśakṛtāṃ tataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.9"> dadyād uktena vidhinā klinnasikthāmapicchilām |
                        <caesura/>
                         agnigdhalavaṇaṃ svacchamudgayūṣayutaṃ tataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.10a"> aṃśadvayapramāṇena dadyāt susvinnam odanam |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.10b"> tatas tu kṛtasaṃjñena hṛdyenendriyabodhinā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.11"> trīn aṃśān vitared bhoktum āturāyaudanaṃ mṛdu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato yathocitaṃ bhaktaṃ bhoktum asmai vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.12"> lāvaiṇahariṇādīnāṃ rasair dadyāt susaṃskṛtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnamadhyottameṣv eṣu virekeṣu prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.13a"> ekadvitriguṇaḥ samyag āhārasya kramas tv ayam |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.13b"> kaphapittādhikān madyanity ān hīnaviśodhitān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.14a"> peyā 'bhiṣyandayet teṣāṃ tarpaṇādikramo hitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.14b"> vedanālābhaniyamaśokavaicittyahetubhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.15"> narān upoṣitāṃś cāpi viriktavad upācaret |
                        āḍhakārdhāḍhakaprasthasaṃkhyā hy eṣā virecane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.16"> śleṣmāntatvād virekasya na tām icchati tadvidaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         eko virekaḥ śleṣmānto na dvitīyo 'sti kaś cana || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.17"> balaṃ yat trividhaṃ proktam atas tatra kramas tridhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrānukramamekaṃ tu balasthaḥ sakṛdācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.18"> dvirācarenmadhyabalastrīn vārān durbalas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kecid evaṃ kramaṃ prāhur mandamadhyottamāgniṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.19"> saṃsargeṇa vivṛddhe 'gnau doṣakopabhayādbhajet |
                        <caesura/>
                         prāk svādutiktau snigdhāmlalavaṇān kaṭukaṃ tataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.20"> svādvamlalavaṇān bhūyaḥ svādutiktāvataḥ param |
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdharūkṣān rasāṃś caiva vyatyāsāt svasthavattataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.21"> kevalaṃ snehapīto vā vānto yaś cāpi kevalam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa saptarātraṃ manujo bhuñjīta laghu bhojanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.22"> kṛtaḥ sirāvyadho yasya kṛtaṃ yasya ca śodhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa nā pariharenmāsaṃ yāvadvā balavān bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.23"> tryahaṃ tryahaṃ parihared ekaikaṃ bastim āturaḥ ||
                        tṛtīye tu parīhāre yathāyogaṃ samācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.24"> tailapūrṇāmṛdbhāṇḍasadharmāṇo vraṇāturāḥ |
                        snigdhaśuddhākṣirogārtā jvarātīsāriṇaś ca ye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.25"> krudhyataḥ kupitaṃ pittaṃ kuryāt tāṃs tān upadravān |
                        <caesura/>
                         āyāsyataḥ śocato vā cittaṃ vibhramam ṛcchati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.26"> maithunopagamād ghorān vyādhīn āpnoti durmatiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ākṣepakaṃ pakṣaghātam aṅgapragraham eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.27"> guhyapradeśe śvayathuṃ kāsaśvāsau ca dāruṇau |
                        <caesura/>
                         rudhiraṃ śukravac cāpi sarajaskaṃ pravartate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.28"> labhate ca divāsvapnāttāṃstān vyādhīn kaphātmakān |
                        <caesura/>
                         plīhodaraṃ pratiśyāyaṃ pāṇḍutāṃ śvayathuṃ jvaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.29"> mohaṃ sadanam aṅgānām avipākaṃ tathā 'rucim |
                        <caesura/>
                         tamasā cābhibhūtas tu svapnam evābhinandati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.30"> uccaiḥ saṃbhāṣaṇād vāyuḥ śirasy āpādayed rujam |
                        <caesura/>
                         āndhyaṃ jāḍyamajighratvaṃ bādhiryaṃ mūkatāṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.31a"> hanumokṣamadhīmanthamarditaṃ ca sudāruṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.31b"> netrastambhaṃ nimeṣaṃ vā tṛṣṇāṃ kāsaṃ prajāgaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.32"> labhate dantacālaṃ ca tāṃs tāṃś cānyān upadravān |
                        <caesura/>
                         yānayānena labhate chardimūrcchābhramaklamān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.33"> tathaivāṅgagrahaṃ ghoram indriyāṇāṃ ca vibhramam |
                        <caesura/>
                         cirāsanāt tathā sthānāc chroṇyāṃ bhavati vedanā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.34"> aticaṅkramaṇād vāyur jaṅghayoḥ kurute rujaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakthipraśoṣaṃ śophaṃ vā pādaharṣam athāpi vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.35a"> śītasaṃbhogatoyānāṃ sevā mārutavṛddhaye |
                        <caesura/>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.35b"> tato 'ṅgamardaviṣṭambhaśūlādhmānapravepakāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.36"> vātātapābhyāṃ vaivarṇyaṃ jvaraṃ cāpi samāpnuyāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         viruddhādhyaśanān mṛtyuṃ vyādhiṃ vā ghoram ṛcchati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.37"> asātmyabhojanaṃ hanyād balavarṇam asaṃśayam |
                        <caesura/>
                         anātmavantaḥ paśuvad bhuñjate ye 'pramāṇataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogānīkasya te mūlam ajīrṇaṃ prāpnuvanti hi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.38"> vyāpadāṃ kāraṇaṃ vīkṣya vyāpatsv etāsu buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         prayatetāturārogye pratyanīkena hetunā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.39"> viriktavāntair hariṇaiṇalāvakāḥ śaśaś ca sevyaḥ
                        samayūratittiriḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṣaṣṭikāś caiva purāṇaśālayas tathaiva mudgā laghu yac ca kīrtitam ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne āturopadravacikitsitaṃ
                        nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||39 ||</l>
