                <div n="40" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.1"> athāto dhūmanasyakavalagrahacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.3"> dhūmaḥ pañcavidho bhavati tad yathā prāyogikaḥ, snaihiko,
                        vair enikaḥ, kāsaghno, vāmanīyaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.4"> tatrailādinā kuṣṭhatagaravarjyena ślakṣṇapiṣṭena
                        dvādaśāṅgulaṃ śarakāṇḍamaṅgulipariṇāhaṃ kṣaumeṇāṣṭāṅgulaṃ veṣṭayitvā lepayed
                        eṣā vartiḥ prāyogike, snehaphalasāramadhūcchiṣṭasarjarasagugguluprabhṛtibhiḥ
                        snehamiśraiḥ snaihike, śirovirecanadravyair vair ecane,
                        bṛhatīkaṇṭakārikātrikaṭukāsamardahiṅgviṅgudītvaṅmanaḥśilācchinnaruhākarkaṭaśṛṅgīprabhṛtibhiḥ
                        kāsaharaiś ca kāsaghne,
                        snāyucarmakhuraśṛṅgakarkaṭakāsthiśuṣkamatsyavallūrakṛmiprabhṛtibhir
                        vāmanīyaiś ca vāmanīye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.5"> tatra bastinetradravyair dhūmanetradravyāṇi vyākhyātāni
                        bhavanti | dhūmanetraṃ tu kaniṣṭhikāpariṇāhamagre kalāyamātrasroto mūle
                        'ṅguṣṭhapariṇāhaṃ dhūmavartipraveśasroto 'ṅgulānyaṣṭacatvāriṃśat prāyogike,
                        dvātriṃśat snehane, caturviṃśatirvair ecane, ṣoḍaśāṅgulaṃ kāsaghne vāmanīye
                        ca | ete 'pi kolāsthimātracchidre bhavataḥ | vraṇanetramaṣṭāṅgulaṃ
                        vraṇadhūpanārthaṃ kalāyaparimaṇḍalaṃ kulatthavāhisrota iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.6"> atha sukhopaviṣṭaḥ sumanā ṛjvadhodṛṣṭiratandritaḥ sthire
                        samāhite śarāve prakṣipya vartiṃ mūlacchidreṇānyena śarāveṇa pidhāya tasmin
                        chidre netramūlaṃ saṃyojya dhūmamāseveta, praśānte dhūme vartimavaśiṣṭāṃ
                        prakṣipya punarapi dhūmaṃ pāyayed ādoṣaviśuddheḥ; eṣa dhūmapānopāyavidhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.7"> mukhena taṃ pibet pūrvaṃ nāsikābhyāṃ tataḥ pibet|
                        mukhapītaṃ mukhenaiva vamet pītaṃ ca nāsayā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.8"> mukhena dhūmam ādāya nāsikābhyāṃ na nirharet| tena hi
                        pratilomena dṛṣṭis tatra nihanyate|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.9"> viśeṣatas tu prāyogikaṃ ghrāṇenādadīta, snaihikaṃ
                        mukhanāsābhyāṃ, nāsikayā vairecanikaṃ, mukhenaivetarau|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.10"> tatra prāyogike vartiṃ vyapagataśarakāṇḍāṃ
                        nivātātapaśuṣkāmaṅgāreṣv avadīpya netramūlasrotasi prayujyadhūmam āhareti
                        brūyāt; evaṃ snehanaṃ vairecanikaṃ ca kuryād iti| itarayor vyapetadhūmāṅgāre
                        sthire samāhite śarāve prakṣipya vartiṃ mūlacchidreṇānyena śarāveṇa pidhāya
                        tasmin chidre netramūlaṃ saṃyojya dhūmam āseveta, praśānte dhūme vartim
                        avaśiṣṭāṃ prakṣipya punar api dhūmaṃ pāyayed ādoṣaviśuddheḥ; eṣa
                        dhūmapānopāyavidhiḥ|| </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.11"> tatra
                        śokaśramabhayāmarṣauṣṇyaviṣaraktapittamadamūrcchādāhapipāsāpāṇḍurogatāluśoṣacchardiśiro
                        'bhighātodgārāpatarpitatimirapramehodarādhmānordhvavātārtā
                        bālavṛddhadurbalaviriktāsthāpitajāgaritagarbhiṇīrūkṣakṣīṇakṣatoraskamadhughṛtad
                        adhidugdhamatsyamadyayavāgūpītālpakaphāś ca na dhūmamāseveran || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.12"> akālapītaḥ kurute bhramaṃ mūrcchāṃ śirorujam |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghrāṇaśrotrākṣijihvānām upaghātaṃ ca dāruṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.13"> ādyās tu trayo dhūmā dvādaśasu kāleṣūpādeyāḥ | tad yathā
                        kṣutadantaprakṣālananasyasnānabhojanadivāsvapnamaithunacchardimūtroccārahasitaruṣitaśastrakarmānteṣv
                        iti | tatra vibhāgo mūtroccārakṣavathuhasitaruṣitamaithunānteṣu snaihikaḥ,
                        snānacchardivāsvapnānteṣu vair ecanikaḥ, dantaprakṣālanasya
                        snānabhojanaśastrakarmānteṣu prāyogika iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.14"> tatra snaihiko vātaṃ śamayati, snehād upalepāc ca; vair
                        ecanaḥ śleṣmāṇamutkleśyāpakarṣati, raukṣyāttaikṣṇyādauṣṇyādvaiśadyācca;
                        prāyogikaḥ śleṣmāṇamutkleśayatyutkliṣṭaṃ cāpakarṣati śamayati vātaṃ
                        sādhāraṇatvāt pūrvābhyām iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.15"> bhavati cātra naro dhūmopayogācca prasannendriyavāṅmanāḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛḍhakeśadvijaśmaśruḥ sugandhiviśadānanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.16"> tathā
                        kāsaśvāsārocakāsyopalepasvarabhedamukhāsrāvakṣavathuvamathukrathatandrānidrāhanumanyāstambhāḥ
                        pīnasaśirorogakarṇākṣiśūlā vātakaphanimittāś cāsya mukharogā na bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.17"> tasya yogāyogātiyogā vijñātavyāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra yogo rogapraśamanaḥ, ayogo rogāpraśamanaḥ,
                        tālugalaśoṣaparidāhapipāsāmūrcchābhramamadakarṇakṣveḍadṛṣṭināsārogadaurbalyānyatiyogo
                        janayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.18"> prāyogikaṃ trīṃstrīnucchvāsānādadīta mukhanāsikābhyāṃ ca
                        paryāyāṃstrīṃś caturo veti, snaihikaṃ yāvadaśrupravṛttiḥ, vair
                        ecanikamādoṣadarśanāt, tilataṇḍulayavāgūpītena pātavyo vāmanīyaḥ,
                        grāsāntareṣu kāsaghna iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.19"> vraṇadhūmaṃ śarāvasaṃpuṭopanītena netreṇa vraṇam ānayet,
                        dhūmapānādvedanopaśamo vraṇavaiśadyam āsrāvopaśamaś ca bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.20"> vidhireṣa samāsena dhūmasyābhihito mayā |
                        <caesura/>
                         nasyasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ niravaśeṣataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.21"> auṣadhamauṣadhasiddho vā sneho nāsikābhyāṃ dīyata iti
                        nasyam | tad dvividhaṃ śirovirecanaṃ, snehanaṃ ca | tad dvividham api
                        pañcadhā | tad yathā nasyaṃ, śirovirecanaṃ, pratimarśo, avapīḍaḥ,
                        pradhamanaṃ ca | teṣu nasyaṃ pradhānaṃ śirovirecanaṃ ca; nasyavikalpaḥ
                        pratimarśaḥ, śirovirecanavikalpo 'vapīḍaḥ pradhamanaṃ ca; tato nasyaśabdaḥ
                        pañcadhā niyamitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.22"> tatra yaḥ snehanārthaṃ śūnyaśirasāṃ grīvāskandhorasāṃ ca
                        balajananārthaṃ dṛṣṭiprasādajananārthaṃ vā sneho vidhīyate tasmin vaiśeṣiko
                        nasyaśabdaḥ | tat tu deyaṃ vātābhibhūte śirasi
                        dantakeśaśmaśruprapātadāruṇakarṇaśūlakarṇakṣveḍatimirasvaropaghātanāsārogāsyaśoṣāvabāhukākālajavalīpalitaprādurbhāvadāruṇaprabodheṣu
                        vātapaittikeṣu mukharogeṣv anyeṣu ca vātapittaharadravyasiddhena sneheneti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.23"> śirovirecanaṃ śleṣmaṇā
                        'bhivyāptatālukaṇṭhaśirasāmarocakaśirogauravaśūlapīnasārdhāvabhedakakṛmipratiśyāyāpasmāragandhājñāneṣv
                        anyeṣu cordhvajatrugateṣu kaphajeṣu vikāreṣu śirovirecanadravyais
                        tatsiddhena vā sneheneti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.24"> tatraitaddvividhamapyabhuktavato 'nnakāle pūrvāhṇe
                        śleṣmarogiṇāṃ, madhyāhne pittarogiṇāṃ, aparāhṇe vātarogiṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.25"> atha puruṣāya śirovirecanīyāya tyaktamūtrapurīṣāya
                        bhuktavate vyabhre kāle dantakāṣṭhadhūmapānābhyāṃ viśuddhavaktrasrotase
                        pāṇitāpaparisvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśāya vātātaparajohīne
                        veśmanyuttānaśāyine prasāritakaracaraṇāya kiñcit pravilambitaśirase
                        vastrācchāditanetrāya vāmahastapradeśinyagronnāmitanāsāgrāya viśuddhasrotasi
                        dakṣiṇahastena sneham uṣṇāmbunā prataptaṃ
                        rajatasuvarṇatāmramaṇimṛtpātraśuktīnām anyatamasthaṃ śuktyā picunā vā
                        sukhoṣṇaṃ snehamadrutam āsiñced avyavacchinnadhāraṃ yathā netre na prāpnoti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.26"> snehe 'vasicyamāne tu śiro naiva prakampayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         na kupyen na prabhāṣec ca na kṣuyān na haset tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.27"> etair hi vihataḥ sneho na samyak pratipadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ kāsapratiśyāyaśiro 'kṣigadasaṃbhavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.28"> tasya pramāṇamaṣtau bindavaḥ pradeśinīparvadvayaniḥsṛtāḥ
                        prathamā mātrā, dvitīyā śuktiḥ, tṛtīyā pāṇiśuktiḥ, ity etāstisro mātrā
                        yathābalaṃ prayojyāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.29"> snehanasyaṃ nopagilet kathaṃ cid api buddhimān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.30"> śṛṅgāṭakam abhiplāvya nireti vadanād yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphotkleśabhayāccainaṃ niṣṭhīvedavidhārayan || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.31"> datte ca punarapi saṃsvedya galakapolādīn dhūmamāseveta,
                        bhojayeccainam abhiṣyandi, tato 'syācārikam ādiśet;
                        rajodhūmasnehātapamadyadravapānaśiraḥsnānātiyānakrodhādīni ca pariharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.32"> tasya yogātiyogāyogānāmidaṃ vijñānaṃ bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.33"> lāghavaṃ śiraso yoge sukhasvapnaprabodhanam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vikāropaśamaḥ śuddhirindiryāṇāṃ manaḥsukham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.34"> kaphaprasekaḥ śiraso gurutendriyavibhramaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         lakṣaṇaṃ mūrdhnayatisnigdhe rūkṣaṃ tatrāvacārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.35"> ayoge vātavaiguṇyamindriyāṇāṃ ca rūkṣatā | rogāśāntiś ca
                        tatreṣṭaṃ bhūyo nasyaṃ prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.36"> catvāro bindavaḥ ṣaḍ vā tathā 'ṣṭau vā yathābalam |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirekasnehasya pramāṇam abhinirdiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.37"> nasye trīṇyupadiṣṭāni lakṣaṇāni prayogataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddha(śuddhi)hīnātisaṃjñāni viśeṣācchāstracintakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.38"> lāghavaṃ śirasaḥ suddhiḥ srotasāṃ vyādhinirjayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cittendriyaprasādaś ca śirasaḥ śuddhilakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.39"> kaṇḍūpadehau gurutā srotasāṃ kaphasaṃsravaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrdhni hīnaviśuddhe tu lakṣaṇaṃ parikīrtitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.40"> mastuluṅgāgamo vātavṛddhirindriyavibhramaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śūnyatā śirasaś cāpi mūrdhni gāḍhavirecite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.41"> hīnātiśuddhe śirasi kaphavātaghnam ācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyagviśuddhe śirasi sarpirnasyaṃ niṣecayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.42"> (ekāntaraṃ dvyanataraṃ vā saptāhaṃ vā punaḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekaviṃśatirātraṃ vā yāvadvā sādhu manyate ||) </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.43"> mārutenābhibhūtasya vā 'tyantaṃ yasya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dvikālaṃ cāpi dātavyaṃ nasyaṃ tasya vijānatā ||) </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44"> avapīḍastu
                        śirovirecanavadabhiṣyaṇṇasarpadaṣṭavisaṃjñebhyo dadyāc
                        chirocirecanadravyāṇām anyatamam avapiṣyāvapīḍya ca,</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44a"> śarkarekṣurasakṣīraghṛtamāṃsarasānām anyatamaṃ kṣīṇānāṃ
                        śoṇitapitte ca vidadhyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.45"> kṛśadurbalabhīrūṇāṃ sukumārasya yoṣitām |
                        <caesura/>
                         śṛtāḥ snehāḥ śiraḥśuddhyai kalkastebhyo yathā hitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.46"> cetovikārakṛmiviṣābhipannānāṃ cūrṇaṃ pradhamet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.47"> nasyena parihartavyo bhutavānapatarpito
                        'tyarthataruṇapratiśyāyī garbhiṇī pītasnehodakamadyadravo 'jīrṇī dattabastiḥ
                        kruddho garārtastṛṣitaḥ śokābhibhūtaḥ ānto bālo vṛddho vegāvarodhitaḥ
                        śiraḥsnātukāmaś ceti; anārtave cābhre nasyadhūmau pariharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.48"> tatra
                        hīnātimātrātiśītoṣṇasahasāpradānādatipravilambitaśirasa ucchiṅghato vicalato
                        'bhyavaharato vā pratiṣiddhapradānāc ca vyāpado bhavanti tṛṣṇodgārādayo
                        doṣanimittāḥ kṣayajāś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.49"> bhavataś cātra nasye śirovireke ca vyāpado dvividhāḥ
                        smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣotkleśāt kṣayāccaiva vijñeyāstā yathākramam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.50"> doṣokleśanimittās tu jayecchamanaśodhanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atha kṣayanimittāsu yathāsvaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ hitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.51"> pratimarśaś caturdaśasu kāleṣūpādeyaḥ; tad yathā
                        talpotthitena, prakṣālitadantena, gṛhānnirgacchatā,
                        vyāyāmavyavāyādhvapariśrāntena, mūtroccārakavalāñjanānte, bhuktavatā,
                        charditavatā, divāsvapnotthitena, sāyaṃ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.52"> tatra talpotthitenāsevitaḥ pratimarśo rātrāvupacitaṃ
                        nāsāsrotogataṃ malam upahanti manaḥprasādaṃ ca karoti,
                        prakṣālitadantenāsevito dantānāṃ dṛḍhatāṃ vadanasaugandhyaṃ cāpādayati,
                        gṛhānnirgacchatā sevito nāsāseotasaḥ klinnatayā rajodhūmo vā na bādhate,
                        vyāyāmamaithunādhvapariśrāntenāsevitaḥ śramam upahanti, mūtroccārānte sevito
                        dṛṣṭergurutvam apanayati, kavalāñjanānte sevito dṛṣṭiṃ prasādayati,
                        bhuktavatā sevitaḥ srotasāṃ viśuddhiṃ laghutāṃ cāpādayati, vāntenāsevitaḥ
                        srotovilagnaṃ śleṣmāṇamapohya bhaktākāṅkṣām āpādayati,
                        divāsvapnotthitenāsevito nidrāśeṣaṃ gurutvaṃ malaṃ cāpohya cittaikāgryaṃ
                        janayati, sāyaṃ cāsevitaḥ sukhanidrāprabodhaṃ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.53"> īṣaducchiṅghataḥ sneho yāvadvaktraṃ prapadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         nasye niṣiktaṃ taṃ vidyāt pratimarśaṃ pramāṇataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.54"> nasyena rogāḥ śāmyanti narāṇāmūrdhvajatrujāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         indriyāṇāṃ ca vaimalyaṃ kuryād āsyaṃ sugandhi ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.55"> hanudantaśirogrīvātrikabāhūrasāṃ balam |
                        <caesura/>
                         valīpalitakhālity avyaṅgānāṃ cāpy asaṃbhavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.56"> tailaṃ kaphe savāte syāt kevale pavane vasām |
                        <caesura/>
                         dadyāt sarpiḥ sadā pitte majjānaṃ ca samārute || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.57"> caturvidhasya snehasya vidhirevaṃ prakīrtitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmasthānāvirodhitvāt teṣu tailaṃ vidhīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.58"> ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kavalagrahaṇe vidhim |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturdhā kavalaḥ snehī prasādī śodhiropaṇau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.59"> sngidhoṣṇaiḥ snaihiko vāte svāduśītaiḥ prasādanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte kaṭvamlalavaṇai rūkṣoṣṇaiḥ śodhanaḥ kaphe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.60"> kaṣāyatiktamadhuraiḥ kaṭūṣṇai ropaṇo vraṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturvidhasya caivāsya viśeṣo 'yaṃ prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.61"> tatra trikaṭukavacāsarṣapaharītakīkalkamāloḍya
                        tailaśuktasurāmūtrakṣāramadhūnāmanyatamena salavaṇam abhiprataptam
                        upasvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśo dhārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.62"> sukhaṃ saṃcāryate yā tu mātrā sa (sā) kavalaḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         asaṃcāryā tu yā mātrā gaṇḍūṣaḥ sa prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.63"> tāvac ca dhārayitavyo 'nanyamanasonnatadehena
                        yāvaddoṣaparipūrṇakapolatvaṃ nāsāsrotonayanapariplāvaś ca bhavati tadā
                        vimoktavyaḥ, punaś cānyo grahītavya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.64"> evaṃ snehapayaḥkṣaudrarasamūtrāmlasaṃbhṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kasāyoṣṇodakābhyāṃ ca kavalā doṣato hitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.65"> vyādher apacayastuṣṭirvaiśadyaṃ vaktralāghavam |
                        <caesura/>
                         indiryāṇāṃ prasādaś ca kavale śuddhilakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.66"> hīne jāḍyakaphotkleśāvarasajñānam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         atiyogān mukhe pākaḥ śoṣatṛṣṇāruciklamāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.67"> śodhanīye viśeṣeṇa bhavanty eva na saṃśayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tilā nīlotpalaṃ sarpiḥ śarkarā kṣīram eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.68"> sakṣaudro dagdhavaktrasya gaṇḍūṣo dāhanāśanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kavalasya vidhirhyeṣa samāsena prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.69"> vibhajya bheṣajaṃ buddhyā kurvīta pratisāraṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalko rasakriyā kṣaudraṃ cūrṇaṃ ceti caturvidham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.70"> aṅgulyagrapraṇītaṃ tu yathāsvaṃ mukharogiṇām |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmin yogamayogaṃ ca kavaloktaṃ vibhāvayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.71"> tān eva śamayed vyādhīn kavalo yān apohati |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣaghnam anabhiṣyandi bhojayec ca tathā naram ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.trailer1"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne
                        dhūmanasyakavalagrahacikitsitaṃ nāma catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.trailer2"> iti bhagavatā śrīdhanvantariṇopadiṣṭāyāṃ tacchiṣyeṇa maharṣiṇā
                        suśrutena viracitāyāṃ suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthānaṃ samāptam || </l>
                </div>

            </div>
